Seven generations of ancestors will be delivered from the Three Wretched Paths and the Five Sufferings, ascending to the Heavenly Halls. The blessings of life and death will reciprocate like echoes. The Three Officials and Nine Palaces record the merits and transgressions of people—this principle is most clear.

The second scroll of *The Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns* concludes.
The third scroll of *The Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns* begins.

Master Wang Xuanhe of the Vast Ocean of Lu, Feathered Guest of the Great Tang, on the Methods of Ingesting and Consuming:

*The Biographies of the Immortals, Lower Scroll* states: "Cease eating and rest the roots to expel grain-qi. Through breathwork and guiding the qi, exhale the old and inhale the new."

*The Upper Scroll of Jade Characters of Inner Sounds* states: "If you wish to become an immortal and not die, you must expel the Three Worms and the corpse-worm lurking beneath the heart. Regularly at midnight and cock’s crow, recite this invocation:

*To the Azure Fang of the East, consume the Azure Fang, drink the morning blossom—three swallows, then stop.
To the Vermilion Cinnabar of the South, consume the Vermilion Cinnabar, drink from the Cinnabar Pool—three swallows, then stop.
To the Central Wilds, where Wu and Ji rise high, consume the essence-qi, drink from the Sweet Spring—three swallows, then stop.
To the Luminous Stone of the West, consume the Luminous Stone, drink the numinous liquid—three swallows, then stop.
To the Mystic Nourishment of the North, consume the Mystic Nourishment, drink the Jade Syrup—three swallows, then stop.*

After thirty days of this, the Three Worms will all die, and the corpse-worm will flee. The true spirit and true qi will naturally settle; the corpse-worm will no longer return to the heart, and you shall become an immortal. This is the method of the Five Directions and Five Fangs—it is also the Five Kitchens. Thus, the *Scripture of the Five Kitchens* by Laozi states: 'Cultivate and uphold the Great Harmony, neither deficient nor excessive. Taste it and find no flavor; smell it and find no fragrance. If you come to know this, your destiny aligns with the true stars. Once received, it is never lost, and eternal joy arises naturally.' The *Forty-Four Methods Scripture of the Yellow Plain* also contains this text on ingesting and invoking."

*The Upper Scripture of Astronomy* states: "The reason the people of remote antiquity lived long was that they did not consume grains even in haste."

*The Scripture of Great Possession* says: "The Five Grains are the chisels that hollow out life, rotting the five viscera and shortening the lifespan. Once these roots enter the mouth, do not hope for longevity. If you desire not to die, keep your intestines free of filth."

*The Seventh Scroll of the Transmission of Daoist Learning* states: "Lu Xiujing, styled Yuande, was a native of Dongqian in Wuxing. Though outwardly he mingled with worldly affairs, inwardly he preserved purity and simplicity. From youth, he practiced grain avoidance and slept alone."

The sixteenth scroll states: "Tao Yan, styled Aijing, was a native of Xunyang in Lujiang. At fifteen or sixteen, he consumed and ceased grains, initially still eating wheat flour, later only jujubes."

*The Lower Scroll of the Essential Rites of the Numinous Treasure Fast* states: "If Daoists eat the Five Grains but take no other sustenance, they will hunger. If consuming medicinal substances, take them precisely at noon; after noon, drink only clear water and cease eating. At dawn, drink congee; at midday, eat vegetables."

*The Lower Scroll of the Great Perfection Regulations* states: "Those who study the records of external and internal cultivation to learn immortality should all consume and swallow qi to repel evil and cure illness. For those who cannot yet cease grains, meals should be regular: congee at dawn, vegetable stew and rice at midday, with dried vegetables and fermented beans—enough only to stave off hunger, not to indulge in rich flavors or fine tastes. Take care never to kill living beings or waste fat and fresh foods. As for sauces and vinegar, these too must not be overused, for excess harms one’s nature. Moreover, do not overeat; it is best to stop one or two mouthfuls short. After eating, walk leisurely to aid digestion. Before and after meals, meditate on the boundless grace of the ancient sages, whose beneficence endures without end. Universally wish that all beings attain fullness and satisfaction, that they may receive the sweet dew and mushroom nectar, never hunger again, and no longer crave the dusty flavors of the world. If accepting food from others, feel humility and gratitude toward the host. With heart and mouth, wish the donor wealth, joy, fullness, and long life, that they too may partake of the flavor of the Dao, forever free from calamity and decline, without hunger or thirst. Always have Dharma-food and worldly food to offer all beings without end, aiding and liberating them with generosity, free from regret or stinginess, never harboring resentment, forever sharing joy. After the first meal, scatter rice in the mountains and waters, beneath cliffs and forests, or beside fences and walls—never toss it onto rooftops, lest insects and birds peck through and cause leaks and decay."

*The Scripture of the Forty-Four Methods of the Yellow Plain* states: "Whenever Daoists are about to eat, they should hold their chopsticks in the left hand, tap the plate three times, and softly invoke: *'The Two Mysteries ascend the Dao, the Four Poles are clear and cool. The Supreme One, the Lord Emperor, and the hundred spirits are at peace. Receive the roots of the Three Palaces, irrigate and nourish the numinous spleen. Partake of the Great Harmony, feast on the five fragrances. The life of the soul-embryo, the seven fluids flow and settle; the hundred passages harmonize, the five viscera bloom with radiance. The Twin Sovereigns merge with the light, soaring to ascend the Upper Clarity.'* After eating, tap the plate three more times—this is called the Way of the Soul-Embryo receiving fragrance and the hundred spirits feasting on the roots. Practicing this regularly makes one’s spirit bright and qi harmonious, the hun and po at peace, repelling evil and dispelling trials, forever preserving good fortune and purity."

*The Ninth Scroll of the Biographies of Divine Immortals* states: "Jie Xiang, styled Yuanze, was a native of Kuaiji. Entering the mountains, he encountered an immortal woman who resembled an image. He kowtowed and begged for longevity. The woman said: *'Your qi from blood and food is not yet exhausted. Cease grains for three years, then return—I will await you here.'* Xiang returned home, ceased grains for three years, and went back. The woman was still in the same place and gave him a scroll of the *Scripture of the Returning Elixir*, saying: *'Attain this, and you shall become an immortal. Do nothing else.'*"

*The Scripture of the Nine Radiances* states: "Jujubes are the fruit of the rosy clouds; rosy clouds are the essence of the sun. Consuming them, the body generates jadelike radiance—this is the method of reflecting the Upper Clarity."

*The Rituals of the Three Sovereigns’ Fasts* states: "Those who cultivate the Dao eat once at midday and once at the hour of living qi at midnight. These two meals, day and night, are taken at the hour of living qi to avoid the hour of dead qi. At other times, not even the slightest morsel may be tasted, for it would violate the dead qi. If ill or gathering herbs, or consuming medicines to cease grains, follow what is appropriate without rigid constraints. Food is for nourishing the body; when the body is at ease, the spirit is joyful. Those who are not hungry find cultivation easy to accomplish; those weakened by hunger and emaciation will not achieve their work."

It further states: "At the hour of the single meal in Daoist practice, one must burn incense in contemplation, making offerings to the former sages. With eyes closed, one visualizes the descent of the prior spirits, who partake of the offering for a long while. One’s wishes and thoughts extend to all beings, that all may be equally sated and fulfilled."

*The Scripture of the Five Wondrous Talismans of the Cavernous Mystery* states: "Consuming the essence of the moon grants longevity; consuming the essence of the stars ascends one to the Grand Clarity."

*The Hidden Instructions for Ascending to Perfection, Second Scroll* states: "Ingesting *yunya* allows one to cease grains and expel the corpse-worms."

*The Hidden Instructions for Ascending to Perfection, Fourth Scroll* states: "Ingesting *yunya* enables the cultivation of the Dao of True Unity, the preservation of primordial qi, and the swallowing of saliva. If hunger arises, one should consume wheat-based foods, gradually reducing grain intake until grains are abandoned entirely. One must not abandon them all at once—this is what is meant by 'diminishing and diminishing again, until reaching non-action.'"

*The Scripture of the Golden Tablet and Jade Characters* states: "Those who consume medicinal substances to cease grains must abstain from wine, meat, and the five pungent vegetables. They should bathe, wear clean clothes, and burn incense." This is also seen in *The Scripture of Great Possession and Wondrous Mystery*.

*The Cavernous Mystery Scripture of the Supreme Unity* states: "If you cannot consume medicinal substances to cease grains and purify the intestines to refine the true, you should at least moderate all foul and bloody meats, as well as mixed foods of pungent and rank vegetables, strictly prohibiting them. This can extend the span of life."

It further states: The Perfected Consort Wang of the Purple Tenuity, a true immortal, advocated the consumption of *muxu*: "For the true person nurturing life, the Most High treasures it. The Seven Classics and Five Effulgences, the Two Pure Internal Dao—all emerge from it. Consuming and employing various medicines, gathering and refining the hundred herbs, warding off pestilence and securing life, *mu* is the finest. It flushes away the hundred evils, dispels illness, and resists aging. The body generates radiant luster, filling the flesh and replenishing the brain. Without diligent devotion, one cannot obtain it—without natural endowment, without methods and recipes, one will surely wither."

It further states: "Nurturing nature and halting aging, preserving the blackness of hair—this is what the *mu* family governs." It also states: "Now, *mu* blocks the paths of evil and obstructs the roads of ghosts. Consuming its nine preparations refines the spirit and quickens the four limbs, making the constructive and defensive qi light and agile. Ingesting its decoctions and powders dispels the hundred illnesses—this enables longevity and enduring vision." The methods for compounding *mu* are numerous, so they are not transcribed here.

It further states: "Rub the face and eyes with both hands until slightly warm, making this a regular practice, to be done frequently. When a person ages, wrinkles first appear below the eyes. When a person’s qi and power wane, it first begins between the nostrils. These two places are the gates of wrinkles and decline, the passes of the body’s qi and strength. Thus, in daily life, one should regularly practice this method to ward off wrinkles and decline, preserving qi and strength in constant harmony."

*The Scripture of Great Peace, Scroll One Hundred Fourteen* states: The Azure Lad gathers *feigen*, swallows solar effulgences, ingests the Luminous Spirit Talisman, the Lunar Splendor Talisman, and the Talisman for Expelling the Two [Demons]. He binds the three *hun*, restrains the seven *po*, wears the Star and Constellation Talisman, consumes *huadan*, drinks Yellow Water and Returning Water, eats *huangang*, consumes phoenix brain, eats pine pears and plum jujubes, ingests silver, purple gold, and cloud fat, eats bamboo shoots, wears the Five Spirit Talismans—with these, his transformations are endless. He transcends beyond the Three Realms, roaming within the Six Directions."

*The Hidden Instructions for Ascending to Perfection, Seventh Scroll* states: "Those who consume the Five Minerals can eat nine times a day, with the hundred passages flowing purely. They can also go a full year without hunger, reverting from old age to infancy. When food is encountered, they eat; when not, they remain at ease. This is the wondrous method of the highest immortals, the marvelous efficacy of ceasing grains." Tao Hongjing’s commentary states: "Though they eat nine times a day, they absorb and exhale without sound, their flow and transformation unchanging, producing no saliva. Though they go a year without eating, their complexion becomes fresher."

The Azure Lad says: "Dry mineral [powder] with rice, mixed with eastern green and vermilion essence—one dose immediately extends a person’s lifespan by a thousand years, with each day’s consumption further prolonging it."

The Perfected of Pure Numinosity also says: On Mount Huo, there were Daoist practitioners Deng Boyuan and Wang Xuanfu, who received the method of consuming *qingjing* [azure essence] rice and swallowing solar effulgences. They practiced this from the time of the Celestial Master Fang until thirty-four years had passed, whereupon they could internally perceive the five viscera and write in darkness at midnight.

It further states: "Thrice-steamed azure rice is not an ordinary food." It also states: "Eating wheat-based foods makes reducing grains easier, or supplementing and filling the body is simple. The intestines and stomach become full, no longer empty and weak. Consuming [azure] rice, the hundred harms cannot injure you, illnesses cannot afflict you. It dispels all distracting thoughts, severs the Three Corpses, sharpens hearing and vision, and lightens the steps."

The commentary states: "Cinnabar and azure harmonize the spirit and nurture qi, enabling one to resist and repel disasters and pestilence. Thus, harms and illnesses no longer assail you. With the essence and *hun* in joyful harmony, there are no worries or sorrowful thoughts. Once grains are abandoned, the corpse-worms naturally dissolve. The liver and kidneys become clear and moist, the ears and eyes bright and penetrating, the sinews strong and bones firm—movement is like flying."

It further states: "In famine years without grain, or when impoverished and unable to obtain it, one may consume *nanzhu* alone, or mix it with *fuling*, or blend *nanzhu* with honey, or combine it with pine and cypress leaves."

It further states: "Ceasing grains does not necessarily grant longevity. The necessity of ceasing grains lies in following the cultivation of numinous wonders, freeing oneself from the burdens of cooked foods and rooted grains, and consuming medicinal minerals to seek swift efficacy."

It further states: "Through grains, one ceases grains, transforming the six bowels gradually." It also states: "For ease of absorption and attraction, nothing surpasses the Seven Luminaries. For swift success in cultivation, nothing exceeds the Nine Ways. For steadfast preservation, nothing surpasses *zhensheng*. For urgent defense and protection, nothing surpasses *hunshen*. For rapid efficacy of medicinal minerals, nothing excels *qingjing*. For utmost responsiveness in prayer and worship, nothing is superior to morning and evening offerings."

Those who consume the Five Minerals stabilize the five viscera. If they briefly die, their white bones become like jade. The seven *po* attend them, the two *hun* guard their dwelling, the Three Primes rejoice in rest, the great spirits close within, and externally, they infuse the skin and flesh. Though the body may decay, if the viscera and bowels remain unharmed, their appearance and form remain as in life. The bone marrow does not wither, the sinews and brain interflow, the *hun* and *po* stand guard, the Three Palaces are tranquil and still. Since the great spirits no longer roam the Nine Transformations but remain closed within the Cavern Chamber, they will only resume their circulation on the destined day of rebirth.

Should one emerge after forty years, twenty years, ten years, or three years—each according to their will—at the moment of rebirth, blood is gathered anew, flesh nurtured, fluids generated, and essence reconstituted into form, surpassing even their appearance before death. This is what is meant by "the Perfected refining the body in the Great Yin, transforming countenance in the Three Bureaus."

The Heavenly Thearch Lord states: "Refining the body in the Great Yin excels all; consuming the Nine-Turned Elixir, one’s form becomes upright and solemn, the complexion like numinous clouds. Ascending the Terrace of the Great Ultimate, one’s name is inscribed among the Perfected."

It further cites the Nine Radiance Serene Consort: "Worries and burdens do not disturb the Mystic Abode; sorrowful thoughts do not agitate the Crimson Ford. In tranquil detachment and distant contemplation, one delights in the shared reflection of light. Observing the four seasons in their revolutions, daily attaining perfection, one gazes into the farthest reaches, all having merged with the divine."

The days for audience at the Jade Court are: the fourth day of the first month, the fifteenth day of the third month, the eighth day of the fourth month, the fourth day of the sixth month, the seventh day of the seventh month, the eighth day of the eighth month, the ninth day of the ninth month, the fifth day of the tenth month, the third day of the eleventh month, and the twelfth day of the twelfth month.

The days for audience at the Great Simplicity are: the ninth day of the first month, the eighth day of the second month, the seventh day of the third month, the sixth day of the fourth month, the fifth day of the fifth month, the fourth day of the sixth month, the second day of the seventh month, the second day of the eighth month, the first day of the ninth month, the tenth day of the tenth month, the eleventh day of the eleventh month, and the twelfth day of the twelfth month.

The days for audience at the Great Ultimate are: the first day of the first month, the twentieth day of the second month, the twenty-seventh day of the third month, the sixth day of the sixth month, the twentieth day of the eighth month, the third day of the eleventh month, and the sixth day of the twelfth month.

On the seventh, eleventh, and fifteenth days of the month, one visualizes the Mystic Elixir.
On the first, eleventh, sixteenth, twenty-first, and twenty-sixth days of the month, one visualizes the Precious Mirror—envisioning one’s two eyes transformed into two luminous mirrors, illuminating the entire body.

On the first, fifteenth, and twenty-seventh days of the month, one consumes the Mingtang Talisman and the Imperial Likeness Talisman.
On *dingmao* days, one pays audience to the Azure Lad.
On *jian* and *chu* days, one visualizes the Three Ones.
At the *yin* hour, one visualizes the Three Sections of the Upper Radiance Talisman and consumes the Mystic Perfection.
On *mao* days, one consumes mist, the solar emblem, the solar rays, the Seven Stars Talisman, the Dissolution Talisman, pays audience to the Supreme Subtlety, audience to the Jade Dawn, and consumes the Three Qi and the Soaring Dragon.

At the *xu* hour, one consumes lunar essence, Mystic Perfection, and lunar rays.
At the *hai* hour, one absorbs water, recites the incantation of the Three Clouds, the Five Bamboo Shoots, the Six Palaces, visualizes the Great Lord, lies reciting the Sword and Ring, and further visualizes the Dipper, the Lower Radiance, and the Five of the Head.
At the *chen* and *chou* hours, one visualizes the Double Radiance—all these are methods for cultivating the Dao.

It further states: "Ascending the Mystic, pacing the flying steps, and returning in gratitude; restraining the *hun* and controlling the *po*—these too are its methods."

The *Upper Clarity Scripture on Dispelling Demons* says: "Jade teeth and dense blossoms, the Seven Yangs’ Infant, the fluid of the Nine Jades, the essence of the Eight Precious Stones, the purple nectar of the Four Pistils, the Five Pearls descending to give birth to the Three Florets flying as steel, the twin pearls of lunar brightness, orchid liquid and golden stalks, sweet dew in jade vases, divine lotus elixir and cinnabar powder, cloud branches linked in camps, jade groves forming at dawn, the Western Thearch’s plain abundance—rinsing and transforming these, one enters the Purple Court."

It further says: "The waters of the Eastern Culmen’s Weaving Maiden, the westernmost reaches of Long Geng and Yu Yuan, the southern extremity of the Yang Light’s root, the northern depths of the Great Yin’s Liquid Citadel."

It further says: "From the north, gather the black crabapple of the Mystic Expanse; gazing upward, rinse the vermilion honey of cloud mountains. From the east, pluck the cinnabar mulberries of Fusang; bending down, probe the patterned algae of the Long Abyss. Above, harmonize the flying jade of the Nine Turns; below, swallow the rosy treasures of the Azure Mystery. The Great Void forms its rings; the Plain Infant cradles them. The Purple Dragon Lad, the Nine-Enveloped Phoenix Brain, the Hidden Mushroom of the Great Ultimate, the Crimson Tree of the Solar Path, the Rainbow Plum of the Supreme, the Great Grass of the Celestial Han, the Giant Pearl of the Southern Palace, the Aged Supporter of the Western Ministers, the Three-Beamed Dragon Flower—these are what the Numinous Consort seeks. Those who obtain and consume them divide their spirit into myriad paths."

It further says: "The secluded mushrooms of the Upper Clarity, the Great Harmony; the speckled dragon’s black embryo, the striped tiger’s white foam—these emerge from the Western Mound. The Seven Mysteries’ flying nodes, the Nine Apertures’ jade pearls, cloud nectar and numinous fluid, the jade richness of the Mystic Orchard, the white glue of Bell Mountain, gold born of blue unfolding, the stone brain of Langfeng, the black river’s coral, the white discharge of Meng Mountain, the jade lungs of the Numinous Mound, the azure simurgh’s golden essence, the Eastern Flower’s vermilion melon, the nine-jointed interlacing, the purple hemp of the Supreme Subtlety. Jade blossoms and jade fruits, the whale waves of Flowing Abyss, the red river’s crimson jade. From the north, draw from the well of the Great Ultimate; in the center, string the vermilion veins of the Patterned Cinnabar. The divine peach of the Cloud Court, the jade fluid of Kun Garden. The night essence and solar grass, the azure ford and blue reeds. Above, summon the divine radiance; below, drink from the dark rapids. Gaze upward to grasp the jade essence of the Mystic Orchard; bend down to pluck the purple crabapple of the Garden Mound. The divine clam of White Water, the red leeks of the Eight Heavens—once in ten thousand generations, their radiance flows through the nine descendants. Those who obtain and consume them are treasured by the Supreme."

It further says: "Refining the nine stones into smoke, the cinnabar fluid and jade sap, the flowing pearls of Xunshou, the essence of speckled blossoms, the golden fluid of the cinnabar furnace, the purple blossoms and rainbow petals, the Nine Turns of the Great Clarity, the nectar of the Five Clouds, the dark frost and crimson snow, leaping through the Three Yellows, the white fragrance of the Eastern Sea, the azure coins of Canglang, the surplus grain of the high mounds, the flying fields of piled stones, the returning elixir of the Great Void, the dark firmness of the Great Simplicity, the flowing grass of eternal light, the flying thousand of the cloud lads—these too enable one to ascend and soar lightly."

It further says: "The thirty-six mushrooms, the flying furnace refining smoke, the solar waters and lunar blossoms, the richness of the Five Lords—these stabilize the five viscera and refine the countenance, transforming the body. Even the cloud-scattered marvelous blossoms, the golden powder and jade softness, can extend one’s years to ten thousand."

It further says: "The dark water and cloud blossom nectar, the five yellows within the dense numen, the essence-dried stone □ meal, the many greens and vermilion flowers, the fruits of the white chariot’s flying nodes, the purple wood’s yellow of the flowing crow—consuming these at once grants one a lifespan of a thousand epochs."

It further says: "The fat of pine and cypress in the shade, mountain ginger that subdues essence, calamus, ophiopogon, sesame, polygonatum, chrysanthemum, lycium, cliff honey, poria, peach bark, alisma, Solomon’s seal, coptis, cimicifuga, rehmannia, gastrodia, vermilion blossoms, and the numinous flying ice cassia—consuming these brings minor benefit, yet grants no hope of ascending to the azure heavens."

The *Supreme Unity Cavern-True Mystery Canon* states: "The Supreme Unity draws in the purple mist." The Supreme Unity is the spirit within the human body.

The *Eight Simplicities Canon* states: "The blossom of the moon is the qi of the solar radiance, reflected in the Eastern Well."

The *Twenty-Four Images of Life* states: "At dawn, array the essence of the Five Stars; at midday, gather the essence of the sun’s nectar; at dusk, consume the yellow blossom of the moon."

The *Eight Yang Songs of the Nine Chapters* states: "Looking up, one inhales the pearl-like blossoms; looking down, one awakens to clarity."

The *Seventh Hidden Instructions on Ascending to Perfection* states: "As the years and months grow distant, let diligence never wane. Strengthen the body and refine the qi; cultivate the elixir with propriety. Then the five richnesses transform the countenance—this is the liquid of the dark water. The seven yangs alter the substance—this is the essence of the crooked. The crane refines the void—this is the nine-times-cycled cinnabar. The dragon soars with the sun—this is the blossom of langgan jade. The tin scroll ascends the jade steps—this is the journey to the Supreme Subtlety. Receiving the affair in the jasper chamber—this is the journey to the Jade Dawn. My Dao is complete."

The text further states: "Inhale the blossoms of flying langgan jade, rinse the dragon embryo, drink the essence of jade, ingest the golden elixir, draw from the nine transformations, consume the numinous treasure, practice the Nine Perfected, refine the frost of white lang, and the ten-times-cycled purple blossom. Conceal and shift the white haze, disperse the spirit and stone essence, form the golden radiance numinous pellet—these are the dregs of the *Golden Sword Scripture’s* Crooked Dawn Elixir, the Nine Palaces Right Perfected Lord Guo’s Lesser Golden Licorice Pellet Formula, Master Chang Sang’s Wood-Inhaling Method, Bian Que’s Death-Reversing Formula, the Sesame Powder, the Poria Pill, the Nine Jade Nectars, the Eight Jade Flying Essences, the Supreme Lord’s Refined Immortal Pellet—these are the Eight Jade Elixirs.

The Grand Ultimate Perfected’s Azure [Grain] Meal, the Upper Immortal’s Numinous Formula, the Grand Ultimate Perfected’s Cloud Bud Jade-Inhaling Method, Master High Mound’s Four-Fan Divine Immortal Powder Formula, the Tortoise Terrace Queen Mother’s Four Youths’ Numinous Formula, the Supreme Lord’s Eight Jade Flying Essence Elixir’s Embryo-Ingesting Method, the Returning Spirit and Guarding the Corporeal Soul’s Yellow-Red Inner Perfected Preserving Numinous Pine-Soot Flowing Azure-Purple Pellet, the Primordial Spirit’s Root-Cutting Worm Pellet, the Cinnabar’s Dark Essence, the Golden Azure Purple Syrup, the Eight Jade Crimson Liquid, the Dragon Embryo and Phoenix Brain, the Cloud Lang Jade Blossom, the Nine Cauldrons’ Cloud Powder, the Rainbow Elixir and Stone Brain, the Nine Blossom Elixir, the Northern Nurtured Fire Elixir, the Flowing Pearl Elixir, the Furnace Fire Elixir, the Min Mountain Elixir, the Rainbow Elixir’s Liquid, the Cloud Blossom Elixir, the Singing Elixir, the Golden Liquid, the Eight Directions’ Dao-Guiding Elixir, the Stone’s Yellow, the Cloud Syrup, the Grand Ultimate Perfected’s Bequeathed White Powder and Azure Essence Stone Meal, the Flowing Brightness Powder, the Refined Immortal Pellet, the Worm-Cutting Pellet, the Alisma and Cypress Fruit Pellet, the Alisma and Wood Powder.

The *Seventh Hidden Instructions on Ascending to Perfection* states: 'The five stone cloud richnesses.' The Azure Youth Lord says: 'The five lords’ richnesses settle and generate the five viscera, refining the countenance and transforming the body.' The following is excerpted from the *Five Stone Cloud Richnesses Formula, Fourth Scroll*, cited and annotated in the *Hidden Instructions on Ascending to Perfection*.

The third scroll contains the Langgan Elixir, the Crooked Dawn Elixir, the Nine-Turn Elixir, the Five Lords’ Stone Richness, the Azure Essence Stone Meal, the Four Guardians Pellet, the Four Youths’ Powder, the Four-Fan Powder, the Licorice Pellet, the Primordial Spirit Pellet, the Poria Pellet, the Sesame Pellet, the Flowing Azure Pellet, the Flowing Refined Richness, and the Wood-Ingesting Method.

It further states: 'Cinnabar-yellow seals the ears to dissolve the corpse—this is the essential Dao of refining the corporeal soul.' The Corporeal Soul-Cutting Method: '[Missing character] extinguishes the Three Worms. Cloud buds sever grain to expel the corpse. The Primordial Spirit Pellet kills grain worms and withers the Three Worms. The Five Phases Purple Text eliminates the Three Worms. Ingesting white awn disperses the Three Worms. Frequent bathing washes and refines the corpse and corporeal soul.'

It further states: 'Ingesting and severing grain, resting from grain in the mountains. Severing grains to purify the intestines, purifying the fast and resting from grain. Ingesting [missing character] meal for five years severs grain. Swallowing cloud buds to sever grain. To sever grain, first ingest the Primordial Spirit Pellet and the Supreme Unity’s Four Guardians Pellet—these also sever grain. If one does not sever grain, the *Great Cavern* cannot yet be attained. Severing grain has its own methods in the world. These nine methods consider severing grain as excellent.'

It further states: 'The Licorice Pellet, ingested in small amounts while desiring food, harmonizes with grain to achieve immortality. Next, ingest [missing character] meal while supplementing grain without neglect, benefiting the body and dispelling illness, filling and fattening the flesh, then ascend mountains to chant cavern scriptures and discourse on subtleties.' These two methods consider not severing grain as excellent. Combined with the seven white numinous vegetables, harmonized with scallions to dissolve [impurities], hence it is called 'combining.' The cloud grass’s dark purity: the black sesame’s richness, the wood’s essence cloud grass—grass moistened like clouds, also likened to clouds containing water, with grass holding its essence. 'Dark' refers to color; 'purity' refers to nourishment. The blossoms of lush herbs’ sweet wine: white honey. The sweet wine is the blossoms of lush herbs, brewed into wine. Honey is the earth’s essence. The five lights and seven scallions’ numinous vegetables: scallion greens. 'Scallion' is pronounced *hu mai* (胡迈反). The 'five' refers to the fifth month, when they are unearthed to avoid the harm of intense fire. The 'seven' is the metal number. White scallions are pungent, the flavor of metal, the essence of scallion metal. 'Numinous vegetables' refers to divine greens. The white plain flying dragon: white quartz. 'White plain' describes its form and color; 'flying dragon' refers to its hidden transformations. The dark water jade liquid: the dark purity’s rich water. 'Jade liquid' is the quartz’s liquid, also called flying dragon cloud richness. 'Flying dragon' is the name of quartz; 'cloud richness' is the name of cloud richness grass. Also called the refined five stones’ blossom ointment. 'Blossom' refers to essence; 'ointment' refers to dark richness. Fanning the southern candle’s eastern glow, summoning the vermilion spirit of the first bud. 'Southern candle' is the essence of yang things; 'eastern glow' is the light of hidden numinosity. 'First bud' is the tender leaf of the thorn tree."

The vermilion spirit is the pure and radiant essence of cinnabar liquid. When the five fluids harmonize and dissipate, the hundred passages become full and flowing, the fluids of the five viscera achieve balance and regulation, and all joints receive their proper overflow—thus, there is no longer the affliction of withering and desiccation.

It is also said: Reinforce this with morning rinses of the Flowering Spring’s five-directional numinous essences, sounding the drum of the Jade Pool, inhaling and exhaling the dark purity, and concurrently employing the method of cloud sprouts—rinsing and washing with clear springs to assist in replenishing their moisture. Then both qi and substance will be sound and flourishing.

The Flowery Richness, when steamed in the □ direction until the stomach is full and settled with malachite, transforms honey to reverse aging and restore youth, making the eyes bright and clear. Malachite stabilizes the generative essence and replenishes fluids, thus filling the intestines with □ radiance.

It is further said: Therefore, with a single initiation of a thousand calculations, longevity follows the flourishing of years. As the years advance with the medicine, one ascends the immortal courts in flying steps. After consuming one dose, life no longer declines. The Five Clouds generate the body, embodying the spirit, qi, and essence. The Azure Lad says: A thousand years of long calculation refers to a single dose. Thus, it is said that a thousand calculations begin with one initiation; consuming ten doses grants ten thousand years of life. When the elders of the five directions descend to bestow the Azure Essence upon a person, and the spirit attaches to the body, that person becomes a perfected one.

The Supreme Ultimate Perfected One’s Azure Essence Dried Stone □ Meal is a divine recipe of the highest immortals. The commentary states: This herb possesses the spirit of Azure Essence and is also mixed with vermilion and azure to make dried meals, hence it is called Azure Dried Stone □ Meal. □ is pronounced *xùn*. This is a divine recipe of the highest immortal palaces, not a lesser method.

The azure rice of Mount Yu-zhang’s Western Mountain and the Azure Dragon rice of Wu and Yue are examples. Azure rice regulates deficiency and receives the qi of medicines. Pound the Southern Candle herb and tree to extract their juice, then soak the Azure Dragon rice in it to prepare the medicine for consumption. This tree is woody yet resembles a herb, hence it is called the Southern Candle herb-tree. It is also named Monkey Medicine, Male Continuance, Posterior Excellence, Wei-na Wood, and King of Herbs and Trees. It grows on Mount Song’s Shao-shi, Mount Bao-du’s Chicken Head Mountain, and in all famous mountains—not merely in a few places. In the regions of Jiang-zuo and Wu-Yue, it is especially abundant. The locals call it Monkey Uncle or Dye Uncle, resembling gardenia. Its seeds resemble the fruit of the *Zanthoxylum* tree. The *Inner Transmission of Perfected King Jun of Pure Emptiness* elaborates on its methods in full.

The *Upper Prime Treasure Scripture* states: Those who consume the qi of the King of Herbs and Trees commune with the spirit; those who consume the sap of the Azure Candle will never fall. The Southern Candle is Azure Essence, hence it is also called Azure Candle. Consuming it leads to immortality.

It is also said: Regularly rinse with the Flower of the Dark Pool to benefit the six fluids. The commentary states: Diligently cultivate the Way of Cloud Sprouts to replenish the qi of the six palaces. Malachite is empty and luminous, with a youthful countenance—it is a superior immortal-grade mineral medicine as well as an herb or tree.

Regarding the thorn tree, the *Six Jia Yin Talismans* states it is also called Goat Thorn, Hollow Sparse, and Strong Thorn. The *Upper Clarity Six Jia Inner Scripture* contains the *Upper Clarity Jade Palace Five Thearchs’ Inner Contemplation Upper Method*, the *Upper Clarity Numinous Flight Six Jia Inner Contemplation Communion with the Numinous Upper Method*, and the *Pure Emptiness Perfected One’s Offering to the Numinous Flight Upper Method*.

The *Eight Simplicities Scripture* states: The sun’s essence is red with the metal’s essence; the stone’s radiance is the flower of the Water Mother. Refined by the sun’s soul, its eight rays shine. Consuming it, the mysterious gates of essence and spirit generate wondrous light in the body, granting the same lifespan as the sun and moon.

The Yellow Flower of Moonlight: On the twenty-fifth day of the lunar month, when the moon passes above the Eastern Well, bathe in its numinous radiance to adorn and refine the essence’s rays, making the Yellow Flower bright and resplendent. Those who seek immortality should gather the Yellow Flower from the Eastern Well on that day, consume the yang essence from the moon’s soul, allowing it to flow and moisten the nine orifices, and spiritually stabilize the five palaces’ chambers. Cultivating this Way, one ascends to the moon’s court. The moon’s soul resides within the Eastern Well, which is the gateway where the sun and moon’s radiance commune.

The *Three Primes True Unity Scripture* states: Su Lin consumed the Flowing Azure Purple Pellets of Preserving the Numinous Pine Smoke, granting longevity, emerging from yin into yang, and making one’s complexion shine like jade.

If the Three Corpses are not expelled, even if one abstains from grains and the five flavors, the worms will not die. The *Scripture of the Three Ways’ Sequential Practice* states: The Upper Prime Lord of the Southern Culmen received the essentials of the Highest Sequential Practice of the Three Ways—the Way of Yellow Qi and Yang Essence. Gathering and guiding the numinous radiance, sipping the August Flower, gazing upward to consume the Flying Root, contemplating the Seven Luminaries in the Purple Dawn, the Three Radiance’s reflections hanging down, the Seven Essences flanking the chariot, the Five Numinous intertwining like sashes, the Four Offices composing the chapters, the Western Tortoise determining the records—this is titled the Inscription of the Lofty Dawn.

The *Fourth Hidden Instructions of Ascending Perfection* states: The Supreme Ultimate Perfected One consumed the Four Poles’ Cloud Sprouts.

The *Upper Scripture of the Sacred Sword* states: The Barbarian Immortal Mushroom is the flower of flying to heaven. There is also the Fragrance of Reversed Life and the Mountain of Jade Honey.

The *Golden Root Scripture* states: Consume the radiance and swallow the qi, chewing the mysterious root.

The *Upper Scripture of Great Possession* states: The Three Ones of the Mud-Pellet Heavenly Thearch are the numinous ancestors of the single body, the life roots of the hundred spirits, the mountain source of fluids and humors, and the jade chamber of the soul’s essence. Thus, the Stomach Pool’s body is square to receive things, the Brain Palace is round and empty to accommodate the true. Ten thousand hairs stand erect, a thousand pores emit smoke, virtue equips one with heaven and earth, and one merges with the Great Mystery—hence it is named the Mud-Pellet.

The Mud-Pellet is the supreme spirit of the bodily form. It is also said: Between the brows, when one retreats inward, on the left resides the Luminous Youthful Perfected Lord, on the right the Luminous Female Perfected Official, and at the center the Luminous Mirror Spirit Lord. These three lords jointly govern the Hall of Luminosity. They wear belts adorned with four jade bells and hold jade mirrors in their mouths, the bells and mirrors all of red jade. Should a Daoist feel fear, they may visualize these three spirits causing the jade bells to chime, their sound reaching the Great Ultimate, and the mirrors to emit light for ten thousand yards. Visualizing these three lords exhaling red qi to pour into the adept’s mouth will subdue a thousand demons and extinguish ten thousand ghosts. If the Daoist feels hunger or thirst, they may absorb and swallow this qi, and in a moment exhale red qi to pour into their own mouth, then absorb and swallow it again—soon they will be sated.

Moreover, upon rising each morning, one should swallow saliva thirty times, wipe the face with the hands, and rub the eyes as a regular practice, visualizing the spittle transforming into fluid essence.

The *Mysterious Scripture of the Supreme One Heavenly Lord* states: Those who wish to visualize and absorb the qi of the sun and moon must first understand the images of the sun and moon. The sun is round in form but square in its radiance, while the moon is square in essence but round in its image. The radiance is concealed within the form, and the essence is hidden within the image. The radiance is red, the image yellow—these are the hun-souls of the sun and moon. Knowing this Dao, one may then exhale and inhale the flowing rosy clouds.

The method for absorbing solar qi: At dawn, gather the moon’s essence; at midnight, visualize it so that its light and image illuminate one’s Mud-Pellet, penetrating the five viscera and suffusing the entire body—thus may one attain long life. It is also said: Visualize the sun entering your mouth as if savoring its flavor. Visualize the moon entering your navel, descending to the Gate of Life to illuminate the chamber of yin.

It further states: Close the eyes and click the teeth five times. With the third finger of the left hand, press the philtrum beneath the nose seven times. With the second finger of the right hand, press between the brows nine times. This is the method of restraining the three, five, seven, and nine to seal and govern the gates of the hundred spirits.

The *Eight Gates Scripture of the Mysterious Mother* states: The medicines consumed by the Perfected of Great Simplicity include *Cloud-Grass of Mysterious Purity*, which is the fat of black sesame vine—also called *Mysterious Purity*. *Flower of Sweet Wine* is white honey. *Five Radiance Seven White Numinous Greens* is garlic chives. *White Essence Flying Dragon* is white quartz. The fat of black sesame and white honey congealed like snow are also mentioned. It further states: *Cloud-Fat* is fragrant, sweet, and delicious; it strengthens and replenishes essence, stabilizes the five viscera, preserves qi, and congeals fluids, nourishing the hun and po souls—it is the supreme medicine. It is also called *Mysterious Water Jade Liquid*, *Flying Dragon Cloud-Fat*, and *Refined Essence of the Five Stones*. After fifteen years of consumption, the body will emit jade-like light, internally and externally luminous, attaining long life with heaven and earth and the ability to command ghosts and spirits. After three years, one will be able to read at night. This medicine surpasses the ingestion of the eight minerals. Moreover, when the five minerals enter the throat, they refine the five viscera, causing five-colored flowers to bloom within them.

It further states: Those who regularly absorb the essence of the sun and moon should frequently eat bamboo shoots. Bamboo shoots are the embryo of solar essence—also called *Great Luminosity*. One should also eat pine needles, for the pine is the finest of trees. To absorb the sun and moon, one must consume these substances to resonate with their qi.

The Perfected of Great Void states: The pine is the finest of trees. All pines and cypresses are called *fine trees*.

The *Scripture of Great Pervasion* states: The Dao Lord disperses teachings to nourish the form, expelling the old and receiving the new, gathering essence and expelling filth. Rinsing with morning radiance to summon the Solar Sovereign, drawing in night’s brightness to embrace the Moon Pearl, knotting the luminous and absorbing the celestial, the twin effulgences unite in journey. Flying mushrooms and mysterious blossoms clothe one like a mountain’s raiment.

It further states: The Dao Lord exhales and inhales the seven darknesses, wields the six perfections with wisdom, and lodges the eight liberations to achieve far-reaching clarity. Light and unbound, the heart rests in serene simplicity, returning to the state of infancy.

It further states: The Dao Lord gazes upward to pin the sun’s radiance in the hair, gathers fallen moon pearls, plucks the crimson fruits of the forest of jade, and consumes the purple lotuses of the Mysterious River. Leaning against the numinous carriage, he governs the tiger-script.

It further states: The warm foam of the three yellows transmutes essence; the crimson liquid refines spirit. The nine jades emit their brilliance, the jade-like stones transform endlessly. Azure reflects the watery yang, the eight jades scatter their light. The lush green nectar rides the dawn’s mist, flowing gold and moon-brightness, the Mysterious Ford’s jade liquid, the numinous fat of the five lords, the scattering light-leaves of sound. One chant unfolds eight manifestations, the waves of wisdom like fire’s essence, the jade ginger of Yi and Li, the golden mirror of a hundred convergences, the refining incense of śarīra, the lush and numinous treasure—transforming and transmuting the patterns of scripture. Once the knife’s edge is arrayed, life becomes immeasurable. These are the precious medicines of the Sovereign of Primordial Perfection, the secrets of the Celestial Thearch. Some refine the five-cloud jade-flower numinous gold elixir, the vermilion soul and green lotus, the flowery fat and azure essence, the southern candle and emerald [omission], the cinnabar sand and hollow azure, gathering the five dawns’ jade abyss and pure nectar—all capable of reverting the old to the new and transforming age into infancy.

It further states: Suspend the crucible and refine five times to soften water; the nine jades merge and coalesce into jade. Fire-jade becomes pearls, flowing gold gathers jade. Aligning with the supreme contract, how could life be overturned?

The *Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection, Fourth Scroll* states: The Perfected of the Great Ultimate consume the Cloud-Sprouts of the Four Poles, the supreme immortal method, bowing to the primal radiance of the five directions and consuming the essence of the nine rosy clouds. The commentary states: This refers to the primal qi of the clear dawn and the radiant essence of the first rosy clouds. The yang number of the sun is nine—hence the nine rosy clouds. The main text states: Thus the divine light shines internally, the vermilion flowers manifest externally, and the body generates jade-like luster. The commentary states: The form, together with the luminous, draws in the dawn’s radiance to quench thirst and consumes the essence of rosy clouds to nourish the root. The viscera and the divine light merge in brilliance; the complexion and countenance glow with the vermilion flowers. Jade-like moisture suffuses the body, harmonious qi illumines the form—all achieved by the numinous edge of the five dawns and the abyssal liquid of the six streams.

It further states: Those who obtain the ninefold jade liquid and the eightfold flying essence of fine jade unite the two luminaries at life’s end, their fate harmonizing with Heaven and Earth.

It further states: When emptiness and tranquility fill the interior, guarding the primal while swallowing saliva—this is called the True One.

It further states: Draw the divine with the six liquids and five qi.

It further states: Constantly swallow the crimson liquid to nourish the Three Palaces.

It further states: Cloud sprouts are the essence and qi of the Five Elders, the rosy mist of the Great Ultimate. Thus, one gathers the numinous edge of radiant light to harmonize the six liquids. In profound and obscure resonance, the ten thousand spirits descend; in hidden illumination, they seek one another, responding without a call.

Therefore, when the dragon intones over the abyss, rosy clouds descend from the heavens; when the tiger roars on the sacred peak, the four winds surge in all directions. The yang-burning mirror summons brightness, and vermilion fire arises in abundance; the yin-gathering vessel rarely meets shade, yet dark streams brim and overflow—naturally, their depths defy measurement. How much more so for the scholar who anchors the heart in the mysterious, refining the roots of the Dao, purging impurities from the breast, and preserving true correctness within the Three Palaces? They gather the scattered radiance of the five dawns, consume the rosy nectar of the six bodies, harvest the rare treasures of the nine heavens, and utter the arcane and wondrous secret words. Dragon brilliance leaps forth, luminous light shines sevenfold. They savor the three flowers upon their gleaming teeth, take their fill of liquid at the edge of their lips, internally refine the six viscera, and open their faculties to penetrating clarity. Inhaling and exhaling the primal of Heaven, they temper the hun and po to refine the form.

*The Declarations of the Perfected, Fifth Scroll* states: The Yellow Mountain Lord’s formula says: In nurturing nature and consuming medicinal substances, one should not eat garlic or pomegranate seeds. Daoists must not partake of these, and they are also forbidden from chamber arts. Not only do these obstruct the efficacy of the medicine, but each pound consumed also diminishes one’s lifespan by a hundred days. Shen Xi’s oral formula states: When ingesting divine medicine, do not face north—this is a great taboo. On *hai* and *zi* days, one must not spit, lest one lose essence and qi, shortening lifespan and rendering the medicine’s potency as inert as earth.

*The Declarations of the Perfected, Seventh Scroll* states: During the reign of Emperor Zhao of Han, a woman named Wei Zi, daughter of Zhang Qing, regularly consumed mist qi. She claimed that mist qi is the flowering essence of mountains, marshes, water, and fire, the flourishing qi of metal and stone. Prolonged consumption enables one to disperse the form and enter emptiness, merging the body with clouds and mist. Wei Zi said: She received this method from Ting Wenqi, the Jade Consort of the Eastern Sea. It further states: The female immortal Li He transmitted the rites for consuming the qi of the five planets and attaining the Dao. It further states: The immortal woman Fan Qiulin practiced gathering the radiance of the sun and moon, consuming the blossoms of the ninefold luminous mirror. It further states: Chen Shijing consumed atractylodes and the cold blossoms of alisma. It further states: When the Perfected One of the Primordial Unity first entered Mount Tiantai, he consumed sesame. It further states: Sima Jisheng consumed the blossoms of bright cinnabar, gathering the radiance of the supporting dawn, rendering his complexion like that of a twenty-year-old girl, his beard three feet long, black as ink.

*The Declarations of the Perfected, Ninth Scroll* states: Gather the sun’s blossom on the left, and on the right, seize the moon’s root.

*The Inner Formula of the Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected Ones of the Upper Clarity* states: The incantation for hastening to the sun and moon reads: Consume the azure essence of the sun’s grain, drink the cloudy sapphire’s richness, feast in the city of the eight poles, ascend the terrace of luminous perfection, sit in the hall of rare groves, and chant the words of the Jade Dawn. It further states: O spirit of the sun’s soul, radiant child of the pearl’s light, let me journey west to the gate of the six ridges, enter the Jade Palace of Harmonious Dawn in the Woven Silk Hill’s Eight Radiance Upper Chamber. May I obtain the talisman of a thousand lights, wear the insignia of the streaming star’s night glow, sit in the Hall of Great Harmony, ascend the Terrace of the Seven Spirits, drink the moon’s blossom and cloud’s cream, consume the yellow jade’s purple nectar, chant the verses of the Most High, and recite the words of the Jade Dawn.

It further states: The formula for the Divine Elixir of the Eight Radiance and Four Blossoms of the Most High, the Crimson-Born Five-Pearl Spirit Pill—this elixir has eight names: sometimes called the Four Blossoms’ Flower, sometimes the Purple Jade Sap of the Great Tenuity, sometimes the Five-Pearl Flower Elixir, sometimes the Crimson-Born Dawn Blossom, sometimes the Three-Flower Upper Elixir, sometimes the Most High Flying Rigor, and sometimes the Nine Dawns’ Upper Elixir.

*The Arrayed Records of the Latter Sage Dao Lord* states: The Yellow Water Moon Blossom Elixir, the Returning Water Jade Essence Elixir, and the Azure Reflection Liquid of the Water Yang. Thus, the Perfected Ones of the Most High feast upon the seven awakenings and roam the ten thousand directions—truly, it is through the flying essence of the four liquids and the cinnabar sovereign of the five pearls. It further states: When spat upon the ground, it becomes the light of the sun and moon. It further states: The northern capital’s langgan blossom is the cinnabar-born elixir’s grain.

*The Scripture of the Seven Stars’ Transference* states: When thirsty, sip from the fine well’s vast spring of jade mushrooms; when hungry, ingest the dragon embryo’s fine jade and the crimson tree’s red child.

*The Scripture of the Purple Radiance of Blazing Light* states: The Nine Sovereigns’ Great Essence, the Perfected Lord of the Northern Ultimate, augment my essence-embryo, strengthen my three hun, draw the sun’s blossom on the left, and seize the moon’s essence on the right.

*The Scripture of the Dao’s Foundation and Exhalation* states: When Daoists cultivate the body through exhalation and inhalation, fasting for one ten-day period, their essence and qi grow slightly warm, their complexion sallow. By the second ten-day period, movement causes dizziness and vertigo; the limbs feel restless, defecation becomes slightly difficult, urination turns reddish-yellow, or there may be a single movement—loose in the front, hard in the back. By the third ten-day period, the body grows emaciated, and walking becomes laborious. By the fourth ten-day period, the complexion brightens, and the heart and mind find peace. By the fifth ten-day period, the five viscera harmonize, and essence and qi are internally nurtured. By the sixth ten-day period, the body returns to its former state, and the joints function smoothly. By the seventh ten-day period, the heart detests clamor and deceit, and the will aspires to lofty heights. By the eighth ten-day period, one becomes serene and tranquil, faithfully understanding the methods and arts. By the ninth ten-day period, one’s countenance becomes sleek and lustrous, and one’s voice clear and resonant. By the tenth ten-day period, essence and qi are fully present, and the effects grow daily more manifest. If cultivation continues without cease, lifespan naturally lengthens. After three years, scars and marks fade, and the complexion gains luster. After six years of cultivation, the marrow fills and the brain solidifies, and one foreknows life and death.

After nine years of practice, one commands ghosts and spirits, and is titled a "Perfected Person," assisting the Supreme August One above. One’s lifespan aligns with Heaven, and one’s radiance merges with the sun. Should the teachings be transmitted to the unworthy, the transgressor bears the calamity.

*The Celestial Writings of the Upper Canon* speaks of the Dragon-Embryo Golden Elixir of Nine Refinements, which preserves form and dispenses with grain, repelling the myriad deviations. The Five-Titled Master’s ritual includes the Purple Court Golden Night.

*The Jade Instructions, Lower Scroll* states: The Primordial Five Qi invariably ascend at cock’s crow to assemble at the Numinous Treasure Jade Mountain in the Mystic Capital’s Upper Palace. As the yang light first brightens, it scatters the radiance of the Primordial Beginning, surveying the myriad heavens. Its qi is lush and dense, its brilliance warm and pervasive, its essence like moon-pearls, its light like purple clouds. The qi revolves like a chariot’s wheel, ascending to govern the passes of the Nine Heavens, centrally securing the numinous mountains of the Five Emperors.

The appended note reads: The roots of the Five Teeth of the Learned Scholar, the Great Wisdom Perfected of the Upper Palace, and the host of sages all partake of this radiance at its appointed time, inhaling its essence aloft. In harmony with Heaven, they attain boundlessness. Later sagely Daoists, who abstain from grain, maintain long fasts on the Five Peaks, sever ties with the dusty world, and aspire to purity and truth, may daily ingest the solar root’s rosy dawn and swallow the sun’s essence. They swiftly perceive their bodies suffused with jade-like luster, their faces aglow, and ascend to the rank of Jade Sovereign.

*The Scripture of Guiding and Absorbing the Three Luminaries* states: The Three Luminaries are named Flowing Essence, Luminous Infant, Dharma Qi, Yang King, Cloud Blossom, Guiding Immortal, Nine Transformations, and Settled Radiance—these refer to the immortal arts of embryo refinement through the Three Luminaries.

*The Transmission of Daoist Learning, Scroll Two* records: Xu Mai, styled Shu Xuan, was originally named Ying in his youth but later changed his name. He wandered into Xincheng Daoshan, consuming the valley’s *ju* vine and seeds, and practiced qi-absorption, sustaining a single breath for over a thousand cycles. In the second year of the Jin Yonghe reign, he relocated to the Western Mountains of Lin’an. It further states: Yan Xuanzhi of Gaoping and Peng Chu of Langye both sought instruction from Xu Mai. Xu Mai said, "Master Yan may practice qi-absorption to cease grain consumption. Master Peng should take herbs to augment his qi." He then taught Peng to ingest *zhu* (atractylodes) and entrusted him with the method. After three years of devoted service, Xu Mai said, "You have grasped this; you need only cultivate diligently." With single-minded devotion, their hearts became like dead ashes, their forms like discarded husks. Each was to seek a secluded place to refine their essence. Thereupon, Xuanzhi went to Qian to focus on ingesting *zhu*.

Scroll Three further records: Wang Jia, styled Zinian, a native of Longxi, dwelled in a cave hewn into the cliffs of Dongyang Valley. He consumed no grains, wore no fine garments, and practiced pure emptiness and qi-absorption, shunning worldly intercourse. Yao Chang and Murong sought him, but he did not respond.

*The True Reports, Scroll Five* states: Fan Youzhong of Liaoxi was the Supervisor of Huayang. He underwent embryonic transformation and shape-shifting, and now resides here, perpetually absorbing the Three Qi. The method of the Three Qi involves visualizing blue, white, and red qi, each like a bowstring descending from the eastern sun into the mouth, drawing it in ninety times until sated. After a decade of practice, the three-colored qi spontaneously arise within the body, and one attains transcendence. This is the High Prime Lord’s method of the Inner Effulgences of Grand Simplicity. Practicing it daily with eyes closed yields ever-improving results.

The Jade Maiden of Eastern Sea’s Eastern Flower, Ting Wenqi, transmitted the Mist-Swallowing Method to the Female Perfected of Containing Truth Terrace, Zhang Weizi. At dawn, in quiet repose, one may sit or lie as preferred. First, close the eyes and inwardly visualize the hair and temples until the five viscera are seen. Then exhale through the mouth twenty-four times. As one performs this, the eyes perceive five-colored qi coiling around the face. With prolonged practice, one habitually rides clouds and mist in travel.

It further states: In practicing the Way of Preserving the Mysterious and White, at dawn one sits or lies as desired, visualizing black qi in the Mud-Pellet Palace, white qi in the heart, and yellow qi in the navel. The three qi arise together like clouds covering the body, then transform into fire that burns the body, rendering it translucent and unified inside and out. The practice continues until midday, concluding with 120 qi-absorptions. The Dao is thus complete, granting longevity, averting disasters, and repelling harm. It strictly prohibits wine, meat, and the five pungent flavors. One should dwell apart in quiet contemplation, especially avoiding sexual intercourse, for it leads to death.

It further states: In learning the Dao, one must only seek to silence the breath and nurture the spirit, drawing the breath to its utmost and exhaling gently. One must not speak loudly or shout, lest the spirit be wearied and depleted. Such practices do not nurture life.

*The True Reports, Genuine Mandates, Scroll Four* states: The body soars on high, tasting the mysterious and savoring the real. Drawing in the radiant luminaries, the Six Spirits congeal in stillness. The Eight Brilliances shine forth, submitting to the numinous root. Sorrows and burdens do not disturb the Mystic Abode; grief and longing do not agitate the Crimson Ford.

*The True Reports, Scroll Seven* states: Fan Youchong of Liaoxi underwent embryonic transformation and shape-shifting, and now resides here, perpetually practicing the method of the blue, red, and white Three Qi, thereby attaining transcendence. It further states: Xu Zongdu of Jinling received the qi-restraining Way from the Master of Wind Valley. It also records: Long Shu, styled Bogao, a man of the Later Han, learned the method of ingesting embryonic qi from the immortal Diao Daolin. He shed his form and departed, concealing himself on Fangtai, where his master was the Recorder of Destinies. There was also Liu Aping, who dwelt in a grotto on Fangshan, perpetually absorbing the morning qi of the sun and moon. His complexion was like jade, and he appeared to be about thirty years old.

*The Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: In the ancient Chanli world, King Dui had a daughter named Guayin who, at fourteen, had never spoken. The king abandoned her in a desolate mountain. With no provisions, she daily faced the sun to swallow qi and drew in the moon’s essence, naturally sustaining herself without bodily decline.

*The Cavernous Numinous Chapters* states:
At dawn, ingest the qi of the Five Clouds;
at dusk, chant the Three Morning Lights.

It further records:
Feast on qi to fill the long mounds,
swallow saliva as golden water blooms.
Seal the night to pluck the decayed frame—
restore youth to teeth of ivory white.
The body enters the kalpa of no death,
its name inscribed in the Jade Numinous Capital.

*The Nine Songs of the Eight Yang Essences* declares:
Seven-jeweled jade grains, golden elixir,
purple rays concealed in lingzhi—
gather with the left, pluck with the right,
night-glowing phoenix brain,
tiger foam, cloud jade,
exquisite frost, rare flavors—
one taste and the body brushes the Great Void.

*The Hidden Writ of the Rushing Sun and Moon’s Two Radiant Forms* states:
Drink the moon’s flowery cloud cream,
consume the essence of yellow jade and purple perfection.

*The Second Scroll of the Traditions of Daoist Learning* records:
In place of rock candy cakes, use stalactites.
These two substances both arise from the moisture of stones.
This appears in the *Biography of Xu Mai*.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* states:
King Mu of Zhou journeyed north to Kunlun,
where he drank the crimson mountain’s stone marrow
and ate the fruit of the jade tree.

*The Third Scroll of the Traditions of Daoist Learning* records:
Yan Ji, styled Zhongwei, lived at the end of Emperor Ming’s reign in the Han.
From youth he cherished the Dao and virtue,
and never served in the world.

At first entering Mount Huayin, he consumed tree saplings, great yellow essence, cultivated mica, realgar, cinnabar, and zhi grasses.

*The Fourteenth Scroll* states: Shuang Xi, styled Zhongyuan, was a man of the Liang dynasty. Initially, after abstaining from grains, he grew emaciated. A wealthy man, Fan Xin, requested him to identify efficacious herbs and provided servants to gather them. Soon after, he regained his strength. The water buffalo given by the Fan family had plowed the mountains for many years.

*The Twentieth Scroll* states: The female official Xiao Zhen, a native of Dantu in Donghai, left home in her youth to study the Dao in Yishan, consuming only cypress leaves.

*The Upper Scroll of the Biographies of the Immortals* states: Chi Jiang Ziyu was a man of the Yellow Emperor’s time. He did not eat the five grains but consumed the flowers of a hundred herbs. Another, Wo Quan, was a herb-gatherer from Mount Huai. Fond of eating pine nuts, his body grew hair several inches long, his eyes became square, and he could fly to keep pace with galloping horses.

Master Luli received the *Mountain-Hidden Numinous Treasure Formulae*:
First, the *Flying Turtle Mat of Yi and Luo*;
Second, the *White Yu’s Correct Mechanism*;
Third, the *Balanced Pressing Union*.
Consuming these daily restores youth. One could walk five hundred li in a day, lift a thousand斤, shed skin ten times in a year, and finally ascend as an immortal.

*The Inner Transmission of the Perfected Lord Wang of Pure Emptiness* states: The Lord of the Dao of Immortals bestowed upon Lord Wang two sheng of *Cloud Azure Yang Water* and *Morning-Flown Cinnabar Fat*. Lord Wang bowed and consumed them. Over nine years, he could see ten thousand li away, walk three thousand li in a day, sit and vanish at will, and command a host of spirits.

*The Licorice Pill Formula* from the transmission of Lady Wei of Mount Nanyue:

First, six liang of licorice.
Second, three liang of cinnabar, of the finest quality.
Third, five liang of rhubarb.
Fourth, seven liang of dried rehmannia.
Fifth, ten liang of white wood.
Sixth, five liang of schisandra.
Seventh, five liang of ginseng.
Eighth, four liang of poria.
Ninth, three liang of tangkuei.
Tenth, four liang of asparagus.
Eleventh, two liang of stephania.
Twelfth, three liang of polyporus.
Thirteenth, two liang of asarum.
Fourteenth, two liang of cassia seeds.

For these fourteen ingredients, use only the freshest and finest herbs; do not employ stale or aged ones. First, grind each finely without sifting, then weigh the powders to ensure the correct liang. Place them in a mortar in order, beginning with licorice, and pound one thousand times. Next, add cinnabar and pound another thousand times. Continue adding each ingredient in sequence, pounding one thousand times after each addition. In total, the fourteen herbs require sixteen thousand poundings, amounting to thirty thousand poundings in all.

Once the medicine is prepared, form it into honeyed pills the size of firmiana seeds. Take ten pills after meals, beginning with a small dose; up to thirty pills may be taken. This medicine internally eradicates illness, is non-toxic, and has no prohibitions. Consuming it for a year yields great benefit; do not expect immediate results. Women who take it will bear many children and suffer no illnesses. Prolonged consumption leads to immortality and deathlessness.

Prepare the medicine in a separate, clean room. Do not allow many people to witness the process. Bathe, purify yourself, and maintain a fast for three or four days before grinding the ingredients. It cures a hundred afflictions and a thousand diseases; their names cannot all be recorded here. As for the practices of consuming medicines and guiding qi, the various scriptures contain much on this; it will not be repeated here.

*Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns, Scroll Three*
*Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns, Scroll Four*

**Master Wang Xuanhe of Luhai, Feathered Guest of the Great Tang, on the Art of Grain Abstention**

*The Sixth Scroll of Accounts of Daoist Learning* states: Chu Boyu, styled Yuanqu, was a native of Qiantang in Wu Commandery. He secluded himself on Mount Huo, refining essences and ingesting mist, and for many years abstained from grain.

*The Scripture on Exhalation and Inhalation* says: Grain abstention is the Way of the primordial spirit. When one first practices qi-ingestion for one or two days, the grain-qi has not yet stabilized, and the complexion appears dull and sallow. By the third day, grain-qi departs, and essence-qi arrives. On the fourth and fifth days, essence-qi harmonizes yin and yang. By the sixth day, spirit and essence settle, the ears and eyes grow keen, steps become nimble, and the body daily strengthens. On the seventh day, one constantly desires to ascend lightly—such is the effect of the supreme Way. In dreams and waking, one faintly perceives communion with divine luminosity. By the eighth day, the spirit roams the eight extremities; one can act in silence, the mouth naturally savors sweetness, and the will and bones strengthen of themselves. On the ninth day, spirit and essence are complete; the weak in form grow strong, and the spirit-qi daily solidifies. Without movement, one travels afar; without approach, one draws near. The complexion daily brightens. By the tenth day, all spirits arrive, the gates are sealed, jade maidens attend, and one ascends lightly to either side, drifting like a heron in the clouds—thus is the Way attained.

It further states: The Way treasures essence as its jewel. Bestowed, it gives life to others; retained, it gives life to the self. Life to the self ensures eternal transcendence—this is the rank of a worldly immortal. Bestowing life to others is the fulfillment of merit, after which one retreats into reclusion. The vulgar deem this arduous; how much worse to forget bestowal and cast it aside, wasting much through lack of study, thus aging and forfeiting life! Lord Lao said: Essence is the river that flows through the blood vessels. When essence departs, one withers and ages—hence its value. The human body is a state; spirit is its ruler, essence its minister, and qi its people. Constantly cherishing essence is the essential Way.

Lord Lao said: The Way is qi. Treasuring qi is to attain the Way; attaining the Way is to endure long. Spirit is essence. Treasuring essence is to attain spirit luminosity; attaining spirit luminosity is to attain long life.

It further states: The Way of long life treasures essence as its jewel, for essence is that by which humans are born. Essence is the treasure—hence it is called the Way. The Way of a single day: sated at dawn, hungry at dusk. The Way of a single month: not losing its waxing and waning. The Way of a single year: lean in summer, plump in winter. The Way of a hundred years: moderating grain and eating jujubes. The Way of a thousand years: solitary man, no woman. This is called long life and enduring vision—none can count its measure. The above passages all derive from the foundations of the Way.

*The Scripture on Exhalation and Inhalation* further states: I have heard the Eight Lords say: Those who eat plants gain strength; those who eat meat gain courage; those who eat grain gain wisdom; those who eat qi gain spirit. The sage, who eats nothing, does not die.

*The Scripture of the Yellow Court* says: When immortals and Daoists ingest qi, it is not due to divine power but to the accumulation of essence and the focus of harmonious qi. All people eat grain and the five flavors; I alone consume the great harmony of yin-yang qi—thus I do not die. Resting the root and eating qi is the Way of life; returning essence through yin and yang is the supreme treasure. How fortunate to cultivate the body and attain longevity! Yet some vainly yearn for distant things, believing them nonexistent, and thus revert to folly, hastening old age. A thousand gold pieces spent on burial bring no benefit; grief, wailing, and lamentation only bring remorse. Nothing compares to long life as the greatest good. Thus, the essentials of the Way are few in words and brief in writing. If the brush falls upon truth, cultivate it without falsehood, and you will ascend to Great Wu without ceasing.

*The One Hundred Twentieth Scroll of the Scripture of Great Peace* states: Therefore, those who eat have a fixed term of life; those who do not eat conspire with the spirits. Those who eat qi attain spirit luminosity; those who neither drink nor eat complete their years with Heaven and Earth.

*The One Hundred Forty-Fifth Scroll* states:
Question: What do those of the upper, middle, and lower ranks who attain the Way and transcend the world consume?
Answer: The highest of the upper rank consume wind and qi; the second rank consume medicinal flavors; the third rank eat sparingly to clear their intestines and stomachs.

It further states: Heaven is distant and boundless. Without consuming wind and qi, how can one move swiftly and circulate through the Way of Heaven? One must also communicate merit with spirit officials, forming companionship—hence the consumption of wind and qi. Next, one should join forces with the essence of Earth, harmonizing the five soils, traversing high and low mountains and rivers, entering water along the mountains, and mutually communicating with Earth, sharing in its merit. One cannot eat grain—hence one drinks water and travels. Those who practice moderation in eating as the Way have not yet fully formed their semblance; they differ only slightly from ordinary people. Thus, eating sparingly to clear the intestines is also a means to attain the Way.

*The Scripture of the Foundations of the Way* states: Consuming medicinal herbs and eating wheat is excellent! In ancient times, the Daoist Gan Shi ingested qi and ate wheat to transcend the world.

It further states: One who unites with the Way does not speak of attainment; the true one remains awake day and night without sleep. Sun and moon merge their light; one is neither hungry nor thirsty—this is the breathing of the tortoise and dragon embryo.

It further states: Those who eat grain are called grain immortals. If they practice without ceasing, they may prolong their years. Those who do not eat grain may ascend through the clouds and transcend the world, attaining deathlessness.

*The Inner Transmission of the Perfected Lord Wang of Pure Emptiness* states: The Perfected of the Great Ultimate said: Those who receive life-qi from the five grains form embryos and nurture beings, inevitably embracing the flowing essence of grain-qi. Uniting with the myriad transformations of the true also refines the mysterious moisture of the five grains. Like a child lodging in its parents, one relies on what gives life to grasp life itself. If one does not follow the original source of what gives life but abruptly abandons its foundation, has there ever been one who did not wither in partial vision and sever their years, withering away? All should follow their origin, comply with its flow, refine and harmonize it, subtly dispersing the root. Thus, the constructive and defensive qi are easily refined in daily use, and the six viscera transform grain gradually. Therefore, relying on grain is the excellent art of employing life; following the root to depart from the root is the wondrous trace of grasping illumination.

Thus, fanning the eastern radiance of the southern candle, summoning the vermilion spirit of the nascent sprout, the five fluids become serene and still, the hundred passages fill and overflow. The spirit delights in the three palaces, the hun-soul softens and the po-soul settles into tranquility. Further invigorated by morning rinsing with the blossoming spring, the five directions’ ethereal essence, drumming the jade pool, and inhaling the mysterious essence, the radiant fatness flourishes in the □ direction, the stomach fills and is steadied by the void azure. Therefore, a thousand calculations unfold as one, longevity flourishes with the years, and with each year the elixir advances—one ascends the immortal court in flying steps.

Those who consume a full dose will never again face the collapse of life. Five-colored clouds arise around the body, and the bodily spirit, qi, and essence are all refined. They may eat nine times in a single day, the hundred passages flowing smoothly, or go a full year without hunger. Returning from old age to infancy, they eat when encountering food and remain at ease when not—this is the wondrous method of the highest immortals, the marvelous numen of grain-abstention.

The aforementioned "southern candle" is an immortal herb. Though its form is woody, it resembles a grass, hence it is called the "southern candle grass-wood." It is also named "monkey medicine," "male continuance," "posterior brilliance," "Weina wood," and "king of grasses and trees." It grows on Song Gao’s Shaoshi Peak and Baidu’s Jitou Mountain, and its methods of ingestion have already been recorded in the *Register of Dietary Practices*. This formula also appears in the *Dengzhen Yinjue* (Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection), Scroll Ten. The previous dietary practices described therein are largely similar to this, with only minor differences.

The *Scripture on Exhalation and Inhalation for Daoist Foundations* states: Those who abstain from grains, cease rice consumption, and consume only pure substances must not drink wine, for it causes confusion, knotting the qi and vessels, obstructing the hundred meridians. It generates heat—better not to drink at all, that one may remain pure and undefiled.

The *Supreme Yellow Plain Scripture of Forty-Four Methods* states: All Daoists who absorb harmonious qi, preserve the spirit, ingest the radiance, and pursue longevity must carefully avoid the five pungent vegetables and the corruptions of wine and lust. Thus did the divine beings of old say: The five pungents are the axes that hew at the storehouses of life; wine and lust are the coffin and outer casket that bury the body. Only by severing the harm wrought by axes and sealing the deathly abode of coffin and casket may one ascend the path to longevity and gradually tread the trail to divine transcendence.

The *Scripture of Boundless Transformation* states: Those who eat meat and the five pungents—no spirit will dwell within their bodies.

The *True Record of the Golden Book* states: Consuming the five pungents mars the countenance of immortality. The five pungents are: scallion, garlic, leek, Chinese chive, and *xingqu* (the latter now obscure in common usage).

The *Register of Divine Elixirs and Immortal Medicines* and the twenty-ninth section, "Hidden Mountain Grade," of the ninth scroll of *Dietary Practices* both list the names of immortal herbs.

The *Supreme Scripture of the Eight Radiant, Four-Blossomed, Purple-Essence, Five-Pearled, Crimson-Born Spirit Elixir* states:

First, Crimson Mound Vermilion Child—*Oral Instructions* say this is cinnabar, the finest essence from Ba and Yue.
Second, Cinnabar Mountain Sun-Soul—*Oral Instructions* say this is realgar, selected for its cavernous luminosity.
Third, Mystic Terrace Cinnabar Flower—*Oral Instructions* say this is orpiment.
Fourth, Azure Essence Jade Maiden—*Oral Instructions* say this is malachite.
Fifth, Numinous Flower Liquid Fat—*Oral Instructions* say this is frankincense.
Sixth, Northern Emperor Mystic Pearl—*Oral Instructions* say this is saltpeter.
Seventh, Purple Mound Patterned Marquis—*Oral Instructions* say this is purple quartz.
Eighth, Eastern Flower Youth—*Oral Instructions* say this is costus root.
