They affirmed: “Your bones and destiny align with the Dao; you are to inherit the legacy of ancient loyal ministers. Today, we confer upon you the hereditary title of Ghostly Marshal, so that your descendants may lead the state without end.” Thereupon, Lord Lao personally transmitted to Daoling the *Step-by-Step Mandate of the Most High*, instructing him to tread the cosmic warp and weft, govern the Three Heavens, assist the state and sustain destiny, nurture all beings, and regulate the *qi* of spirits. He was established as the State Preceptor. In accordance with its measures, he founded the twenty-four *zhi* and nineteen *jinglu* retreats, and was entrusted with the Orthodox Unity Alliance of Awesome Might, to punish the false and perverse. He was allied with the myriad spirits under heaven through divided talismans, all adhering to the Orthodox Unity Dao.

On the seventh day of the seventh month in the first year of *Shanghuang*, the Most High Dao Lord Lao established the essential oral instructions of the eight upper *zhi* grades, held in the palm. The Five Dragons of the *Fu Kui* shaped heaven and earth, arrayed mountains and peaks, and Lord Lao established the *zhi* positions to transform the vulgar. The foolish, insatiable in their greed, fail to grasp this true path to immortality—how could it be casually transmitted to the unrefined?

**First: Yangping Zhi**
Located within the boundaries of Fan County in Shu Commandery, one hundred eighty *li* from Chengdu. The route follows the Luo River into the twin peaks of Two-Fork Mountain, a waterway of forty *li*. To the east of the *zhi* stands Dragon Gate, guarded by divine waters, with two cypress trees growing above. To the southwest lies a great spring, its waters flowing eastward. The *zhi* corresponds to the Horn Mansion; its rise is initiated by the noble, and its governance endures. The Heir Master, son of the Celestial Master, was named Heng, styled Lingzhen. Broad in wisdom and lofty in aspiration, he concealed himself to cultivate immortal arts. Emperor Ling of Han summoned him to serve as Gentleman of the Palace, but he declined. On the fifteenth day of the first month in the second year of *Guanghe* (a *jisi* day), he ascended to immortality upon this mountain. A *zhi* stele was erected, with a pair at the gate, named the Heir Master’s *Zhi*.

To the right lies Yangping Zhi Mountain, which contains the Main Registrar’s *Zhi*, the Heir Master’s *Zhi*, and the Lineage Master’s *Zhi*.

**Second: Lutang Mountain Zhi**
Located in the northern countryside of Fan County in Shu Commandery, three hundred *li* from Chengdu. Above stand immortal chambers and terraces, ancient sites of transcendence. In the first year of *Yongshou*, the Most High Lord Lao, together with Celestial Master Zhang, convened at this *zhi* with the Four Guardian Generals of the Great Year, the spirits of river shrines, and a hundred ghosts to carve stone and swear oaths, all adhering to the Orthodox Unity Alliance of Awesome Might. The mountain bears pines and cypresses, and the Five Dragon Immortal Caverns, through which boats may pass. Holding a torch, one may enter the cavern for three days without exhausting its depths. The *zhi* corresponds to the Neck Mansion; its rise is initiated by the archer, and its governance endures for eighty years.

**Third: Heming Divine Mountain, the Most High’s Zhi**
The *zhi* stands upon it, the mountain linked to Qingcheng Tian’guo Mountain, two hundred *li* from Chengdu, within the boundaries of Linqiong County in Shu Commandery. The direct path spans three hundred *li*, unknown to the world. It is the place where Ma Dizhi and He Danyang attained the Dao. Before the *zhi*, three waters converge into a single belt, where divine dragons reside. There are four golden nails, two stone vessels of gold and silver, and three *hu* of silkworms—some say Yin Xi presides over them. The *zhi* corresponds to the Root Mansion; its rise is initiated by the lowly, and its governance endures for sixty years. *The Fifth Biographies of Divine Immortals* states: When Celestial Master Zhang encountered turmoil in the Central Kingdom, he entered Heming Mountain in Shu to study the Dao.

**Fourth: Liyuan Mountain Zhi**
Located within the boundaries of Fan County in Shu Commandery, connected to Lutang Mountain Zhi, eighty *li* apart, two hundred fifty *li* from Chengdu. Above grow fruit pines and divine herbs; consuming them grants ascent to immortality. The Four Dragon Spirits emerge from the Gate of Riding. Fan Li presides over it. The *zhi* corresponds to the Room Mansion; its rise is initiated by the commoner, and its governance endures for twenty years.

**Fifth: Ge Gui Mountain Zhi**
Located within the boundaries of Fan County in Shu Commandery, connected to Liyuan Mountain, two hundred thirty *li* from Chengdu County, forty-eight *li* from the water mouth of Yangping Zhi. Yang Xianxian attained the Dao here. Above stands Pine-Chestnut Mountain, six hundred *zhang* in height.

**Sixth: Gengchu Zhi**
Corresponding to the Heart Mansion, initiated by the Daoist, its governance endures for ninety years.

**Seventh: Gengchu Zhi**
The mountain rises three hundred ninety *zhang* above the plain, located west of Yangquan County in Guanghan Commandery, five *li* from the county seat and two hundred eighty *li* from Chengdu. Immortals constantly come and go here, where one may transcend calamity and cultivate nature. This was once the place where Zhang Li attained the Dao. The mountain has two stone chambers and three dragon heads, with Huai River winding around it. Corresponding to the Tail Mansion, initiated by the ordained Daoist, its governance endures from beginning to end.

**Eighth: Qinzhong Zhi**
The mountain lies nine *li* east of Mianzhu County in Guanghan Commandery, two hundred *li* from Chengdu. The mountain floats; in ancient times, Han Zhong attained immortality here. To the front flows Fire Water; to the east, a Daoist path leads to Han and Luo. To the west of the *zhi* stands a great stone marker of bronze. Corresponding to the Winnowing Basket Mansion, initiated by the deranged, its governance endures from beginning to end.

**Ninth: Zhenduo Zhi**
The mountain lies in Xindu County of Guanghan Commandery, one hundred fifty *li* from Chengdu. The mountain bears *zhi* herbs and divine medicines; consuming them grants a lifespan of a thousand years. The mountain rises two hundred eighty *zhang* in height, with a pond at its front where sacred fish with five heads dwell. Here, Wang Fangping once met the Most High Lord Lao. Corresponding to the Dipper Mansion, initiated by a woman, its governance endures for seventy years.

On the fifth day of the tenth month of the first year of Wuji, the True and Upright Most High established the Eight Grades of Qi-Speed Formulas in the Central Zhi.

**First: Changli Mountain Zhi**
Located ten *li* east and west of *Xian* County in Guanghan Commandery, one hundred fifty *li* from Chengdu, this was where Li Babai of Shu Commandery first studied the Dao. Babai, master of Tang Gongfang, wandered through the famous mountains of Shu, often appearing in the markets of Chengdu for amusement. At dusk, he would lodge on Mount Qingcheng, hence the name "Eight Hundred." To the south of the mountain lies a stone chamber, capable of holding eighty people, with three dragon gates as markers at its front. Corresponding to the Ox Mansion, initiated by the deluded, its governance endures for five hundred years.

**Second: Lishang Zhi**
Here, Master Jizi studied the Dao and ascended as a flying immortal. The *zhi* lies one hundred twenty *li* northeast of Yangquan County in Guanghan Commandery. The mountain has two stone chambers and a sacred well where white deer, white cranes, and white turtledoves come to drink. A stone stands before the *zhi*, connected to the Cimu Zhi. To the west flows the Red Stone Creek, with three pines as markers above. The mountain rises two thousand nine hundred *zhang* above the plain. In ancient times, Wei Shuqing of Zhongshan attained the Dao here. Corresponding to the Woman Mansion, initiated by the poor and lowly, its governance endures for a hundred years.

**Third: Yongquan Mountain Divine Zhi**
Here, Ma Mingsheng of Guanghan studied the Dao and attained immortality. The Most High Lord Lao transformed and dwelled here. The *zhi* lies within the boundaries of Xiaohan County in Suining Commandery, where a numinous spring heals all ailments of the people, its efficacy transmitted through generations as blessing water. Two hundred *li* from Chengdu, the mountain has a hundred-*zhang* cliff near Mian River, where monkeys, apes, and a hundred crows gather. Corresponding to the Void Mansion, initiated by the rustic, its governance endures for thirty years. The mountain is small yet lofty, with wandering paths on all four sides.

**Fourth: Chougeng Zhi**
Located in Nan’an County of Qianwei Commandery, one hundred ten *li* from Chengdu, nine *li* from the Min Mountain River. The mountain rises one thousand seven hundred *zhang* above the plain—this was where the Yellow Emperor studied the Dao. The *zhi* is flanked by continuous ridges; to the northwest flows the Wei River. The mountain also bears *zhi* herbs and medicines for cultivating life.

The *zhi* corresponds to the Rooftop Mansion, initiated by a nobleman, and its governance endured for fifty years.

**Fifth: Beiping Zhi**
Located in Nan’an County of Qianwei Commandery, one hundred forty *li* from Chengdu. The mountain bears a pool, two hundred *bu* in length and breadth, wherein grow divine *zhi* herbs and grasses. Those who consume them may endure as long as Heaven. In ancient times, Prince Qiao of Yue attained immortality here. The *zhi* corresponds to the House Mansion, initiated by a Daoist master, and its governance endured for forty years. It is also called □ Mountain *Zhi*.

**Sixth: Benzhu Zhi**
The mountain lies in Nan’an County of Qianwei Commandery, one hundred twenty-five *li* from Chengdu. Rising one thousand three hundred *zhang*, it holds a stream above, with fragrant forests along the *zhi*’s paths. To the north lies a dragon’s cave, its underground passage connecting to Mount Emei. Pines and cypresses grow atop, where Guo Zisheng once attained the Dao. Behind stand groves of bamboo, fifteen *li* west of which the *zhi* was hewn to link with Crane Cry Mountain. At the water’s end, divine dragons often sport within. The *zhi* corresponds to the Wall Mansion, initiated by an official of Dragon Gate, and its governance endured for five hundred years.

**Seventh: Mengqin Zhi**
The mountain stands west of Qiongdou County in Yuexi Commandery, twenty *li* from the city and one thousand four hundred twenty *li* from Chengdu. The *zhi* is separated from Yuexi Commandery by a river, with a small mountain before it and a great mountain behind, rising one thousand *zhang*. In ancient times, Yi Yin studied the Dao here on the northern mountain. Above grow *zhi* stalks and golden liquid grasses; consuming them grants transcendence of the world. Later, Zhao Sheng of Hanzhong Commandery resided here. The *zhi* corresponds to the Straddler Mansion, initiated by an ordinary person, and its governance endured for ninety years.

**Eighth: Pinggai Zhi**
The mountain lies in Wuyang County of Qianwei Commandery, eighty *li* from Chengdu. At the foot of the mountain stands a jade figure, thirteen *chi* in height. In ancient times, Cui Xiaotong of Wu Commandery studied the Dao here and attained flight as an immortal. To the west of the mountain flows the great river; to the south stretches a long ridge; to the north lies a level plain; and at its center stands the Dragon Gate. The *zhi* corresponds to the Bond Mansion, initiated by a woman of the hidden realm, and its governance endured for one thousand years.

On the seventh day of the first month in the second year of the Wu Shang era, Wuwei of the Great Dao and Mysterious Perfection established the eightfold *qi*-essential formulas of the lower *zhi*, held in the palm.

**First: Yuntai Mountain Zhi**
Located sixty *li* west of Langzhong County in Baxi Commandery, the mountain requires an eighteen-*li* ascent before reaching its summit, with its base one thousand three hundred seventy *li* from Chengdu. Celestial Master Zhang, leading three hundred seventy disciples, resided upon the *zhi* to teach and transform; after two years, they ascended to heaven in broad daylight. One year thereafter, the Celestial Master’s wife likewise ascended. Thirty years later, Zhao Sheng and Wang Chang again attained ascension in broad daylight. Before the *zhi* flows the great river of Baxi; upon the mountain grows a peach tree that blooms once every three years and bears fruit once every five, its branches spanning seven hundred *zhang* above a bottomless ravine. Only Zhao Sheng could cast himself forth to pluck its fruit; none others could retrieve it. The *zhi* corresponds to the Stomach Mansion, initiated by a master in human form, and its governance endured for fifty years.

It is also said that within Yuntai Zhi, jade maidens rode white cranes, immortals rode white deer, and celestial spirits came to welcome the Celestial Master’s ascension in broad daylight, witnessed by all the people. This is the Heavenly Pillar Mountain. Before Yuntai Zhi stands a pair of steles.

**Second: Jin Kou Zhi**
The mountain lies in Jiangyang County of Hanzhong Commandery, two thousand nine hundred twenty *li* from Chengdu. Chen Anshi studied the Dao upon this mountain and attained immortality. Anshi was a native of Jingzhao. The river of Hanzhong flows past its front; the mountain is also called Pingyuan Mountain. To the west stretches a long ridge; to the east lies the flowing sea; and the Azure Dragon Gate stands where emperors reside. The *zhi* corresponds to the Pleiades Mansion, initiated by a common person, and its governance endured for five hundred years.

**Third: Houcheng Zhi**
The mountain lies in Nanzheng County of Hanzhong Commandery. In ancient times, □ Ziran studied here and attained the immortal Dao. To its left flows a great river; behind it rise layered mountains.

The mountain bears divine *zhi* mushrooms; consuming them grants a lifespan of a thousand years. It is also called Mount Huangling. To its south stretches a long mountain range; to its north lies the Azure Dragon; and to its east, pines serve as its marker. The *zhi* corresponds to the Mansion of Net, initiated by an ordinary person, and its governance endured for eighty years.

**Fourth: Gongmu Zhi**
The mountain lies in Nanzheng County of Hanzhong Commandery, one hundred *li* from the *zhi*. In ancient times, Su Zi studied the Dao here and attained immortality. It is also called Mount Beifengxian. To its south lies a stone ravine; to its north, cascading waters flow. The *zhi* corresponds to the Beak of Turtle Mansion, initiated by an ailing person, and its governance endured for seventy years.

**Fifth: Pinggang Zhi**
The mountain lies in Nan’an County of Qianwei Commandery, one hundred *li* from Chengdu. In ancient times, Li A of Shu Commandery studied the Dao here and attained immortality, ascending to the heavens in broad daylight. The *zhi* corresponds to the Three Stars Mansion, initiated by a Daoist, and its governance endured for twenty years. To its north lie three layers of Caoxi; to its south, a mountain serves as its marker.

**Sixth: Zhubu Mountain Zhi**
The mountain lies within the borders of □dao County in Qianwei Commandery, one hundred fifty *li* from Chengdu. Wang Xing of Shu Commandery studied the Dao here and attained immortality. It is also called Mount Qiuchang. To its south stand stone chambers and jade halls; pines and cypresses grow before them. The *zhi* corresponds to the Bitter Mansion, initiated by a humble person, and its governance endured for eighty years?

**Seventh: Yuju Zhi**
Located two *li* to the left of the southern gate of Chengdu. On the seventh day of the first month in the first year of Yongshou, the Most High Lord Lao rode a white deer, and Celestial Master Zhang rode a white crane, arriving here to sit upon a jade bed with leg braces—hence the name Yuju Zhi. The *zhi* corresponds to the Ghost Mansion, initiated by a giant of a thousand *zhang*, and its governance endured for three generations.

**Eighth: Beimang Mountain Zhi**
The mountain lies in Chang’an County of Jingzhao Commandery. The Liang River flows to the left of the *zhi*; Wucheng Zi attained the Dao here. To the east of Mount Dahuang lies a cave spring; to the south, eastward-flowing waters. The *zhi* corresponds to the Willow Mansion, initiated by immortals and sages, and its governance endured for sixty years.

In the first year of Han’an, on the seventh day of the seventh month, the Celestial Master established the Four *Zhi* and entrusted them to his successor to align with the Twenty-Eight Mansions:
1. **Ganghu Zhi**, on Mount Lanwu, corresponding to the Star Mansion.
2. **Baishi Zhi**, on Mount Xuanji, corresponding to the Spread Mansion.
3. **Jushan Zhi**, on Mount Fanyang, corresponding to the Wings Mansion.
4. **Zhongmao Zhi**, on Mount Yuandong, corresponding to the Chariot Mansion.

In the third year of Jian’an, on the fifth day of the tenth month, the successor established the Eight Passes to correspond with the *Zhi*:
- **Liyuan Zhi**, on Mount Xuanchang.
- **Lili Zhi**, on Mount Gaotang.

Pinggong Zhi, on Oxhead Mountain. Gongmu Zhi, on Shenxiong Mountain. Tiantai Zhi, on Yellow Ox Mountain. Laixiang Zhi, on Lesser World Mountain. Zunling Zhi, on Danfang Mountain. Daiyuan Zhi, on Upper Hall Mountain.

In the second year of Taiyuan, on the seventh day of the first month, the Successor Master established the Eight Graded Wandering *Zhi*:
- **Emei Zhi**, within the borders of Shu Commandery.
- **Qingcheng Zhi**, within the borders of Shu Commandery.
- **Taihua Zhi**, within the borders of Jingzhao Commandery.
- **Huangjin Zhi**, within the borders of Shu Commandery.
- **Cimu Zhi**, within the borders of Chengbu Mountain.
- **Hefeng Zhi**, within the borders of Shangdang Commandery.
- **Pingdu Zhi**, within the borders of Ba Commandery.
- **Jiyang Zhi**.

The Successor Master was the son of the former Successor Master, named Lu, who attained the immortal Dao of *shijie* (corpse liberation) on Yangping Mountain. Each person established one *Zhi*, called the Successor Master’s *Zhi*. However, the Successor Master’s *Zhi* and the Chief Clerk both belonged to the Celestial Master’s lineage, and thus another *Zhi* was established.

Now, according to the *Statutes on Offices and Governance of the Mysterious Capital, Chapter Nine*: Daiyuan Zhi and Pingdu Zhi are external wandering *Zhi*. From this, it is known that Emei Zhi and the others are also wandering *Zhi*.

**Twenty-Four Qi Grades**
According to the *Statutes on the Opening of the Mysterious Capital*: The twenty-four *qi* serve as celestial emissaries. Each *qi* spans fifteen days; a year has twelve months, with two *qi* per month, totaling twenty-four *qi* in a year—all are natural *qi*.

The *Scripture of the Cavernous Mystery* states: The Three Origins are established by three *qi*. The Three Heavens are: the Beginning *Qi* as the Heaven of Pure Tenuity, the Original *Qi* as the Heaven of Yu the Great’s Remnant, and the Mysterious *Qi* as the Heaven of Great Redness.

The *Upper Gate of Mastery by Song Wenming* states: Lesser Yin, Greater Yin, Lesser Yang, Greater Yang, and the Central Harmonizing *Qi* combine to form the Five *Qi*. These Five *Qi*, together with the earlier Mysterious, Original, and Beginning *Qi*, complete the number eight, as the *Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: "Each of the Three Origins has eight, totaling twenty-four *qi*, from which the species and clans of living beings arise."

This *qi* disperses into clouds and mist, coalesces into forms and shadows, emerges as differentiation, and enters as the True One. Its root is called the *qi* of the Primordial Beginning and Great Brahmā, which divides into three to form the Upper Three Heavens.

As the *Hidden Instructions on Ascending Perfection: Exegesis on Times and Days* states: The twenty-four *qi* are: Beginning of Spring, Rain Water, Waking of Insects, Spring Equinox, Pure Brightness, Grain Rain, Beginning of Summer, Lesser Fullness, Grain in Ear, Summer Solstice, Lesser Heat, Greater Heat, Beginning of Autumn, Limit of Heat, White Dew, Autumn Equinox, Cold Dew, Frost’s Descent, Beginning of Winter, Lesser Snow, Greater Snow, Winter Solstice, Lesser Cold, and Greater Cold—these constitute the twenty-four *qi*.

The *Fifth Declaration of Perfection* states: The Eastern Azure Heaven of Nine *Qi*, the Southern Cinnabar Heaven where Three *Qi* flow in essence, the Western Heaven of Seven *Qi*, and the Northern Mysterious Heaven where Five *Qi* circulate—these also combine into twenty-four *qi*. As for the Center, it is said: The Central Yellow Center governs the *qi*, presiding over the Mysterious and True, unconcerned with *qi* numbers, as it governs the twenty-four *qi* of the four directions.

The *Scripture of the Arrayed Records of the Lords of the Three Heavens of Supreme Purity* states: Where *qi* resides, it follows where the spirit is born. Where the spirit is, *qi* is; where the spirit departs, *qi* departs. *Qi* is the upright *qi* of the twenty-four spirits. When dispersed, it scatters into clouds and mist; when coalesced, it forms shapes and shadows. When emitted, it becomes immortal transformation; when absorbed, it becomes the True One. Above, it binds the Three Origins; below, it binds the myriad things. In stillness, it serves as the omen of the body; in motion, it serves as the omen of the spirit.

**Three Divisions and Eight Effulgences of the Twenty-Four Spirits**
From the *Inner Instructions of the Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected of Supreme Purity*, already recorded in the previous *Eighth Category: The Eight Effulgences*—not repeated here.

**Twenty-Four Hells**
According to the *Middle Scroll of the Regulations of the Great Perfected*: Beneath the Wanyuan Heaven lies Mount Fengdu in the north, in the *gui* region. On the mountain are eight hells governing the Upper Three Offices:
1. **Heaven-Monitoring Hell**
2. **Heaven-Pacifying Hell**
3. **Void Hell**
4. **Natural Hell**
5. **Ninefold Pacification Hell**
6. **Pure Edict Hell**
7. **Heavenly Mysterious Hell**
8. **Original Rectification Hell**

At the center are eight hells governing the Middle Three Offices:
1. **Mysterious Sands Northern Hell**
2. **August Heaven Hell**
3. **Prohibition and Punishment Hell**
4. **Mysterious Sands Hell**
5. **Form Rectification Hell**
6. **Statutes and Ordinances Hell**
7. **Nine Heavens Hell**
8. **Pure Cold Hell**

Beneath the mountain are eight hells governing the Lower Three Offices:
1. **Boundless Hell**
2. **Great Perfected Hell**
3. **Mysterious Capital Hell**
4. **Forty-Nine Hells**
5. **Heavenly One Northern Hell**
6. **River Earl Hell**
7. **Accumulated Kalpas Hell**
8. **Female Perfected Hell**

The twenty-four hells each have twelve subordinate officials: golden-headed, iron-faced, colossal celestial enforcers, totaling 2,400 per hell, wielding golden hammers and iron staves to govern the punishment of sinful souls according to the dark statutes.

**Twenty-Four Offices**
According to the *Statutes on Offices and Governance of the Mysterious Capital, Rising Tone, Chapter Nine*:
- **Heaven-Monitoring Office**: Oversees the monitoring of chaos and the rectification of deviance.
- **Governance-Supervising Office**: Oversees the supervision of all *Zhi*, the conduct of Orthodox Unity Masters, and the investigation of greed, corruption, or violations of master’s laws.
- **Qi-Offering Office**: Oversees the selection of male and female officials, the examination of Orthodox Unity Masters’ bodies for scars, deformities, or disabilities, ensuring they are upright and unadorned.
- **Great Capital Attack Office**: Oversees the world’s encampments, talismanic temples, the Qin, Hu, Qiang, Man, Rong, Di, Chu, and Yue peoples—any who attack without righteous *qi*, evil persons, or rebellious ghosts—all must be clearly investigated and recorded.
- **Merit-Directing Office**: Oversees the merits and rewards of the world’s Five Directions, Four Seas, Eight Extremities, Twelve Provinces, One Hundred Twenty Commanderies, One Thousand Two Hundred Counties, Twelve Thousand Townships, and market towns; encampments of sand and stone; the Five Peaks and Four Waterways; and the merits of mountain and river spirits. Upright talismans and punitive killings of the myriad ghosts must all be settled.

**Capital Merit Office**: Oversees merits and labors, records officials and common folk, manages charitable contributions of grain and wealth, gold, silver, jade, silk, the six livestock, rice, and goods; regulates receipts, disbursements, and the keys to granaries and treasuries; governs the property of ghosts and spirits, rituals and trustworthiness, the construction of halls and dwellings, bridges, roads, towers, pavilions, and spirit chambers—all fall under its authority.

**Spirit-Directing Office**: Oversees the selection of the worthy and good, the demotion and removal of the false and evil; convenes assemblies of all *qi*; and governs all violations and transgressions.

**Spirit-Monitoring Office**: Oversees the investigation of past offenses, compiles written records, examines advantages and harms, restrains errors and delusions, and transforms through admonitions and commands.

**Bureau-Directing Office**: Oversees the selection and appointment of the twenty-four offices, their merit registers, and all official documents; arranges them in order and submits them to the register of destinies.

**Qi-Inspecting Office**: Oversees the inspection of all *qi* across the Four Directions and their auspicious signs and responses.

**Qi-Balancing Office**: Oversees the assessment of the world’s *qi*, ensuring balance across the Four Directions and Eight Extremities, governing their climates.

**Upper Qi Office**: Oversees the collection of the myriad ghosts, distinguishing upright *qi* from deviant spirits.

**Capital Qi Office**: Oversees the triennial assemblies of officials and commoners seeking governance and salvation; distinguishes by age, commandery, county, township, and village; and records the titles they receive.

**Dignity and Ritual Office**: Oversees the instruction and enforcement of ritual systems, attire, demeanor, regulations, and hierarchical order; corrects deviations and upholds right and wrong; and implements laws and rites.

**Qi-Directing Office**: Oversees the five-colored *qi*, discerns their transformations and climatic anomalies, and concurrently oversees the *Qi*-Knowing Office. *(One version omits the Qi-Directing Office.)*

**Judgment-Directing Office**: Oversees ghostly *qi*, the transmission of teachings through possessed men and women, and distinguishes the authenticity of the Qin, Yi, Hu, Rong, Di, and Qiang peoples.

**Four Qi Office**: Oversees the submission of petitions, written documents, and assemblies in all governance halls; manages household registers and population counts; and records births and deaths.

**Spirit-Executing Office**: Oversees the dissemination of *qi* and the proclamation of transformations, making the Daoist teachings manifest.

**Dao Qi Office**: Oversees the exhortation of the rebellious and the transformation of evil into good.

**Sage Qi Office**: Oversees the verification of documents, the annual assessment of merits, and the submission of reports and petitions.

**Qi-Receiving Office**: Oversees the receipt of governance and medical treatments, recording their merits.

**Qi-Administering Office**: Oversees the administration of all offices, their ranks, and hierarchical order.

**Integrity and Equity Office**: Oversees the supervision of integrity and the correction of deviations, ensuring equitable distribution of food and drink.

**Teaching-Executing Office**: Oversees the proclamation of the Master’s teachings and the exhortation of the ignorant and lawless.

**Righteousness-Establishing Office**: Oversees the commendation of meritorious deeds, aiding the times, and the timely advancement or retirement of officials.

As stated in *The Statutes on Petitions, Scroll Thirteen*: "The twenty-four offices of male and female officials are precisely these."

---

**Twenty-Four Earthly Responses**
As recorded in *The Scripture of Myriad Chapters*: When the Primordial Beginning unfolded the chart, the earth emitted twenty-four responses, rejoicing the divine perfected.

1. At that time, the primordial heavens were in chaos, devoid of light. The morning cock heralded dawn, the Four Sceneries grew bright and clear, the Dark Heavens unfurled, and the earth expanded, giving rise to the Five Phases.
2. For thirty-six thousand days and nights, the earth below shared the same radiance, illuminating even the darkest nights with boundless brilliance.
3. The Azure Bird bore a missive to inform the Five Thearchs, rectifying the heavens’ divisions and degrees.
4. The White Tiger spat forth gold, pacifying and securing the Jade Spirits.
5. The Azure Dragon presented talismans to inform the Water Thearch, regulating and hastening the cycles, opening the rivers and seas.
6. The Jade Phoenix bore the imperial seal to offer to the Thearchs and Kings, securing the state and preserving the mandate, ensuring the Five Marchmounts endure forever.
7. The startling phoenix sang in unison, their soaring cries resonant and clear.
8. Flocks of birds danced in flight, rejoicing at the heavens’ edge.
9. Dragons leapt and frolicked, stirring the deep abysses and marshes.
10. The Yellow River’s waters flowed smoothly, fish scales interlacing in harmony.
11. Sweet dew arose spontaneously, and lingzhi mushrooms flourished in abundance.
12. Winter brought no frost or ice, and withered trees bloomed anew.
13. Forests, trees, and crops bore flowers and fruit in both winter and summer, lush and thriving, untouched by decay or harm.
14. The Four *Qi* harmonized, calamities and epidemics ceased, heaven and humanity rejoiced, and none met untimely deaths.
15. Venomous creatures sealed their fangs, harboring no harmful intent.
16. Lions and fierce beasts dwelled alongside humans as neighbors.
17. Across the world, the blind, deaf, lame, and infirm regained their forms, free from illness or injury, all restored to health and strength.
18. The aged reverted to youth, the young never aged, their countenances resplendent, their spirits radiant and bright.
19. Birds, beasts, and the six livestock, whether pregnant or bearing young, all gave birth safely, untouched by harm.
20. Pregnant women across the world bore sons.
21. The earth’s treasures were revealed, gold and jade exposed, scattered across the roads, with none hidden in obscurity.
22. The heavens trembled and the earth split, dry bones revived, sunken corpses and wandering souls arose as whole beings; the world sang in celebration, rejoicing in the Great Peace.
23. The earth sprouted lotus flowers, and heaven and humanity praised and rejoiced, all exultant.
24. The Five Peaks opened their caverns, talismanic scriptures emerged in unison, teaching and guiding heaven and humanity. At that time, all learners became flying immortals.

---

**Twenty-Four Perfected Charts**
As recorded in *The Scripture of the Five Invocations, Upper Scroll*: To seek the Daoist methods, first bathe and cleanse away filth and stench, and one shall obtain the *Eastern Well Chart*.

**Twenty-Five Natured Colors**
As recorded in *The Central Scroll of the Left Mysteries, Ninth Chapter*: The eyes perceive the five colors, the ears hear the five sounds, the nose smells the five fragrances, the tongue tastes the five flavors, and the body senses the five touches.
The *Thirteenth Chapter* states: Fragrances refer to rank, scorched, fishy, rotten, and aromatic; touches refer to hard, soft, cold, hot, and neutral—all are knowable.
The *Thirteenth Chapter* further states: Possessing these five sets of five—twenty-five natured colors—constitutes the small life of the ordinary person.

**Twenty-Seven Gates of the Dharma, Names and Numbers**
Twenty-seven ranks of immortals, perfected, and sages; twenty-seven great men; twenty-seven heavenly beings within the human body; twenty-seven life-*qi* lords.

**The Twenty-Seven Ranks of Immortals, Perfected, and Sages**

As recorded in *The Comprehensive Gate of Song Wenming*: the highest rank is called *sage*, the middle rank *perfected*, and the lowest rank *immortal*. The *sage* rank further divides into three, the *perfected* rank into three, and the *immortal* rank into three, totaling nine ranks. Each of these nine ranks again divides into three, making twenty-seven ranks in all.

*The Profound Meaning of Dao and Virtue by Song Wenming* further cites *The Eight Simplicities Scripture*: the highest *perfected* are attended by two thousand jade boys and jade maidens, the middle *perfected* by one thousand, and the lowest *perfected* by five hundred. *The Ninefold Return to the Primal Simplicities Scripture* likewise distinguishes ranks.

*The Great Cavern Scripture* states: from life one attains the Dao, from the Dao one attains immortality, from immortality one attains *perfected* status, and from *perfected* status one attains *Upper Clarity*. The Yellow and Lao Lords are *upper immortals*, having mastered the Dao of the *upper immortals* but not yet attained the *upper perfected*.

In Buddhism, those who achieve the four fruits are called *worthy sages*; upon attaining Buddhahood and the Dao, they are styled *great immortals*. When the Dao is complete, they ascend from the beginning of flight to the *Great Ultimate*, and upon achieving the *Supreme Realm*, they are called *lofty immortals*.

The heterodox teachings speak of transforming the spirit into a wondrous form, where the hun-soul becomes the spirit of the body, and when unified, it becomes the *true body* and attains the Dao.

*The Thirteenth Chapter of Discourses on the Mysterious Gate*, in its section on *Positions and Karma*, states: beyond the realms, there are three nines—twenty-seven ranks—known as the names of *worthy sages*.

*The Regulations of the Supreme Perfected* states: the *Lesser Vehicle* of immortals has nine ranks: (1) *upper immortal*, (2) *lofty immortal*, (3) *great immortal*, (4) *spirit immortal*, (5) *mysterious immortal*, (6) *true immortal*, (7) *heavenly immortal*, (8) *numinous immortal*, and (9) *ultimate immortal*. The *Middle Vehicle* of the *perfected* has nine ranks: (1) *upper perfected*, (2) *lofty perfected*, (3) *great perfected*, (4) *spirit perfected*, (5) *mysterious perfected*, (6) *immortal perfected*, (7) *heavenly perfected*, (8) *numinous perfected*, and (9) *ultimate perfected*. The *Great Vehicle* of *sages* has nine ranks: (1) *upper sage*, (2) *lofty sage*, (3) *great sage*, (4) *spirit sage*, (5) *mysterious sage*, (6) *true sage*, (7) *immortal sage*, (8) *numinous sage*, and (9) *ultimate sage*.

Though the three nines differ, all are free from desire and engage in contemplation. The object of contemplation is not without distinction, hence the differences among *immortals*, *perfected*, and *sages*. The *upper sage*, *lofty sage*, and *great sage* are the highest ranks of *sages*; the *spirit sage*, *mysterious sage*, and *true sage* are the middle ranks; and the *immortal sage*, *numinous sage*, and *ultimate sage* are the lowest ranks. The ranks of *sages* being thus, those of *immortals* and *perfected* may be inferred. These three nines of people, when viewed in relation to the realms within, constitute the *Great Vehicle*.

**The Twenty-Seven Great Men**

As recorded in *The Regulations of the Supreme Perfected*: the twenty-seven great men correspond to the nine ranks each of *sages*, *perfected*, and *immortals*, totaling three nines—twenty-seven. They align with the celestial lodges, where the twenty-eight lunar mansions omit one, as one is hidden.

**The Twenty-Seven Heavens**

These have already been recorded in the sections on the *Three Names and Numbers*, *Three Qi*, and *Three Heavens*.

**The Twenty-Seven Lords of Life-*Qi* Within the Human Body**

As recorded in *The Scripture of Laozi’s Pillow for Opening the Gate*: within the human body are twenty-seven lords of life-*qi*: the hair is the *Azure City Lord*, the head the *Three Terraces Lord*, the eyebrows the *Eight Poles Lord*, the left eye the *Gazing Clarity Lord*, the right eye the *Mysterious Clarity Lord*, the left ear the *Hearing Clarity Lord*, the right ear the *Decisive Clarity Lord*, the nose the *Lord of the Wondrous Gate of the Celestial Circuit*, the mouth the *Jade Gate Lord*, the lips the *Jade Portal Lord*, the teeth the *Twenty-Eight Primordial Officers Lord*, the tongue the *Limitless Lord*, the throat the *Colonel Lord*, the larynx the *Nine Ministers Lord*, the liver the *Crimson Palace Lord*, the lungs the *Floral Canopy Lord*, the gallbladder the *Longevity Lord*, the heart the *Cinnabar Field Lord*, the navel the *Purple-White Lord*, the stomach the *Great Granary Lord*, the spleen the *Yellow Court Lord*, the left kidney the *Mysterious Wondrous Lord*, the right kidney the *Primal Upright Lord*, the large intestine the *Nourishing Mother Lord*, the small intestine the *Dao-Conducting Lord*, the intestines the *Guardian of the Dao Lord*, the *Triple Burner* the *Mysterious Foremost Lord*, the left thigh the *Small Chariot Lord*, the right thigh the *Wandering Lord*, the left foot the *Thunder and Lightning Lord*, and the right foot the *Cloud and Qi Lord*. These twenty-seven lords of life-*qi* should always remain concealed within the body’s armor; they must not be recklessly revealed.

If counted in detail, there are thirty-one lords, but the specifics are unclear.

The Twenty-Eight Methods of the Central Gates, Each with Its Own Categories

The twenty-eight constellations, as recorded in *The Thirty-Two Heavenly Fast Rites of the Three Sovereigns*, are as follows: the northern quadrant comprises Dongbi, Yingshi, Wei, Xu, Xunu, Qianniu, and Nandou; the eastern quadrant comprises Ji, Wei, Xin, Fang, Di, Kang, and Jiao; the southern quadrant comprises Zhen, Yi, Zhang, Xing, Liu, Gui, and Jing; the western quadrant comprises Shen, Zi, Bi, Mao, Wei, Lou, and Kui. Each quadrant contains seven, totaling twenty-eight.

When one observes the fast of the Three Sovereigns, one invokes the twenty-eight constellations to dissolve the celestial nets and terrestrial webs, to alleviate karmic retribution, and to prolong life.

*The Rites of the Five Tombs Offering* states: the seven constellations of the eastern quadrant are Jiao, Kang, Di, Fang, Xin, Wei, and Ji; the seven constellations of the southern quadrant are Jing, Gui, Liu, Xing, Zhang, Yi, and Zhen; the seven constellations of the western quadrant are Kui, Lou, Wei, Mao, Bi, Zi, and Shen; the seven constellations of the northern quadrant are Dou, Niu, Nü, Xu, Wei, Shi, and Bi. For households with curses or entanglements spanning forty-six generations, these twenty-eight constellations possess the power to resolve and disperse them.

*The Scripture of Stellar Liberation* states: the eastern constellation Jiao is named Lord Di; Kang, Lord Ming; Di, Lord Shang; Fang, Lord Zhen; Xin, Lord Zheng; Wei, Lord Li; Ji, Lord Chang. The northern constellation Dou is named Lord Zi; Niu, Lord Ju; Nü, Lord Chen; Xu, Lord Tong; Wei, Lord Can; Shi, Lord Wang; Bi, Lord Ying. The western constellation Kui is named Lord Shi; Lou, Lord Li; Wei, Lord Ming; Mao, Lord Yu; Bi, Lord Jin; Zi, Lord Ming; Shen, Lord Cheng. The southern constellation Jing is named Lord Jie; Gui, Lord Ju; Liu, Lord Qian; Xing, Lord Ming; Zhang, Lord Fu; Yi, Lord Xin; Zhen, Lord Qian. All these constellations can transmit and deliver the deceased, preventing them from entangling future generations. The names of these constellations were also listed among the twenty-four sacred mountains in the preceding text.

The Thirty-Two Methods of the Central Gates, with Their Names and Categories

The thirty-two heavens, as recorded in *The Scripture of Limitless Salvation* and *The Inner Sounds of Jade Characters Below*, are as follows:

1. **Taihuang Huangzeng Heaven**, separated from Taiming Yuwan Heaven by ninety-nine myriad and nine thousand *qi*. Modern exegesis states that one *qi* comprises ninety-nine thousand nine hundred and ninety layers.
2. **Taiming Yuwan Heaven**, separated from Hetong Heaven by eighty myriad *qi*.
3. **Qingming Hetong Heaven**, separated from Pingyu Heaven by seventy myriad *qi*.
4. **Xuantai Pingyu Heaven**, separated from Wenju Heaven by sixty myriad *qi*.
5. **Yuanming Wenju Heaven**, separated from Moyi Jue Heaven by fifty myriad *qi*.
6. **Shangming Qiyao Moyi Heaven**, separated from Yueheng Heaven by forty myriad *qi*.

*The Central Scroll of the Supreme Perfection Regulations* states: these are the heavens of the Desire Realm, where yin and yang commingle, beings are born of wombs, and lifespans accumulate to ten thousand years.

*The Profound Meaning* states: those who uphold the ten precepts and purify their verbal karma ascend to the Desire Realm; those who purify their physical karma ascend to the Form Realm; those who purify their mental karma ascend to the Formless Realm; those who enter the nine grades of practice ascend to the Heaven of Seed People. These ranks were previously recorded in the "Three Categories of Names and Numbers" under the section on the three karmas.

*The Inner Sounds* states:
7. **Xuwu Yueheng Heaven**, separated from Mengyi Heaven by thirty myriad *qi*.
8. **Taiji Mengyi Heaven**, separated from Heyang Heaven by twenty myriad *qi*.

These eight heavens belong to the eastern quadrant, governed by the Qi of Beginning Azure.

9. **Chiming Heyang Heaven**, separated from Gonghua Heaven by ninety million *qi*.
10. **Xuanming Gonghua Heaven**, separated from Zongpiao Heaven by eighty million *qi*.
11. **Yaoming Zongpiao Heaven**, separated from Huangjia Heaven by seventy million *qi*.
12. **Zhuluo Huangjia Heaven**, separated from Tangyao Heaven by sixty million *qi*.
13. **Xuming Tangyao Heaven**, separated from Duanjing Heaven by fifty million *qi*.
14. **Guanming Duanjing Heaven**, separated from Gongqing Heaven by forty million *qi*.
15. **Xuanming Gongqing Heaven**, separated from Jiyao Heaven by thirty million *qi*.
16. **Taihuan Jiyao Heaven**, separated from Kongsheng Heaven by twenty million *qi*.

These eight heavens belong to the southern quadrant, governed by the Crimson Heaven.

17. **Yuanzai Kongsheng Heaven**, separated from Huangya Heaven by nine million *qi*.
18. **Tai’an Huangya Heaven**, separated from Jifeng Heaven by eight million *qi*.
19. **Xianding Jifeng Heaven**, separated from Xiaomang Heaven by seven million *qi*.
20. **Shihuang Xiaomang Heaven**, separated from Wengchong Heaven by six million *qi*.
21. **Dahuang Fangchong Heaven**, separated from Jiangyou Heaven by five million *qi*.
22. **Wusi Jiangyou Heaven**, separated from Ruanle Heaven by four million *qi*.
23. **Shangdie Ruanle Heaven**, separated from Tanshi Heaven by three million *qi*.
24. **Wuji Tanshi Heaven**, separated from Xiaodu Heaven by two million *qi*.

These eight heavens belong to the western quadrant, governed by the White Heaven.

25. **Haoting Xiaodu Heaven**, separated from Yuandong Heaven by ninety-nine thousand *qi*.
26. **Yuantong Yuandong Heaven**, separated from Miaocheng Heaven by eighty-eight thousand *qi*.
27. **Hanchong Miaocheng Heaven**, separated from Jinshang Heaven by seventy-seven thousand *qi*.

*The Central Scroll of the Supreme Perfection Regulations* states: these eighteen heavens constitute the Form Realm, akin to the Desire Realm. Though yin and yang possess form, they do not commingle; beings are born through transformation, partake of fragrant essences, and do not excrete waste. Their lifespans accumulate to billions of years, free from premature death or harm.

28. **Xiule Jin Shang Heaven**, separated from Changrong Heaven by sixty-six thousand *qi*.
29. **Wushang Changrong Heaven**, separated from Yuji Heaven by fifty-five thousand *qi*.

30. **Yulong Tengsheng Heaven**, separated from Fandu Heaven by forty-four thousand *qi*.
31. **Longbian Fandu Heaven**, separated from Jiayi Heaven by thirty-three thousand *qi*.
32. **Pingyu Jiayi Heaven**, separated from the *qi* of Brahmā-conduct by twelve thousand *qi*.

The *qi* divisions of these eight heavens belong to the Dark Heaven of the North.

*The Central Scroll of the Supreme Perfection Regulations* states: these constitute the Four Kinds of Human Heavens, where those who study the Dao may become seeds of humanity. The Queen Mother welcomes them. Those who ascend to the upper four heavens are called *Brahmā-conduct*; though perilous, they do not fail. They pacify all kinds of people, do not fall into the Three Wretched Realms, and may roam the Three Clarities.

As the *Sutra of Karmic Retribution* truly expounds, this has already been recorded in the previous section on the four kinds of human and heavenly beings, as well as in the section on the names of the Three Realms. If divided by the four directions, each direction has eight heavens, and four times eight makes thirty-two heavens. If divided by the Three Realms, it follows the arrangement below.

Song Wenming’s *Profound Meaning of the Dao and Its Virtue* states that these thirty-two heavens specifically govern the fruits of fortune, differing from the Nine Heavens and the Thirty-Six Heavens. The fruits of fortune arise from karmic actions, and karmic actions originate from the six roots: eye, ear, nose, mouth, body, and mind. If the mouth’s karma can subdue the body and mind, one ascends to the six heavens of the Desire Realm in accordance with merit. The six heavens are from Taihuang Heaven to Shangming Heaven.

Among the six roots, some still engage with sensory objects, some are conditioned by objects but do not engage, and some gradually no longer condition or engage—altogether three kinds. Three times six makes eighteen, thus giving rise to the eighteen heavens of the Form Realm. The eighteen heavens are from Xuwu Yueheng Heaven to Wuji Tanshi Heaven. When the six roots no longer condition or engage at all, one is born in the four heavens of the Formless Realm. The four heavens are from Haoting Heaven to Xiule Heaven. The reason there are only four heavens is that the six roots are all purified, leaving only benevolence, righteousness, propriety, and wisdom—hence four heavens. Those who have faith belong to the realm of the Dao and are not born in the Three Realms.

Altogether, these twenty-eight heavens constitute the Three Realms. Though subdued, if not severed, residual habits remain, and thoughts are not forgotten; thus, one does not attain eternal existence and still resides in the Three Realms. When lifespan ends, one perishes and follows the path of their actions.

From Changrong Heaven to Jiayi Heaven are four heavens, called the Four Palaces of Donghua, Nanji, Xiling, and Beizhen. They penetrate the realm of the Dao and serve as the heavens of the seeds of the world. Below, they follow the kalpic destruction, combining with the previous twenty-eight heavens to make thirty-two heavens.

*Profound Meaning, Lower Scroll* further queries: the Five Virtues of the Supreme One all reside in one division, yet only faith is said to belong to the Dao and not be born in the Three Realms—is this not contradictory? The answer is: the Five Virtues all belong to the Supreme One. Saying that faith belongs to the Dao and does not condition the Three Realms does not mean the other four virtues do not belong to the Dao. It simply means that through conditioning the Three Realms, one ascends and transcends. Faith does not condition the Three Realms because, as the scripture states: "Its essence is most true, and within it is faith." The hidden commentary says: studying the Dao depends on cinnabar faith; faith is the foundation of practice, leading directly to the Three Clarities. Benevolence, righteousness, propriety, and wisdom are the virtues of the Dao. They arise in sequence, no different from the Great Precepts. When all Five Virtues are complete, wisdom alone is singled out for praise. Speaking comprehensively, the Five Virtues are all the Dao.

The *Treasure Mystery Sutra* also states: "The highest virtue is equal to Heaven and returns to unite with the Dao." Speaking separately, faith alone belongs to the Dao, while the other four belong to virtue—no difference. The *Book of Changes* says: "The Way of Heaven is called yin and yang; the Way of Earth is called soft and hard." Yet it also says: "Heaven is yang, Earth is yin; Qian is hard, Kun is soft." The *Jade Explanation* states: "Without the Numinous Treasure, Heaven cannot be born; without the Numinous Treasure, Earth cannot be completed." Yet it also says: "Above, establishing Heaven and Earth is called *ling*; below, stabilizing the Five Peaks is called *bao*." And again: "In Heaven it is called *ling*; on Earth it is called *bao*." Such examples of synthesis and separation, unity and distinction, are many. If one’s mind is sunk in oblivion, it may not seem contradictory.

Song Wenming’s *Miscellaneous Questions on the Numinous Treasure* states: the Three Realms and thirty-two heavens, according to the *Inner Sound of the Numinous Treasure*, are arranged in the four directions. The *Sutra of Resolute Mind and Its Diagram* presents them as three layers. Yet the present commentary explains them as ascending like a ram’s horns—contradicting both. Why? The answer is: this is how both can be reconciled. The ram’s horns follow Zhuangzi’s meaning. The *Ritual of the Grand Ultimate Perfected* by Fuzhai says: Zhuangzi was the Immortal of Nanhua, so his analogy of ram’s horns can be trusted. Like the intestines’ winding path, it spirals upward. The higher it turns, the loftier it becomes—this is layering, and it also encompasses the four directions.

The *Discourse on the Mysterious Gate, Scroll 20* states: the Thirty-Six Heavens are still the wondrous realm of the Three Clarities. Though their positions lie beyond the realms, their transformations are unfathomable. In small measure, they enter the Three Palaces; in great measure, they transcend the Six Directions. All are the divisions of the sagely response, opening and guiding, transforming and receiving. Speaking of this *qi*, it is neither yin nor yang—profoundly transcendent and pure.

Below this, following the *Numinous Treasure Sutra*, the thirty-two heavens are used to illustrate the Three Realms. Thus, the *Sutra of Salvation* says: "The primordial net flows forth through the thirty-two heavens." These thirty-two heavens all reside in the Void, revolving through the ten directions, rising from the northeast on the whirlwind terrace like ram’s horns. Now, according to the *Sutra of the Original Source*, the directional correspondences are as follows:

1. The *qi* of **Taihuang Huangzeng Heaven**, belonging to the northwest, is the *qi* of Brahmā.
2. The *qi* of **Taiming Yuwan Heaven**, belonging to the Eastern Wall constellation.

Third, the *qi* of **Qingming Hetong Heaven**, belonging to the Encampment Mansion.
Fourth, the *qi* of **Xuantai Pingyu Heaven**, belonging to the Rooftop Mansion.
Fifth, the *qi* of **Yuanming Wenju Heaven**, belonging to the Emptiness Mansion.
Sixth, the *qi* of **Shangming Qiyao Heaven**, belonging to the Woman Mansion.
Seventh, the *qi* of **Xuwu Yueheng Heaven**, belonging to the Ox Mansion.
Eighth, the *qi* of **Taiji Mengyi Heaven**, belonging to the Dipper Mansion.

The above eight heavens reside in the eastern direction, corresponding to the Wood number. Their resonant tone is nine, thus collectively termed the "Nine *Qi*"—the azure *qi* associated with the seven northern mansions.

Ninth, the *qi* of **Chiming Heyang Heaven**, belonging to the northeast, the *qi* of Brahmā.
Tenth, **Xuanming Gonghua Heaven**, belonging to the Winnowing Basket Mansion.
Eleventh, **Yaoming Zongpiao Heaven**, belonging to the Tail Mansion.
Twelfth, **Zhuluo Huangjia Heaven**, belonging to the Heart Mansion.
Thirteenth, **Xuming Tangyao Heaven**, belonging to the Chamber Mansion.
Fourteenth, **Guanming Duanjing Heaven**, belonging to the Base Mansion.
Fifteenth, **Xuanming Gongqing Heaven**, belonging to the Neck Mansion.
Sixteenth, **Taihuan Jiyao Heaven**, belonging to the Horn Mansion.

The above eight heavens reside in the southern direction, corresponding to the Fire number. Their resonant tone is three, thus collectively termed the "Three *Qi* of the Cinnabar Heaven"—associated with the seven eastern mansions.

Seventeenth, the *qi* of **Yuanzai Kongsheng Heaven**, belonging to the southeast, the *qi* of Brahmā.
Eighteenth, **Tai’an Huangya Heaven**, belonging to the Axletree Mansion.
Nineteenth, **Xianding Jifeng Heaven**, belonging to the Wings Mansion.
Twentieth, **Shihuang Xiaomang Heaven**, belonging to the Spread Net Mansion.
Twenty-first, **Taihuang Wengchong Futong Heaven**, belonging to the Star Mansion.
Twenty-second, **Wusi Jiangyou Heaven**, belonging to the Willow Mansion.
Twenty-third, **Shangdie Ruanle Heaven**, belonging to the Ghost Mansion.
Twenty-fourth, **Wuji Tanshi Heaven**, belonging to the Well Mansion.

The above eight heavens reside in the western direction, corresponding to the Metal number. Their resonant tone is seven, thus collectively termed the "Seven *Qi* of the White Heaven"—associated with the seven southern mansions.

Twenty-fifth, the *qi* of **Haoting Xiaodu Heaven**, belonging to the southwest, the *qi* of Brahmā.
Twenty-sixth, **Yuantong Yuandong Heaven**, belonging to the Three Stars Mansion.
Twenty-seventh, **Taiwen Hanchong Miaocheng Heaven**, belonging to the Turtle Beak Mansion.
Twenty-eighth, **Taisu Xiule Jin Shangtian**, belonging to the Net Mansion.
Twenty-ninth, **Taixu Wushang Changrong Heaven**, belonging to the Triaster Mansion.
Thirtieth, **Taishi Yulong Tengsheng Heaven**, belonging to the Stomach Mansion.
Thirty-first, **Longbian Fandu Heaven**, belonging to the Bond Mansion.
Thirty-second, **Taiji Pingyu Jiayi Heaven**, belonging to the Straddling Mansion.

The above eight heavens reside in the northern direction, corresponding to the Water number. Their resonant tone is five, thus collectively termed the "Five *Qi* of the Mysterious Heaven." The central direction corresponds to the Earth number, with a resonant tone of one, which unifies the four directions—hence no separate placement is made. Moreover, the Three Clarities are revered as the central axis.

These thirty-two heavens revolve ceaselessly, their *qi* systems governed by the interplay of yang moving within yin and yin moving within yang. The thirty-two heavens ascend in sequence, spiraling upward along the ram’s-horn path, ultimately ascending through the Dao-conduct to enter the Three Clarities.

The *Hidden Commentary on the Treasure Formula* states: "The Mysterious Staircase arises from the Whirlwind Terrace in the northeast—this is the Mysterious Heaven, the origin of ascent, signifying the celestial staircase emerging from the whirlwind." Additionally, the *Inner Tone* and the *Five Refinements of the Corpse* both array the thirty-two positions, distributing them across the four directions. Here, we briefly follow this text as one interpretive path.

**Question:** Why are humans attributed to the heavens but not to the four corner heavens—**Taihuang Huangzeng**, **Chiming Heyang**, **Yuanzai Kongsheng**, and **Haoting Xiaodu**?

**Answer:** Because the corner directions lack stellar mansions.

The *Sacred Records of Lord Lao, Scroll Ten: Deceptive Heresies* states: "This is the Jade Clarity Realm, where the Celestial Worthy of Primordial Beginning resides above the thirty-fifth heaven." It further says: "The *Great Perfection Records of the True Worthies* states: This is the Highest Clarity Realm, where the Grand Supreme Lord of the Dao resides above the thirty-fourth heaven." And: "The Great Clarity Realm, the Palace of the Supreme Ultimate, is where Lord Lao resides above the thirty-third heaven." It also says: "The Buddha, a Western foreigner who attained the Dao, presides over the Palace of Extended Truth on the thirtieth heaven—this is the king of Kapilavastu."

The Thirty-Two Emperors—according to the *Sutra of Boundless Salvation*—are as follows:
1. Yuyan Yuming
2. Xu’anatian
3. Yuanyu Qijing
4. Liudun Neixian

31. Yunshang Xuanyuan
32. Daze Famen

Together with the thirty-two heavens, these are the esoteric names of the various heavens.

The four directions each correspond to eight heavens and eight emperors, making thirty-two heavens and thirty-two emperors in total.

The Thirty-Two Prisons—according to the *Biography of Zhao Wenhe*—are as follows:
The Prison under the Three Heavens’ Bureau,
The Prison under the Northern Culmen’s Record Bureau,
The Prison under the Northern Asterism’s Life Bureau,
The Prison under the General and Grand Year,
The Prison under the Grand Yin and Grand Yang,
The Prison under the Minister of Works and Earth Mansion,
The Prison under the Five Departments’ Earth Lords,
The Prison under the True Officials of the Household,
The Prisons under the various Cold-Heat Hearth Lords,
The Prison at the Eastern Gate of Mount Tai of the Eastern Marchmount,
The Prison at the Southern Gate of Mount Heng of the Southern Marchmount,
The Prison at the Western Gate of Mount Hua of the Western Marchmount,
The Prison at the Northern Gate of Mount Heng of the Northern Marchmount,
The Prison at the Central Gate of Mount Song of the Central Marchmount,
And the twenty-eight stellar mansions.

The Prison under the Central Gates of the Thirty-Five Palaces,
The Prison under the Thirty-Six Chiefs of the Cloudy Heavens,
The Prison under the River Earl and the Nine Yangtze Water Lords,
The Prison under the Twelve River Pacification Luminaries,

The Prison under the Central Offices of Great and Lesser Wastage,
The Prison under the Litigation, Punishment, and Execution of the Three Mounds, Five Graves, and Twelve Tombs,
The Prison under the Central Offices of Restraining Form and Destructive Execution,
The Prison under the Central Gates of the Twelve Bureaus of the Orthodox King’s Tallies,
The Prison under Extended Life and Generated Destiny,
The Prison under the Twelve Monthly Establishments,
The Prison under the Twelve Prohibitions,
The Prison under the Central Offices of the Ten Elders’ Legal Bureau—

All petitions from the Celestial Master’s one thousand two hundred officials are submitted to these prisons, clearly distinguishing and governing the afflictions of the human body, so that no errors arise, no unjust suffering occurs, and one naturally attains peace, stability, and longevity, liberated even unto old age.

*Perfected is the Seventh Scroll of the Three Caverns’ Pearl Bag.*

**The Eighth Scroll of the Three Caverns’ Pearl Bag**
*Compiled by Wang Xuanhe, the Feathered Guest of Lu’s Sea, of the Great Tang*

**Chapter on Auspicious Marks**
*The Original Record of the Supreme Perfected’s Primordial Birth and Transformations* states:
The Primordial Venerable of the Supreme Elder wears upon his head a nine-colored cloud of cinnabar brocade, a hundred-changing radiance of cinnabar and purple clouds, and rides a nine-colored dragon.

It is also said:
The Venerable Elder of the Three Heavens bears twelve auspicious wheels upon his neck and possesses the hue of yellow gold.

*The Inner Secrets of the Nine Perfected of the Supreme Clarity* states:
The Yellow Elder of the Center shines with layered solar brilliance, his connected light illuminating the void. His canopy is woven of five clouds, his fragrant smoke profound and pure.

*The Scripture of the Lesser Kalpa* states:
His entire body is of yellow gold, his neck encircled by a seven-jeweled halo. His feet tread upon lotus blossoms as he walks.

*The Natural Rites of Laozi* states:
Laozi said: The Dao is present in all things. Jade countenance and golden form transcend the heavens, revered by both gods and humans—this is the object of meditative contemplation.

*The Scripture of the Three Dao’s Sequential Practices* states:
The essence of the seven treasures transforms into the seven stars, and the seven youths possess the purple radiance of the seven luminaries.

*The Scripture of the Great Kalpa* states:
The White-Yellow Lord entered a cave and beheld a perfected one, his light canopy resplendent. His form stood sixteen feet tall, his neck encircled by a halo, his entire body clad in seven-jeweled raiment.

It is also said:
The Supreme Sovereign of the Supreme Antiquity, the Perfected One, bears seventy-two marks and eighty-one excellences.

It is further said:
His hands radiate the six perfections, his demeanor profound and smiling, his excellences complete.

*The Scripture of the Feminine One and the Five Elders* states:
The Primordial Yellow Lady of the Yellow Plain, whose taboo name is *Round Flower Yellow Blade* and whose style is *Supreme Zhang*, possesses a form of yellow-golden substance.

*The Scripture of the Three Sovereigns* states:
The people of the northern lands have hair of dark azure hue and stand eight feet tall.

*The Scripture of the Eight Effulgences* states:
Those who ingest the divine elixir of descending life sprout nine morning lights upon their heads, their faces adorned with jade blossoms, their flight mirrored in jeweled radiance.

*The Twenty-Four Images of Life* states:
The flying immortals possess universal golden countenances.

The commentary on *The Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern, Thirty-Nine Chapters* states:
The Golden Immortals are those whose immortal hue and form gleam like golden light.

*The Scripture of Laozi’s Sixteen Transformations* states:
At the first transformation, he was born in the east, his body azure. His compassionate father’s surname was *Sea*, his mother’s *River*.
At the third transformation, his body bore thirty-six colors of brocade patterns.
At the fourth transformation, his forehead displayed the three yangs, his recumbent moon twelve lines, and his hands, though not open, grasped the patterns of scripture.

*The Lower Section of the Precepts of the Supreme Perfected* states:
The Jade Emperor of the Golden Gates of the Supreme Void, most revered and noble, neither born nor dying, abides in serene constancy. His jade countenance and golden form possess wondrous marks beyond compare.

*The Fifth of the Ten Latitudinal Scriptures of the Five Thousand Words* states:
The Heavenly Worthy emitted the luminous pearl from between his brows, illuminating all under heaven.

*The Scripture of the Great Cavern* states:
The Eastern King of Jade Clarity and Primordial Radiance, the Immortal Duke, is titled the Jade Sovereign Dao Lord. His neck bears a halo, his body emits jeweled effulgences, bright as the morning sun. In his hands he holds a flowing bell, his feet tread the seven primals. He gazes upward to the Supreme Origin and points downward to the boundless void.

*The Meaning of the Eight Difficulties in the Nine Chapters* states:
The auspicious marks of the various heavens include long eyebrows and high ears, a prominent nose and square pupils, azure kidneys with striated patterns, and a cinnabar heart with brocade-like lungs.
The inauspicious marks of the base include a crane’s back and tortoise’s breast, a hawk’s head and deer’s face, a fish’s mouth and bird’s beak, a goat’s nose and horse’s cheeks, a deer’s neck and pheasant’s sinews, a duck’s feet and pig’s hooves.

*The Meaning of the Immortal Marks in the Nine Chapters* states:
Azure liver and purple veins, azure kidneys with striated patterns.
Those with the *River Chariot* on their backs bear a black mark shaped like the Northern Dipper.
Those with four pupils in their eyes possess square pupils and round vision.
Those with three palates in their teeth have blade-like palates, their teeth and molars each bearing three-peaked edges.
Those with a thousand paired lines at their brow corners possess patterns of a thousand pairs rising toward the head.
Those with *sequential patterns forming ramparts* use their eyes as city walls, each with horizontal lines following the eyes.
Those with *hidden morning light behind the ears* have bones protruding behind their ears, visible externally, called *hidden morning light*.

The immortal Liu Jing said:
Those with square pupils in their eyes are people of a thousand years.

*The Scripture of the Immeasurable* states:
Their jade pupils shine brilliantly.

*The Third Scripture of the Fundamental Kalpa* states:
The Supreme Dao Lord of the Highest clacked his teeth and smiled, and a nine-jeweled radiance issued from his face, illuminating the Celestial Master’s body. He exhaled a soft voice to address the Celestial Master.

*The Pearl Instructions and Jade Tablets*, along with *The Western Ascent*, *The Womb of Returning Destiny*, and *The Inner Scripture of the Golden Tablet*, describe Laozi’s auspicious marks:
His body stood eight feet and eight inches tall, his complexion yellow. His eyebrows were fine, his ears long, his eyes large, his forehead broad. His teeth were spaced, his mouth square, his lips thick. His forehead bore the three and five penetrating principles. His temples displayed the sun’s corner and the moon’s suspension. His nose had a double ridge, his ears three openings. His feet trod the two and five, his hands grasped the ten patterns.

*The Esoteric Wondrous Chapters* state:
The Mysterious Wondrous Jade Maiden dreamed of a shooting star entering her mouth, whereupon she conceived. After eighty-one years, she gave birth to Laozi.

*The Scripture of the Supreme Origin* states:
Li’s mother, reclining during the day, saw a five-colored pearl the size of a pellet descend from the heavens. She swallowed it and immediately conceived.

*The Scripture of the Ten Pure Offerings to Laozi* states:
The Perfected One possessed the thirty-two marks and eighty excellences. His nape bore a halo of radiance, its light in five colors, luminous and resplendently pure.

*The Eighth Scroll of the Supreme Mystery* states:
Turning the wheel, one attains divine transcendence,
For I refine the essence of the heart.
Receiving boundless retribution,
With resolve fixed, one enters the court of fortune.
The thirty-two marks and eighty excellences
All shine forth from within the body.
His nape bears the seven-jeweled light,
Illumining the forms of all heavens.

*The Nine Chapters* states:
The Heavenly Worthy’s face emitted the five luminous hues.
The commentary explains: the five kinds of wisdom-light, to save the beings of the five destinies. It is also called the majestic radiance of the five virtues, or the light meant to illumine the lands of the five directions.

*The Second Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
As for the appearance of one born of earth: deep-set eyes and a dark bridge of the nose—the bridge being the nose. Hawk-like shoulders and a long neck, broad above and tapering below.
As for Pengzu’s appearance: his face bore unusual bones, his body extraordinary hairs.

*The Third Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
Wang Yuan, styled Fangping, was of yellow complexion, with scant beard and mustache, of medium height.
Also, the transcendent Ma Gu’s attendant maiden appeared to be about eighteen or nineteen, her hair gathered into a topknot, the rest hanging loose to her waist.

*The Fourth Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
The Maiden of Grand Yang had a complexion like peach blossoms, lips like cinnabar held within, her skin lustrous and radiant, her hair and flesh as though she were seventeen or eighteen.
The Master of Grand Yang, though his temples were streaked with white, had plump, glowing skin and a radiant countenance.
The Maiden of Grand Yin drank the water of divine light, her body ascending to the rank of the Prince’s Eminence, her form bearing the sacred mushrooms of the five phases.
Also, Sun Deng dwelled in mountain caves, his hair grown long enough to cover him, reaching over a *zhang* in length.

*The Sixth Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
The Eight Lords transformed into fifteen youths, their hair unbound and adorned with azure hues, their complexions like peach blossoms.

*The Seventh Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
Liu Gen, styled Jun’an, was a native of Chang’an in Jingzhao. His eyes were deep-set, his beard and hair thick, both yellow and measuring two to four *cun* in length. The hair on his body grew one to two *chi* long.

*The Tenth Scroll of the Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states:
Li Gen, styled Ziyuan, had pupils in both eyes perfectly square.
According to *The Scripture of Transcendents*: at eight hundred years, the pupils become square.
Dongguo Yannian, a native of Shanyang, ingested the *Lingfei* powder and could write at night. In a darkened chamber, his body emitted light, illuminating all around him.

*The Chapter on Establishing Merit in the Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection* states:
Born with azure bones, one communes with spirits and joins the Perfected.

*The Inner Scripture of the Six Jia of Supreme Purity* states:
During the ten-day periods of the six Jia, the Jade Maidens all wore three-cornered topknots, the rest of their hair hanging loose to their waists.

*The Scripture of Boundless Transformations and Births* states:
The Most High’s body was golden in color, his face suffused with purple light.

*The Jade Instructions of the Great Cavern* states:
The Golden Flower Transcendent drank the flowing rosy clouds, whereby his five viscera became bright and clear, and his face bore purple clouds.

*The Records of the Deep Mysteries of Han Emperor Wu* states:
The transcendent Bian Bozi ate water caltrops from the sea, his bones grew light, and his body sprouted feathers.
(Note: *Bian* may also be written as *Fu*.)

*The Scripture on Commanding Demons of Supreme Purity* states:
The Perfected Guardian of the Great Treasure set his feet upon the seven measures, grasped the celestial mechanism in his hands, his crown covered the mysterious celestial bodies, and he united with the two primal forces.

*The Scripture of the Eight Simplicities* states:
Those who ingest the essence of the sun and moon have bodies that reflect jade light and faces that emit golden perfection.
It also states: the face has jade luster, the body emits golden light.
It also states: the face has a golden countenance, the head emits purple light.
It also states: the nape emits purple light, the face radiates a golden countenance.
It also states: the three gates open the mechanism, the nine portals receive the numinous. The face emits a golden countenance, the five viscera flourish in splendor. Golden perfection flows freely, the vast expanse is thoroughly illuminated. The spirit blazes with latent radiance, treasure-light arises at night.

*The True Instructions of the Three-Nine Simplicities and Jade Essence* states:
The face emits a golden countenance, the five interiors flourish in splendor. The jade viscera preserve qi, and the Dao of divine transcendence is accomplished.

*The Mysterious Record of the Seven Sages of the Jade Emperor* states:
The Maiden of the Western Florescence, the Youth of the Golden Dawn, displayed cloud-like grace by the jasper side, bearing a golden countenance within the orchid chamber.
It also states: extraordinary hairs of the spirit, purple womb and jade network.
It also states: flowing essence and purple light, inwardly reflecting and outwardly entwining, treasure-hidden golden countenance.

*The Scripture of the Jade Tallies of the Three Origins* states:
The Primordial Lady of Purple Simplicity wore the crown of the Great Perfected and Morning Infants, her hair in a three-cornered topknot, the rest hanging loose to her waist.
It also states: golden bones and jade marrow, the mysterious name recorded in the imperial register.

*The Scripture of the Three Dao in Harmonious Progression* states:
The entire body radiates brightness, the face emits the essence of azure brilliance.

*The Scripture of the Celestial Net and the Terrestrial Record of Pacing the Stars* states:
The Divine Youth of the Western Numinosity had a face bearing jade splendor.
It also states: the True Consort of the Southern Numinosity, the Purple Numinous Lovely Maiden, had a face bearing golden and jade dragon splendor.
It also states: the Pass Keeper Yin Xi had a nape emitting treasure-bright light, the seventy-two marks illuminating his single form.
It also states: Yin Xi’s heart was bound with purple networks, his face bore perfect clarity, his nape supported the heavens, and his back bore the Seven Origins.

*The Miscellaneous Sayings of Laozi* states:
Yin Xi’s eyes held the essence of the sun, his bearing was tall and refined, his arms hung down to his knees, his majestic presence was that of a celestial being.
It also states: his head bore a halo of radiance, his five viscera had patterns, his face had seven stars, above mirroring the celestial patterns, below aligning with terrestrial principles, all perfectly complete.

*The Scripture of the Golden Root* states:
The Azure Essentials Emperor Lord had a face emitting a golden countenance, his body bore numinous talismans, seventy-two hues thoroughly illuminating his jade form, the three dawns entwining, the six qi harmonizing as one.
It also states: golden skeleton and jade bones, name inscribed in the imperial register.
It also states: the face had jade essence, the body emitted purple light.
It also states: the Maiden of Grand Yang had a face emitting golden light.

It also states: Jade Numinosity Master’s nape perpetually emitted purple light, illuminating ten *li* in all directions. His two eyes held flowing essence, like dark stars reflecting; his face radiated a golden countenance, shining with empty brightness at night.

It also states: The Ninefold Perfected Lord was the Nine Heavens’ Venerable One—his eyes round, his mouth square, his voice like thunder’s roar. His nape bore purple light, illuminating the ten heavens and penetrating the Great Primal.

*The Scripture of Great Possession, Lower Volume* states: The Mother of Jade Purity was surnamed Lian, named Xian. Her head wore a topknot of seven-colored pearls and jades (the topknot pronounced *ji*).

It also states: The Highest Purity Maiden was surnamed Jue, named Si. Her head wore a topknot of jade treasures and flying clouds.

It also states: The Empress of the Great Ultimate was surnamed Xuan, named Hu. Her head wore a topknot of seven treasures and dark clouds.

It also states: The Queen of the Supreme Lord was surnamed Qian, named Han’ai. Her head wore a topknot of ninefold dark jade and crumbling clouds, and she also wore a crown, the name of which is recorded in the *Ranks of Robes and Crowns*.

*The Scripture of Great Possession, Upper Volume* states: Extraordinary fur and rare substance, golden bones and jade name.

It also states: The Jade Youth of the Crimson Palace wore a topknot of three-peaked clouds. The Jade Maiden of Constant Yang wore a topknot of flying rosy clouds. The Immortal Youth of Slaying Clouds wore a topknot of three-tiered clouds. The Jade Maiden of the Red Jade Tablet wore a topknot of crumbling clouds.

It also states: When the joyous Red Child’s true numen descended, his face emitted jade luster, his body radiated wondrous light, penetrating the subtle and obscure.

*The Scripture of the Eight Gates of the Dark Mother* states: The Left Azure-Silk Primordial Lord, the Right White-Silk Primordial Lord, and the Central Yellow-Silk Primordial Lord each bore a treasure on their napes, their solar qi forming nine-colored circular radiance that brightly illumined the golden-flowered numinous chamber. To visualize this light is called the *Threefold Silk’s Feminine Unity of True Flowery Refinement*, or also the *Jade Dawn’s Threefold Silk Sun Bathing the Form*.

*The Scripture of the Eight Gates of the Dark Mother* states: The immortal Zhao Chengzi’s face emitted jade light, his dark hair soft and lustrous.

*The Scripture of the Great Cavern, Lower Volume* states: Bones held the jade radiance of the Five Thearchs, the face had flowing golden springs—such were the marks of celestial immortals.

*The Hidden Writ of Jade Purity* states: The Supreme Tenuity Thearch Lord advanced and bowed at the imperial throne, leaning upon his jade countenance in wondrous resonance, gazing up with numinous eyes to present his words.

It also states: Upon reciting *The Hidden Writ of Jade Purity* ten thousand times to completion, one’s body would shine with golden dawn.

*The Commentary on the Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: The Highest Sovereign Perfected One’s nape bore a treasure, a radiant circular light.

*The Jade Chapters of the Divine Continent* states: The circular flower illumined the great radiance—this was the Central Perfected of the Yellow and Venerable.

*The Commentary on the Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: The immortal’s complexion was like the reflection of golden light.

*The Concealed Instructions for Ascending Perfection, Fourth Scroll* states: The Director of Destinies’ eyes held flowing light, his face emitted jade luster.

It also states: The Perfected One of the Great Ultimate’s inner numinous light shone, vermilion flowers manifested externally, his body emitted jade radiance.

*The Declarations of the Perfected, Second Scroll* states: After ingesting the nine-times-cycled elixir, one’s complexion resembled numinous clouds.

*The Declarations of the Perfected, Seventh Scroll* states: The immortal Liu Ping’a had a complexion like jade.

It also states: Sima Jizhu ingested the flower of bright elixir, drawing in the rosy glow of dawn’s twilight. Having attained the Dao in the Palace of Great Possession, his complexion was like that of a twenty-year-old maiden, his beard three feet long, black as ink.

*The Inner Instructions on the Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected Ones of Highest Purity* states: Those who ingest the *Eight Effulgences, Four Blossoms, Five Pearls, Crimson Life-Generating Elixir* will have their heads emit the light of nine dawns, their faces bear jade flowers that fly and reflect precious luminances, penetratingly observing the world below.

Crush the dregs of the *Eight Effulgences Elixir* and ingest one pellet the size of a small bean each day. The body will emit jade light, lifespan equaling the nine dawns, and the fragrance of one’s body will be detectable thirty *li* away.

*The Scripture of the Great Cavern, Central Volume* states: The Thearch’s single body generated six colors, illuminating the golden radiance and flowing numinous form.

*The Scripture of the Great Cavern of Perfection* states: If one’s body naturally lacks treasure bones and green blood, and the five viscera hold no divine light of gold and jade, then the Dao of the Feminine Unity and the Thearch Unity cannot be heard or seen.

It also states: If the omen of one’s body naturally lacks the vermilion cloud’s liquid, the jade-harmonized qi, emits jade flowers within the Muddy Pellet, or the primordial luxuriance of the Great Plain’s essence within the Crimson Palace; if the jade-forest’s branches do not flourish in the Gate of Destiny, or the nine dancing plumes do not lie prostrate above the Great Ultimate, then *The Scripture of the Great Cavern of Perfection* cannot be heard or seen.
