If one lacks these marks of excellence, the Highest Thearch will not permit its transmission.

It also states: Nine lights illumined the form, penetratingly shining through the entire body. The body’s five viscera and ten thousand passages were all brightly revealed.

*The Scripture of Transforming the Barbarians* states: Laozi’s body bore the seventy-two marks of adamantine perfection. His hair was dark blue, his face and eyes emitted purple-golden radiance, his face held five-colored light.

*The Scripture of the Seven Stars’ Transference of Degrees* states: May my body generate ten thousand marvels and seventy-two lights, extraordinary fur and rare bones, flying feathered robes. May I ride the void and drive the sky, entering and exiting the imperial palace, with all blessings arriving and infinite longevity.

It also states: When the seventy-two marks of the Ultimate Dao are fully complete, one ascends to heaven in broad daylight. Thus *The Eight Effulgences of the Three Caverns of Numinous Treasure* states: The twenty-four marks of the upper portion are as follows:

First, both eyes hold twin lights;
Second, both brows resemble newly risen twin moons;
Third, hair is dark blue in color;
Fourth, the crown bears a cloud topknot like a purple-gold seal;
Fifth, the head’s crown is fourfold round;
Sixth, the head’s upper portion is round and lower portion square, like a purple-gold mountain;
Seventh, light arises from the celestial center;
Eighth, within the golden-flower division is seven-jeweled light;
Ninth, within the dark cinnabar division are twin celestial pillars;
Tenth, within the Great Sovereign division is a square like a jade seal;
Eleventh, within the Hall of Light division is a circle like a chariot wheel, naturally bearing white down;
Twelfth, within the Cavern Chamber division are red glows and purple networks.

Thirteenth, within the Mud-Pill division, golden essence flows as liquid, blending myriad aspects;
Fourteenth, both ears resemble golden city walls;
Fifteenth, the face is like a red lotus, round as a full moon;
Sixteenth, the lashes resemble the twin August Celestial Microcosms;
Seventeenth, the eyelids are like twin moons, with upper arcs and pupils clear and limpid, slow and unblinking;
Eighteenth, behind both ears is the handle of the Northern Dipper;
Nineteenth, the nose is like a golden pillar, bearing three apertures;
Twentieth, the mouth is like cinnabar, with three streams of fluid flowing from within the throat, producing boundless subtle and wondrous sounds;
Twenty-first, the teeth are interlinked like carriage shafts;
Twenty-second, the tongue bears a golden flow, broad and long enough to cover the face;
Twenty-third, the cheeks are like a lion’s, the jaw like an inscribed seal;
Twenty-fourth, the head is like a celestial pillar, fully possessing the Three Essentials.

*Lingbao Three Divisions and Eight Radiances*: The twenty-four marks of the middle portion are as follows:

First, the heart possesses nine apertures, each aperture bearing nine hairs;
Second, the chest resembles layered cowrie script, with myriad spokes like wheel hubs, characters distinct;
Third, the body stands upright, both hands resting upon the knees;
Fourth, beneath both armpits is a level fullness like the Pivot Star;
Fifth, the body’s form is like the revolving jade;
Sixth, to the left of the heart is the Palace of Great Light;
Seventh, to the right of the heart is the Palace of Great Mystery;
Eighth, the abdomen hangs like a suspended tray;
Ninth, the navel is like the Pearl of Numinous Treasure;
Tenth, the navel alone possesses the Three Essentials;
Eleventh, the countenance is dragon-like, the bearing phoenix-like;
Twelfth, the yin aspect resembles a lotus seed;
Thirteenth, the back is level and straight like soaring clouds;
Fourteenth, to the left of the back is the Eastern Florescence Gate;
Fifteenth, to the right of the back is the Western Numinous Gate;
Sixteenth, sitting is like a crouching dragon;
Seventeenth, leaning is like the Herdboy star;
Eighteenth, walking is like a phoenix in flight;
Nineteenth, marrow transforms into bone, bones like coiled dragons;
Twentieth, the countenance is flower-like, the substance jade-like;
Twenty-first, the radiance is golden, the visage purple;
Twenty-second, both breasts resemble □□;
Twenty-third, beneath both breasts is the Southern Asterism;
Twenty-fourth, the entire body is purple-hued with a red glow like the sun’s radiance.

*Lingbao Three Divisions and Eight Radiances*: The twenty-four marks of the lower portion are as follows:

First, both feet are level and full like twin wheel gates;
Second, beneath both feet are thousand-spoked wheel hubs;
Third, the soles of both feet are like the Celestial River;
Fourth, the toes are long and joined like a fine net, fully formed;
Fifth, beneath both feet are lotus-wheel pedestals;
Sixth, the heels of both feet are fully formed, distinct and excellent;
Seventh, the insteps of both feet are high and level, well-proportioned to the heels;
Eighth, the ankles of both feet are prominent;
Ninth, both shins are like twin pillars;
Tenth, both arms are like upturned golden boats;
Eleventh, each pore bears a single hair, soft and curling to the right;
Twelfth, both knees are like the *piao* star;
Thirteenth, the inner sides of both knees resemble *qian* fruit;
Fourteenth, the outer sides of both knees resemble *qian* blossoms;
Fifteenth, above the knees is like a jade casket;
Sixteenth, the thighs are like twin jade axles;
Seventeenth, the inner sides of both thighs resemble the Jade Balance;
Eighteenth, the outer sides of both thighs resemble golden beams;
Nineteenth, above both thighs is a jade radiance;
Twentieth, both thighs together bear twin bones like coiled dragons;
Twenty-first, golden bones and jade marrow are visible within and without;
Twenty-second, the entire body is broad and long, its strength like vajra;
Twenty-third, the color is like purple gold, neither deficient nor excessive;
Twenty-fourth, the entire body is luminous and pure, illuminating the ten directions, abundant in wisdom, its profound awakening yet to unfold—throughout the Three Realms and Nine Paths, all living beings ever wish to behold it.

When the Great Vehicle’s myriad practices reach perfection, fully possessing the seventy-two marks, one severs ties with the human world, transcending to ascend heaven in broad daylight, achieving the supreme and ultimate Dao, the ancestor of all immortals, the honored among all sages. Thus, the *Sutra of Insightful Wisdom and the Great Precepts* states: “Resplendent is the vajra body, surpassing the Supreme Transcendents.” Therefore, it is said: the Dao within the Dao, the immortal among immortals.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes* states: “Atop the head’s crown, the Primordial Ultimate is boundless, universally perceiving the immeasurable, penetratingly illuminating the supreme and most true, profoundly tranquil and mysteriously pervading, the source of great wisdom.” If one does not possess the seventy-two marks, all will perish and be reborn among humans, further cultivating merit and establishing virtue, progressing from the subtle to the manifest, thereby attaining the seventy-two marks, transcending to ascend heaven in broad daylight and achieve the supreme Dao without duality. Thus, it is called the True One, the Primordial Beginning, the Great Dao.

Thus, the *Jade Register of the Three Primes* states: “The body penetrates the purple void, the spirit reflects the golden countenance.” The seventy-two marks brightly illumine the great firmament.

The *Dharma Wheel Sutra* states: “Attaining the vajra body with seventy-two marks, the nape bears perfect clarity, penetratingly reflecting the great void, ascending to the rank of lofty immortal.” It further states: “The thirty-two marks of excellence all shine forth from within the body. The nape bears seven-jeweled light, illuminating the forms of all heavens.”

As for Laozi’s seventy-two marks and eighty-one excellences, Laozi undergoes nine transformations: In the first transformation, his body is six feet and six inches tall, wearing a fish-hawk crown and eight-fringed phoenix robe; in the second transformation, his body is seven feet and seven inches tall, wearing a layered crown and white robe with red collar and sleeves; in the third transformation, his body is eight feet and eight inches tall, wearing a *tongtian* crown and five-colored robe; in the fourth transformation, his body is nine feet and nine inches tall, wearing a *bixie* crown and cassia-silk robe; in the fifth transformation, his body is ten feet and three inches tall, wearing a dragon-serpent crown and vermilion radiance robe; in the sixth transformation, his body is ten feet and seven inches tall, wearing a *xuwu* crown and black feathered robe...

In the seventh transformation, his body is ten feet tall, wearing an *yuanqi* crown and dragon-serpent robe; in the eighth transformation, his body is eleven feet and five inches tall, wearing a *baibian* crown and natural robe. When Laozi undergoes his ninth transformation, his body possesses seventy-two marks, corresponding to the seventy-two *qi*, and eighty-one excellences.

The seventy-two marks are as follows: His head is round, modeling Heaven; his crown resembles Kunlun. His hair is coiled like morning clouds, his jade-like nape rising gently. His hoary hair is like a crane’s, over seven feet long; his tiger-like whiskers and dragon-like beard are pure and silken. His brows resemble the Northern Dipper, their color like emerald green; between them grows a purple hair, over five inches long. His ears lack outer rims, with three openings within, rising level with his crown, thick and firm. His two eyes are clear as mirrors, their pupils shining with solar essence and purple light; his square pupils are bright and refined, with green veins at their center. His nose has twin pillars, shaped like a cut tube. His mouth is square as the sea, his lips red as cinnabar. His breath carries a purple hue, its fragrance like orchids. His teeth are like contained cowries, firm as silver, thirty-two in number, evenly aligned above and below. His tongue is long and broad, patterned like brocade; jade-like springs overflow within, its taste sweet and fragrant, its sound like gold, its tone like jade. His cheeks resemble transverse ridges, his jaw like a mound; his forehead is radiant as the sun, his temples concealed as the moon. His brow bears straight, rhinoceros-like lines, his dragon-like visage divinely mutable; his golden countenance is yellow-hued, his jade-like bearing lustrous. His forehead has three lines, ascending in alignment; his celestial court is level and full, his face square—a sign of longevity. His abdomen bears white moles, his jaw a jade-like orb. His neck has three folds, white as a crane’s and towering. His arms hang past his knees, his hands bearing ten lines. His fingers have jade-like nails, his body green down. His back bears the *He Kui* star, his chest the recumbent bone. His heart has nine apertures, its exterior patterned like brocade. His navel is an inch deep, his belly soft as silk. His feet are square as a carpenter’s square, his soles like paired *Dharma* wheels. His steps tread the Two and Five, his toes bearing Qian and Kun. His blood is white within, his outward appearance aged. His body is twelve feet tall, his entire form exuding fresh fragrance. His gait is like a tiger’s stride, his movement swift as a dragon’s.

These are the seventy-two marks. To his left, he is supported by the Azure Dragon; to his right, the White Tiger. Above his head arises the Vermilion Bird; beneath his feet treads the Dark Warrior. His body is like *vajra*, his countenance like lapis lazuli. A fivefold radiance encircles him, purple *qi* rises above his head, and the true character gleams upon his chest. These nine excellences, combined with the preceding seventy-two marks, form the eighty-one excellences.

The *Golden Book of Immortal Records* and the *Arrayed Chronicles of the Nine Mysteries of the Later Sage* both state: The Azure Lad said, "Those with bone registers are inclined toward immortality. Those inclined toward immortality possess immortal aspirations. Among those with immortal aspirations, some are weary, others steadfast. Weariness stems from insufficient merit in past lives; steadfastness arises when the mysterious register and predestined fate are settled. Generally, when celestial registers manifest in the Mysterious Palace, the *qi* and seasons align with the bodily form; when register characters are revealed in the Supreme Ultimate, the heart and spirit are rectified in the cinnabar chamber. If one is born with a name inscribed in the Golden Tower and Jade Register, their eyes will shine with solar light, their teeth will be green, and their blood white. Such a person is benevolent and delights in immortality, intelligent and outstanding. If one possesses the Golden Book and Jade Register of the Upper Clarity, their back will bear the *He Kui* star and their chest the recumbent bone. Such a person is reverent, humble, and extends virtue even to insects. If one bears the cinnabar script and azure characters of the Supreme Ultimate, their hands will display the characters of 'inverted greatness' and 'accumulated humanity.' Such a person is discreet and devoted to truth, pure and tolerant of others. If one has a name inscribed in the dark and white registers of the *Fangzhu*, their eyes will have four pupils with purple light illuminating their form. Such a person cultivates profound and wondrous practices, cleanses the present, and avoids defilement. If one bears the inner jade weft of the Cloud Chamber, their eyes will be round and observant, their mouth dragon-like, their tongue fine. Such a person is open-hearted and embodies truth, discerning and decisive. If one has a cinnabar character and purple name in the Vermilion Palace, their movements will resemble the phoenix’s dance and the simurgh’s leap, their navel palace radiant. Such a person is attentive to life’s inquiries, their heart open and pure. If one has their name compiled in the Jade Register of the Grand Clarity, their voice will carry the tone of jade and the resonance of gold, their mouth square, their eyes round. Such a person is magnanimous and broadly loving, cherishing others as a mother. If one has a name inscribed on the jade slips of the Grand Simplicity, their abdomen will reveal a white aspiration, their mouth emit purple *qi*. Such a person is compassionate and spiritually attuned, humbly benevolent toward all. If one bears the cinnabar script and purple register of the Southern Culmen, five *qi* will rise from their head, connecting to the layered clouds of the celestial towers. Such a person is harmonious, benevolent, and aids the destitute, relieving hardship and rescuing from peril. If one has their name recorded in the mysterious jade registers of the Dipper, their heart will have nine apertures, their lungs bear brocade-like patterns, their jaw a jade orb, their eyes green veins, and their brow angles two ascending lines. Their facial contours are orderly, their temples exposed, their bright hall level and white. The dry lines serve as the passage to true transcendence, the broad forehead as the dwelling of the numinous. Such a person is compassionate toward the poor and humble, their benevolence extending even to birds and beasts. If one bears the azure-gold and cinnabar script of the Upper Primordial in the Mysterious Palace, their heart will be cinnabar with purple apertures, their bones encircled by yellow blossoms, their breath fragrant, and their teeth filled with jade-like fluid. Such a person delights in gazing at the moon’s flowing rosy clouds and the stars’ luminous scenes from youth, their essence pure, their bones firm, their sincerity deep and secret. If one has a name inscribed in white jade and gold characters on the Cinnabar Terrace of the Mysterious Capital, their liver will be green with purple vessels, their kidneys patterned like layered silk, their dark breast brimming with essence, their form rivaling their spirit in purity. Their body is fragrant and supple, their blood clear, their *qi* lustrous. Such a person is devoted to the distant and mysterious, savoring the numinous essence, benevolent toward inferiors, and rescues those in hardship and suffering."

If the Three Primordials Palace bears jade tablets inscribed in azure script, such a person will have a purple brain and brocade tongue, dark aspirations at the temples, green intestines and vermilion marrow, square feet and rounded brow, hidden reinforcing bones, soft hair with purple sheen, three gates at the orifices, movements slightly restrained, eyes gleaming with flowing light, azure essence congealing into fluid, palms marked with four fungi, and teeth with triple palates. Such a person possesses a numinous heart and benevolent love, their kindness stirring the divine; they delight in subtle reverence and trust, love forests and spring, cherish clear-flowing waters, hold mountains and rivers in their heart, yearn to inscribe their name on the Azure Peak, preserve their *po* and nurture their *hun*, their aspirations soaring toward serene tranquility, and long for the celestial immortals.

All who bear these thirteen superior forms are of the highest destiny, certain to attain the rank of supreme immortality—this may be achieved through study or even without it.

Next is the Dark Mountain upon the nose. The Dark Mountain refers to a black mark upon the nose. There should also be a Dark Mound upon the abdomen, directly opposite the Dark Mountain. The Dark Mound is likewise a black mark. If either is lacking, the immortal’s physiognomy is incomplete. If one’s breath is foul and one’s nature tolerates filth, the signs of the Dark Mountain and Dark Mound are entirely ruined.

Next is the Azure Bone. Those with Azure Bone delight in the fragrance of the five incenses and are drawn to the study of divine and numinous matters.

Next are the crane’s gait and dragon’s stride, a jade pillow upon the nape, hidden dawn behind the ears, azure marks beneath the ribs, a network of veins upon the body, a true heart and tranquil gall, firm ears and expansive *qi*—these are all signs of lesser immortals.

The *Scripture of the Supreme Void Sovereign Lord, First Scroll* states: "The feather-robed destiny-immortals bear bones suffused with jade radiance, their blood transformed into nectarous springs; they rejoice in heaven and earth, their years equal to the sun and moon."

The *Lower Scroll of the Jade Characters of Inner Sound* states: "Jade pupils are the essence of flowing fire. Having received the crimson brilliance of the Harmonious Yang Heaven’s flowing fire, they refine the body to generate jade light, filling the Crimson Palace, where the ten thousand spirits converge."

The *Scripture of the Purple Florescence and Blazing Light* states: "The Great Dao Lord of the Supreme traverses the radiant aureole, its light surging upward to awaken the might of the Nine Heavens, descending to extinguish the malice of the Six Heavens. The mysterious light’s empty radiance crowns the Dao Lord’s head, flowing to illuminate the eight directions for four hundred thousand *li*."

The *Hidden Instructions of the Dragon-Flight Plain Silk* states: "The body generates precious luminosity, the nape bears a halo of light."

The *Thirty-Nine Chapters of the Great Cavern Jade Scripture* states: "A golden countenance shines upon the Eastern Flower, a jade form sheds its skin at the Emperor’s Gate. The spirit mirrors the Five Elders, leaping through the Three Primordials. Numinous feathers drape the void, *qi* vast as auspicious clouds. They can also manifest water and fire, emit light for ten thousand *ren*, bear precious luminosity upon the nape, and roam the Nine Mornings. Dispersing their form and scattering their radiance, they ascend as supreme perfected ones."

It further states: "Jade lads and jade maidens, their faces all aglow with jade splendor and golden dawn’s light, illuminate their entire form."

The *Bright Codes of the Four Poles* states: "A halo upon the nape shines to illuminate the Ten Heavens." It also states: "Those who obtain these hidden writings of the Supreme Clarity will have eyes with revolving essence and faces suffused with purple complexion." And: "The chapter *Returning Youth and the Sun’s Radiance, Born of the Void* grants eyes with revolving essence and pupils of flowing light."

The *Seventy-Four Methods of the Supreme Clarity’s Transformations* states: "The Lord of Longevity at the Southern Pole, Wang Yidu, emits solar essence from his face and lightning from his eyes." It further states: "The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens bear halos upon their napes, their bodies generating jade essence, their hands grasping luminous clouds, their feet treading the Seven Primordials." And: "Bones transform and coalesce into jade, the immortal’s countenance flourishing with splendor."

The *Seven Revolutions and Seven Transformations of the Divine Continent* states: "The Purple Dawn Lord’s face emits a golden complexion, his body suffused with jade light, five-colored purple patterns, seventy-two transformations, his essence illuminating his jade visage." It further states: "Those who practice the *Seven Revolutions of the Divine Continent and the Heaven-Dancing Way* will emit golden light from their bodies, their faces aglow with golden radiance, the Seven Stars networked upon their forms, riding clouds to ascend the mornings."

The *Upper Scripture of the Golden Pendants* states: "Eyes bright and penetrating, perceiving the deepest mysteries. A golden complexion upon the face, the body generating jade essence." It further states: "A face with jade luster, the body generating wondrous light, inner and outer brilliance."

The *Scripture of the Foreign Lands’ Liberated Grades* states: "The Azure Lad’s crown emits precious light, illuminating the Ten Heavens."

The *Inner Biography of Lord Pei* states: "The Pure Numinous Perfected, Lord Pei, styled Xuanren, was clear and bright from youth, his countenance and bearing refined and unadorned, skilled in speech and laughter, his eyes bearing essence-light, his arms hanging past his knees, his voice and *qi* resonant and far-reaching, his call ringing like a bell." It further states: "His eyes held pearls resembling the Northern Dipper’s stars, their lower aspect like the River Chariot—this is the aspiration of divine immortals."

The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: "Aqiu and Zengzhong, their thirty-two marks fully manifest, illuminate the female form."

The *Upper Scroll of the Jade Characters of Inner Sound* states: "All who cultivate the Way of Flying Immortals generate jade light from their bodies."

The *Five Talismans* states: "The August Person stands nine *chi* tall, his body covered in dark hair, each over a *chi* long, his hair only a few *cun* in length, dwelling beneath the sheer cliffs north of Mount Emei."

The *Commentary on the Thirty-Nine Chapters of the Great Cavern Jade Scripture* states: "The Supreme August Perfected bears precious luminosity upon his crown, his body suffused with a halo of light, his *qi* harmonizing the Three Simplicities, his spirit penetrating the Five Viscera."

The *Preface to the Scripture of the Inner Chamber* states: "The Ten Signs of Immortality: First, born with a golden frame and jade name; second, the Great Mysterious Palace bears a plain register; third, the left hand bears a great character..."

Fourth, the back bears a blue mark resembling the River Chariot; fifth, the body bears the Seven Stars’ mark; sixth, the crown emits a purple radiance that illuminates the body; seventh, the gait is like a crane’s and the stride like a dragon’s, with the body adorned in networked patterns; eighth, the heart has nine apertures and beneath the lungs lies a blue cavity; ninth, the head generates five *qi* that ascend to meet layered clouds; tenth, the voice rings like jade and gold, and the mouth exhales purple *qi*. Those born with these signs need not study the Dao—they are destined to become immortals.

The *Hidden Writings of the Two Luminaries, Sun and Moon* states: "The August Jade Emperor descends from the Jade Void Sovereign’s lineage, his bones of jade and marrow of gold, born of phoenix brain and dragon embryo."

The *Morning Audience Writ of the Jade Scripture of the Upper Clarity True Writ* states: "His eyes hold mysterious light, his mouth flows with jade nectar, his nose emits jade fire, his ears command numinous spirits, his heart has nine apertures, and he ascends the Nine Heavens of the Dao. His feet bear the Eight Historians, and he ascends to the Gate of Heaven. When he sits, rises, sleeps, or rests, jade lads attend his words, and the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper ever dwell before his breast."

*The Fourth Scroll of the Transmission of Daoist Learning* states: "Fan Cai had fair skin and beautiful hair, with elegant brows and bright eyes."

*The Ritual of the Three Sovereigns* states: "May we attain immortality, our bodies adorned with purple networked feather patterns."

*The Seventh Scroll of the Transmission of Daoist Learning* states: "Lu Xiujing, styled Yuande, was a native of Dongqian in Wuxing. On the day of his birth, his soles bore double wheels, his feet had twin ankles, his palms bore great characters, and his body bore the Dipper’s pattern."

The eighth scroll states: "Tao Hongjing, styled Tongming, was a native of Pingyang in Weijun. His bearing was dignified and pure, his stature seven *chi* and two *cun* tall, his head towering and ears high. Each ear bore over ten long hairs, his right thigh had several dozen black moles arranged in the Seven Stars’ pattern, and his eyes beheld wondrous radiant phenomena."

The ninth scroll states: "Xue Biaozhi was a native of Jinling. He consumed multitudes of blossoms, his years advanced yet his complexion youthful, his beard and hair lustrous and black."

*The Biographies of the Immortals* states: "Wo Quan was a gatherer of herbs on Mount Huai. Fond of eating pine nuts, his body grew hair several *cun* long, his eyes became square, and he could fly to keep pace with galloping horses."

It further states: "The Lady of Yangdu was a girl who sold wine in the marketplace. Born with joined brows and long, slender ears, all marveled at her, calling her a celestial being. She wed a man of Ye named Duzi, and together they entered the mountains."

*The Latter Biographies of the Immortals* states: "Master Ning had a hairy body, broad ears, and unbound hair."

The *Laozi’s Scripture on Virtue and the Dao* states: "Thick hair is the root of attaining the Dao; sweat on hands and feet signals abundant essence-*qi*. Day and night undistracted, the sun and moon merge their light; free from hunger and thirst, one practices the breath of the tortoise and dragon."

*The Fourth Scripture of the Origin* states: "The Most High Dao Lord, with his wisdom of others’ minds and unhindered knowledge of past lives, could observe distant karmic causes, though the shallow and dull had yet to awaken to truth."

*The Luminous Regulations of the Four Poles* states: "Those with names inscribed on the Mysterious Register of the Imperial Chart, characters on purple slips, and bones of jade and gold may receive three transmissions of the *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* within a thousand years."

It further states: "The *Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* is concealed in the Six Harmonies Palace of the Most High. Those with names written in blue on the Eastern Florescence, jade characters of the Upper Clarity, and bodies bearing purple networks may receive three transmissions within seven hundred years."

It further states: "The *Hidden Writ of the Great Elixir* is concealed within the Purple Chamber of the Six Harmonies Palace of the Most High. Those with names inscribed on the Imperial Chart in green characters and bones of purple that harmonize with the True may receive three transmissions within seven hundred years."

It further states: "The *Purple Writ of the Blue Essentials*—those with marrow of gold and bones of jade, their names inscribed on the Imperial Register, may receive three transmissions within seven hundred years."

*The Luminous Regulations of the Four Poles of the Right Palace of the Great Mystery Capital* states: "Those with jade bones may transmit the *Luminous Regulations of the Four Poles* from the treasure store of the Upper Clarity."

*The Inner Biography of Perfected Lord Wang of the Clear Void* states: "Perfected Lord Wang, whose name was Bao and style Zideng, consumed dragon-bright pearls and crimson harmonious cloud fungi. His body radiated golden light, his neck bore a halo, the Seven Luminaries scattered blossoms, and flowing radiance illumined his form."

*The Inner Biography of the Lady of the Southern Marchmount* states: "Her essence was lofty and resplendent, her round spirit doubly radiant, her body that of a phoenix and bones of a dragon. Her brain shone with precious luminosity, her five viscera bore purple networks, and her heart had feathered patterns."

*The Scripture of the Eight Luminaries of the Most High* states: "Those who consume the four medicines, purple nectar, five pearls, and crimson life-generating elixir will have their heads emit the light of the Nine Dawns, their faces bear jade splendor, and flying radiance illumine precious luminosity. They will perceive all under heaven, ascend through the void to the Purple Void, enter and exit the Jade Clarity, and repose in the Morning Chamber."

It further states: "The *Secret of the Celestial Net’s Flight* is concealed within the Purple Chamber of the Jade Void. Those with names inscribed on the Imperial Register in gold, jade tablets of the Upper Clarity, and bones harmonizing with the True may receive three transmissions within seven hundred years."

It further states: "The *Orthodox Law of the Three Heavens* is concealed within the Golden Chamber of the Jade Clarity atop the Nine Heavens. Those with names inscribed in gold and jade characters, bodies bearing purple storehouses and jade marrow, may receive three transmissions within seven hundred years."

*The Scripture of the Golden Register’s Simplified Writ* states: "Closing the eyes and visualizing the body as golden, the neck bears a halo like the sun’s image, illuminating the ten directions. Within the body, all is clearly seen, both inner and outer."

*The Scripture of the True Talismans for Dispelling Demons* states: "Those with marrow of gold and bones of jade, whose five viscera generate blossoms and bodies emit wondrous light, whose names are recorded in the Blue Box, may behold the Cavern Scripture."

*The Inner Biography of the Purple Void Primordial Lady* states: "Perfected Lady Jinglin said to Hua Cun: 'Now I observe your essence—lofty and resplendent, your round spirit doubly radiant, your body that of a phoenix and bones of a dragon. Your brain shines with precious luminosity, your five viscera bear purple networks, and your heart has feathered patterns. Thus your form dwells in the morning clouds, and your spirit communes with the numinous streams.'"

When the Dao harmonizes with supreme peace, and the governance of immortals aids in rule, one’s innate response proves fitting for use—such talent is truly magnificent. The role of such a person is surely not in vain.

*The Scripture of the Hidden and Secret Treasures of the Great Ultimate* states: The Perfected of the Great Ultimate said, "For one who bears the auspicious marks of an immortal, the essential quality lies in a compassionate heart. By encountering all things with kindness to nurture these marks, one may attain immortality. If one cannot restrain the nature and tolerate faults, the immortal marks will be ruined."

*The Inner Biography of the Supreme Perfected* states: Yin Xi’s eyes held the essence of the sun, his form was tall and refined, his arms hung past his knees, and his neck bore a radiant halo. His five viscera bore patterns, his face had the seven stars, above mirroring the celestial patterns and below aligning with earthly principles—nothing was lacking. Thus, he was entrusted with refining his essence, transcending birth in the final kalpa, and destined to become the foremost of noble perfected ones.

*Monthly Ranks of the Heavenly Years*
*The Jade Essence True Scripture of the Three-Nine Plain Speech* states: On the auspicious hour of the first year of the Beginning Era, the Heavenly Venerable of the Nine Heavens and the Jade Lads of the Three Heavens, at the northern pivot of the celestial shift, halted their chariots at the Three Origins, aligned with the splendor of the Nine Emperors, and ascended to the High Jade Palace of the Purple Void Heaven.

*The Three-Nine Plain Speech* states: Unveiling *The Jade Essence True Scripture of the Numinous Pass* governs the myriad immortals.

*The Scripture of the Three Origins’ Jade Tallies and Three Origins’ Array* states: In the first year of the Pure Void Era, the Celestial Venerable of the Origin taught *The Scripture of the Three Origins’ Jade Tallies* to the Three Heavenly Jade Lads in the Cloud Chamber of Bright Radiance within the Palace of Grand Empyrean. It further states: In the first year of the Pure Void Era, on the ninth day of the ninth month, the cyclical sign being gengyin and the hour aligning with the celestial stem, the Celestial Venerable of the Origin ascended in fasting to the Upper Clarity Palace. There, he proclaimed the covenant to the boundless—without summit, without color, without shadow, without form, without name, without ancestry, without lineage, without limit, without end—and the naturally limitless Dao of the Nine Mysteries of the Cavern Clarity. He bestowed the *Three Origins’ Jade Tallies* upon the Three Heavenly Jade Lads, commanding them to transmit it to later disciples whose mysterious names would mark them as Perfected of Upper Clarity.

*The Lower Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: In the first year of the Green Dragon Era, when the year-star resided in xinhai, on the first night of the ninth month, this *Great Cavern Scripture of Thirty-Nine Chapters* was received by the Lady of the Purple Tenuity.

*The Scripture of the Nine Empyreans of the Heavenly Return, Recorded by the Seven Saints of the Jade Emperor* states: In the first year of the Central August Era, on the seventh day of the ninth month, the Seven Saints united in numinosity to present *The White Tallies and Azure Registers of the Nine Empyreans of the Heavenly Return*, elucidating its profound principles.

*The Scripture of the Eight Effulgences’ Flight and Ascent* states: The Heavenly Venerable of the Nine Heavens, in the first year of the Establishing Beginning Era, on the auspicious hour of the celestial stem in the eastern pivot, observed a pure fast. At the Seven-Treasure Jade Terrace of the Grand Void, he swore a golden and azure covenant with heaven to receive the numinous scripture, summon spirits, subdue demons, and reveal the mysterious chapters of the Seven Origins.

*The Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection* states: In the third year of the Primal August Era, within the Flying Dawn of the Grand Void’s Upper Empyrean, the Yellow Elder of the Central Yellow, though but seven years old, grasped the essentials of longevity.

*The Inner Instructions of the Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* states: The Yellow Elder of the Center was born in the sixth year of the Upper August of Pure Numinosity.

*The Scripture of the Seven Stars’ Celestial Shift* states: For those who seek the five supreme wishes of the Lord Emperor’s immortal path, the Lord Emperor regularly observes these five wish-fulfilling assemblies: the ninth day of the ninth month, the fifth day of the tenth month, the third day of the third month, the eighth day of the fourth month, and the seventh day of the seventh month. Ascend to the Jade Palace within the Highest Jade Hall of the Great Ultimate’s Jeweled Palace, and meditate upon the five wishes in the secluded chamber. Yearn for the mysterious and true to descend from the void, and with jade chapters and golden tones, proclaim them across the Grand Void. Summon the Five Emperors to guard the numinous, and ferry the myriad assemblies into the cinnabar chamber. Thus, through sincere aspiration, the perfected are drawn near, and their response descends.

On these days, one should bathe, purify, and fast, enter the chamber, burn incense, bow in reverence to the four directions, face due east, and sit upright. East is the direction of the dawning radiance. Strike the teeth thirty-six times and recite the wishes as follows:

**First Wish:** May I be born of the primordial qi, my body formed within it, equal to the Three Luminaries, and may I eternally enjoy the root of the boundless.

**Second Wish:** May my body ever dwell within the Jeweled Palace and Jade Chamber above the Grand Void, feasting with the Jade Emperor by day and sharing the table of the Mysterious Mother by night. When thirsty, may I sip from the vast well of jade mushrooms and the red tree’s crimson child; when hungry, may I partake of the dragon embryo’s jade fat.

**Third Wish:** May my body generate seventy-two radiant auspices, with extraordinary hair and bones, and may I don feathered robes to ride the void and mount the sky, entering and leaving the imperial palace. May myriad blessings converge, and may my life be boundless.

**Fourth Wish:** May I be born with the unborn and die with the undying, reborn after death to become an emperor-king, ruling the Ten Heavens and governing the host of immortals.

**Fifth Wish:** May all sentient beings—those already born and those yet to be—along with those who preserve the Dao of the Three Luminaries, the ancestors of the Seven Mysteries, ascend to the Southern Palace. May the world’s blessings be without exception, and may the four directions’ five wishes assemble in the Jade Hall.

**Next Wish:** May the Nine Mysteries nurture my body, and may my hun-soul, po-soul, and true spirit eternally dwell within my palace, ascending to commune with heavenly immortals and descending to reach the cavern abyss. May the wishes for heaven, earth, wind, clouds, and spirits unite as one, and may my name be inscribed for eternal life. May purple mists descend from heaven, and may the Five Numinous Ones guard the earth. Riding clouds and mounting the void, may I ascend in a green chariot to the Golden Gate, advancing to the Jade Clarity. May blessings extend to my seven ancestors, who shall be reborn in the womb, and may the five supreme wishes unite for eternal prosperity and purity.

**Middle Wishes (also five):**
May I attain the root of the Dao,
May I harmonize yin and yang,
May I abide in the Grand Void,
May I merge with the Great Nonbeing,
May I unite with the Great Mystery.
Feasting in the Jade Chamber with the Emperor,
May I share karmic ties,
Wandering and gazing upon the Gate of Life,
Unfurling the waves of the Nine Heavens.
May the Primordial Father inscribe my name,
May the Mysterious Mother record my years,
May peaches and elixirs congeal my essence,
And may my cinnabar field be secure.
May my body ascend to the Golden Gate,
My name inscribed in the Jade Chapters,
My seven ancestors liberated,
And blessings and fortune converge.

**Lower Wishes (also five):**
May I attain the Grand Void,
May I attain the Great Existence,
May I attain the Great Above,
May I attain the Great Perfected,
May I attain the divine immortals.

May I traverse the peaks of the Five Marchmounts,
Drifting between the Nine Heavens,
Moving in and out of the Gates of Opening,
Shifting beyond the Portals of Death.
May Heaven and Earth be my father and mother,
May the Three Luminaries guard my myriad spirits,
May I keep the nine springs’ numinous apertures,
And receive the qi of spontaneity.

The eight directions and five wishes resound in harmony.

The *Dragon-Soaring Hidden Instructions on the Foot-Long Silk* states: In the first year of the Shangjing era, on the third day of the third month, at the dawn of the Yuan Shi, the Grand Realized One suddenly received the *Flying Feather Scripture*, which blazed forth in the Jade Void’s courtyard, and also produced the *Scripture of White Feathers and Black Pinions*.

The *Seventy-Four Methods of Shangqing Transformation* states: The Lord of Longevity and Controller of Destiny of the Southern Culmen, whose register is held in the Supreme Purity’s Mysterious Record, bears the surname Wang, personal name Gaisheng, and style Yidu. In the first year of the Taixu era, during the reign of Luo Xi Fan Meng Shang, in the time of Zhu Ming Xie Qian, he was born in the domain of Donglin Guangchang, in the village of Changle.

The *Scripture of the Seven Turns and Seven Transformations of the Divine Continent* states: In the first year of the Yuanjing era, the *Precious Scripture of Supreme Purity* was compiled in one fascicle and sealed in the mountains of the Western Regions.

The *Upper Scripture of the Jade Girdle and Golden Pendants* states: On the first day of the first month of the first year of the Shangxu era, during the Heavenly Yuan’s Convergence of Auspices, on the jiazi day coinciding with the celestial stem, the Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning and the Grand Thearch were moved by the arrival of a blue-black crow, which bore in its beak a purple scripture and presented it to these two lords.

By the first year of the Zhonghuang era, on the first day of the third month, the gengyin day when the Celestial Virtue coincided, within the Frost-Spirit Cinnabar Hall and the Jasper Terrace’s Yellow Chamber, Yuan Shi commanded the Five Immortals to unbind the cloud-brocade wrappings of frost-laden silk and the dense bamboo slips, producing the *Hidden Writ of the Jade Girdle, Golden Pendants, and Grand Empyrean*, which was transmitted to the Highest Jade Dawn and Grand Dao Lord of the Supreme Clarity.

It further states: In the first year of the Shangkai era, on the first day of the ninth month, a blue-black crow bore the Golden Scripture of the Nine Heavens’ secret characters and presented it to the Queen Mother of the West.

The *Hidden Writ of the Primordial Yuan* states: In the first year of the Zhonghuang era, on the first day of the third month, the jiazi day when the Celestial Virtue coincided, the High Minister, the Azure Lad, purified himself in fasting upon the empty mountain.

The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: Hong Natai was born in the first year of the Zhuling era, in the bingwu year, in the Dan Tonglong Luo Wei Heavenly Cavern of the Luminous Jade Land of Zhu Huo’s slopes.

The *Upper Scripture of the Golden Chamber’s Life-Prolonging Methods* states: The Supreme Realized Prohibited Lord of the Southern Culmen, Controller of the Registers, in the first year of the Shihuang era, in the renwu year, on the seventh day of the seventh month at noon, in the Seven-Treasure Cavern of the Boundless Longevity Heavenly King’s domain, beneath the Purple Terrace and Jasper Grove of the Phoenix Capital, inquired of the Heavenly Venerable regarding the methods of life-prolonging and age-reversing. By the first year of the Zhonghuang era, these were transmitted to the Supreme Yuan Lord of the Southern Culmen, the Venerable Master of Myriad Beginnings, and the Golden Gate Thearch.

The *Preface to the Sectional Exegesis of the Laozi* states: In the first year of the Wuji Lingdao era, on the jiazi day of the seventh month, Laozi transmitted the *Five Thousand Character Text’s Sectional Exegesis and Diagrams* to the Pass Keeper Yin Xi, who received them for the sake of longevity.

The *Inner Transmission of the Wenshi* states: In the first year of the Shanghuang era, in the dingmao year, on the twelfth day of the first month, the bingwu day, Laozi descended to become the Zhou’s teacher. It further states: In the first year of the Wuji era, in the guichou year, on the twenty-eighth day of the twelfth month at noon, Laozi transmitted the *Scripture of Dao and Virtue* in its two fascicles. It also states: In the first year of the Zhou Wuji era, in the guichou year, on the twenty-fifth day of the twelfth month, Laozi crossed the pass.

Now, according to the *Essential Record of the Two Teachings*: The first year of the Shanghuang era was the reign title of the Human Sovereign Lord, predating the Zhou by seventeen reigns, an extremely remote era. It may be that the Zhou dynasty emulated this in its own reign titles, or perhaps it mirrored the celestial era names. This resembles how the Earthly Sovereign Lord named the first year of the Chiwu era, and Sun Quan of Wu also named the first year of the Chiwu era. Similarly, the Yuanhuang Lord named the first year of the Kaihuang era, and the Sui dynasty also emulated the name Kaihuang for its first year.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Writ* states: By the first year of the Shanghuang era, the male and female forms of the various heavens had become purely unadorned, but their minds gradually deteriorated, fearing decline and decay. As the orthodox teachings were incomplete, I manifested in every land to perfect their minds. According to this, these are the era names of the various heavens, not those of the Human Sovereign Lord. It appears that the Human Sovereign Lord emulated these in establishing his own era names.

According to the *Scripture of the Nine Heavens’ Divine Engendering*, Shanghuang is an eon name, preceding the Kaihuang eon and following the Chiming eon.

The *Seventy-Four Methods of Shangqing Transformation* states: The Lord of Longevity of the Southern Culmen was born in the domain of Donglin Guangchang, in the village of Changle. It further states: He established the Spirit Palace in the Dark Bureau, securing the register in the Primordial Chart. In the northern wilds of Yangli, in the golden-clouded state of Yinhui, he intermingled the two qi to refine and transform, harmonizing yin and yang to support one another. Thus, Yuan Shi inscribed his command upon the Southern Culmen, and the Three Perfected wrote their writs in Donghua. The curling incense smoke drifted, and he wandered to gaze upon the purple cliffs of the Empyrean. He extinguished the knots of death in the Primordial Womb and repaired the Supreme Perfected in the Dark Capital.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Highest Jade Void coalesced into the Golden Phase Palace of Jade Clarity, the Jasper Heavenly Prefecture of the Eightfold Luminous Village in the Dingzhen Ward, named the Primordial August Supreme Elder.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Highest Clarity Primordial Void coalesced into the Golden Slip Palace of Jade Clarity, the Grand Clarity Prefecture of the Open Luminous Village in the Tongzhen Ward, named the High Numinous Nine Heavens King.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Highest Mystery Primordial Purple Void coalesced into the Cinnabar Numinous Palace of Jade Clarity, the Open Clarity Prefecture of the Threefold Union Village in the Yuanming Ward, named the Jade Perfected Nine Heavens Elder.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Highest Void Primordial Cavernous Void coalesced into the Jade Performance Palace of Jade Clarity, the Golden Fusion Prefecture of the Upper Opening Village in the Zhengyuan Ward, named the August Elder of the Three Heavens.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Ascendant Yuan Perfected and Highest Luminous Primordial Void coalesced into the Jasper Upper Palace of Jade Clarity, the Cinnabar Luminous Prefecture of the Threefold Simplicity Village in the Yuanzheng Ward.

The Ward is named the Jade Youth of the Upper Three Heavens. The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Highest August Yuan Sixfold Void coalesced into the Jade Inaugural Golden Palace of Jade Clarity, the Heavy Guest Prefecture of the Upper Union Village in the Sixfold Assembly Ward, named the Jade Treasure Elder of the Nine Empyreans.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Mysterious Upper Yuan Jade August coalesced into the Jade Sevenfold Radiance Palace of Jade Clarity, the Phoenix-Born Prefecture of the Upper Void Village in the Transcendent Transformation Ward, named the Purple Radiance Perfected King of the Nine Empyreans.

It further states: The qi of the Supreme Yuan Perfected and Mysterious Void Yuan Upper August coalesced into the Jade Primordial Treasure Palace of Jade Clarity, the Golden Upper Prefecture of the Separation-Union Village in the Luminous Light Ward, named the Highest Void August Lord.

The above are the names of villages and wards from the *Scripture of the Seventy-Four Transformations of the Upper Clarity*, of which there are many more; they are not recorded here in full.

The *Scripture of the Seven Revolutions and Seven Transformations of the Divine Continent* states: The Purple Dawn journeyed south to the Vermilion Mound, the Great Cinnabar’s Ultimate Scorching Flowing Fire Ward, where the Southern Culmen Supreme Yuan Lord requested the jade tablets of the Great Cinnabar.

It further states: It journeyed north to the Feathered Yin’s Ninefold Mystery Cold Ward, where the Supreme Yin Jade Dawn Ninefold Yuan Perfected Consort came to receive the treasured chapters of flowing essence and flying radiance.

The *Lower Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* states: The Northern Mystery Highest Void August Lord resides in the Jade Clarity Purple Jade Palace’s Cinnabar Jade Prefecture, Golden Phase Village, Three Augusts Ward, where the revolving perfection descends and reflects into the jade gates of the adept’s two kidneys.

It further states: The Western Florescence Void August Lord resides in the Jade Clarity Sound Primordial Palace’s Eightfold Terrace Prefecture, Fourfold Luminosity Village, Subtle Culmen Ward, where the revolving perfection descends and reflects into the posterior gate of the adept’s lungs.

It further states: The Eastern Luminosity Void August Lord resides in the Jade Clarity Purple Tenuity Palace’s Vermilion Bird Prefecture, Southern Yang Village, Cavernous Life Ward, where the revolving perfection descends and reflects into the ninefold gates of the adept’s liver.

It further states: The Central Abode Void August Lord resides in the Jade Clarity Golden Numinosity Palace’s Phoenix-Call Prefecture, Dark Spirit Village, Union Clarity Ward, where the revolving perfection descends and reflects into the adept’s spleen palace.

The above are the names of various villages from the *Lower Yuan Register Scripture*, of which there are many more; they are not recorded here in full.

The *Precepts of the Host of Perfected, Third Scroll* states: In the Scorching Valley lies the Land of the Upright Tree, sixty thousand li east of the mountains of Kuaiji.

The *Scripture of the Eightfold Might for Summoning Dragons* states: Above it reaches the foundation of the Jade Capital; below it extends to the Abyssal Cavern Ward.

The *Commentary on the Thirty-Nine Chapters of the Great Cavern Jade Scripture* states: The Eastern Florescence is the province of the immortals and perfected. It lies between the First Radiance, where the Jade Guardian of the High Dawn governs. The First Radiance is the land of the sun’s rising.

It further states: The Dark Continent has the ford of Weak Waters, which none but immortals may cross.

The *Transmissions of Daoist Learning, Twentieth Scroll* states: Lady Zhang Yuan, styled Pure Brightness, resided in Cai Slope Village of Qu’e, and at the age of eleven already maintained a perpetual fast.

The *Scripture of the Orthodox Dao of the Three Heavens* states: There was the August Lord of Former Ages, who now appears as Laozi. The one who descended in the first year of the August Lord to serve as the Zhou preceptor was surely the August Lord of the Later Heavens.

This resembles what is said in the *Upper Scroll of the Comprehensive Gate Treatise*: There are the Former Three Yuans, the Middle Three Yuans, and the Later Three Yuans, which serve as analogies for one another.

It resembles what is cited in the *Seventh Scroll of the Mysterious Gate Treatise* from the *Sixth Scroll of the Cavernous Spirit Scripture*: There are the Former Three August Lords, the Next Three August Lords, and the Later Three August Lords, which are analogous.

It resembles how the Liang dynasty’s Xiang Daoist school referred to the Great Clarity Realm, also calling it the first year of the Great Clarity.

The *Chapter on the Differentiation of Lands, First Scroll* and the *Chapter on Responding to the Dao and Descending into Birth* also contain passages on differentiation.

The *Eighth Scroll of the Cavernous Spirit Scripture* states: The Yeni Heaven extends eighty-one myriad li downward, its terrain shaped like a waning moon.

The *Lower Scroll of the Jade Characters of Inner Sound Scripture* states: The Heavenly Venerable, together with the Five Elder Thearchs and the great sages of the ten directions, expounded in the Cypress Mound Abode of the Vermilion Bright World the great Brahmanic esoteric language and the boundless cavernous chapters of the celestial script in eightfold assembly. The Heavenly Venerable issued a command, and the hosts of heaven reverently obeyed. Thereupon, the four assemblies rose as one, made obeisance, and the Heavenly Venerable raised a hand to point upward, then lowered it to point downward—without above or below, without limit or end, without depth or distance, without obscurity or concealment, without great or small, without number or termination. All were universally delivered, equally illumined, and with a flick of the finger, the assembly heard all. At that moment, the four assemblies simultaneously raised their hands, flicked their fingers toward the heavens, and the thirty-two heavens’ sun, moon, and stars all shone at once. The ninefold dark abyss to the bottomless depths was pervaded with light, no darkness remaining. The hidden was universally revealed, the Earth Treasury laid bare, mountains, rivers, streams, and ravines all leveled as one. Winter blossoms bore fruit, withered trees sprouted anew. All rejoiced, and beings received the merit. Fish and dragons leapt, birds and beasts sang joyfully. Divine songs resounded in harmony, no sorrowful cries were heard on the roads. Heaven stilled, earth silenced, the Three Offices lay hidden in tranquility. The registers were closed, the Five Paths ceased to arise, humans and spirits rejoiced in peace, and the sagely Dao flourished in great harmony.

The *Fifth Scroll of the Scripture of the Ten Latitudes of the Five Thousand Words* states: The Perfected One Talara transformed and journeyed to the land of Zhendan in the Middle Kingdom. The land of Zhendan is called Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa were wicked, foolish, and stubborn, and many beings did not believe in the true scriptures. He further divided his form to transform thirty-six kingdoms and also transformed the king of the Naiquan Kingdom. The king detained him and entrusted him with governance, and the king followed in every detail the laws of the Three Caverns from the Five Thousand Words.

The *Eighth Scroll of the Scripture of Ascending Mystery* states: I circulate the five qi through the eight extremities, sometimes called the Most High, sometimes called the Venerable Lord, sometimes called the Mysterious Ancestor, sometimes called the World’s Teacher.

The *Third Scroll of the Scripture of Ascending Mystery* states: Among them are those who appear as national preceptors, those who appear as the patriarchs of the Confucian groves, and those who appear as upholders of ritual and law. In a single day, I traverse the ten directions—one cannot use the form and substance of the foolish and vulgar to limit the sagely ones.

The *Scripture of the Purple Azure Golden Root* states: In life, his surname was Yao and his given name Boyuan. He nurtured his heart in the realm of bright rosy clouds, roamed the ruins of the Jade Kingdom, wielded the tally of the Primordial August, and cast his shadow upon the mounds of the nine domains.

It further states: The Primordial August Jade Emperor ascends to the capital of the Nine Elder Immortals’ Metropolis, the chambers of the Nine Bends, roaming without bound and feasting in the Nine Heavens.

It further states: The Ninth Completion Duke, the Nine Heavens Venerable, rides a flying phoenix and a dark dragon, wandering above the Whitewater Sands and the empty mountains.

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* states: The boundless heavens of the Dark Mound Jade Kingdom, the misty shores of the Ninefold Citadel—this is the birthplace of the Azure Essence Emperor Lord.

*Volume Eight of the Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns* concludes.
*Volume Nine of the Pearl Satchel of the Three Caverns*
Compiled by Wang Xuanhe, the Feathered Guest of the Tang’s Vast Sea
*On Kalpas and Cycles*

The *Scripture of the Orthodox Methods of the Three Heavens of Highest Clarity* states: The heavens are round, governed by twelve celestial nets; the earth is square, ordered by twelve terrestrial records. The celestial net revolves through its pivots, three hundred sixty wheels completing one cycle. The terrestrial record’s mechanism turns, three hundred thirty wheels making one degree. Three thousand six hundred celestial cycles constitute a yang surge; three thousand three hundred terrestrial degrees form a yin eclipse. Heaven’s qi culminates in the Supreme Yin; earth’s qi is exhausted in the Supreme Yang. Thus, when yang is stimulated, it surges; when yin is obstructed, it eclipses. When yin and yang surge and eclipse, the qi of heaven and earth reverse. The reversal of heaven and earth’s qi is called a minor kalpa. When minor kalpas intersect, the ten thousand emperors exchange thrones, the nine qi alter their courses, the sun and moon contract their motions, land surges from the Nine Springs, the Water Mother bursts through the Five Rivers, the Great Crow gathers at Dragon Gate, and the Five Emperors convene in the Dark Metropolis. At this time, the wicked and defiled perish, while the virtuous people endure.

Nine thousand nine hundred celestial cycles constitute a yang eclipse; nine thousand three hundred terrestrial degrees form a yin surge. When yang eclipses, qi is exhausted in the Supreme Yin; when earth surges, qi is schemed in the Supreme Yang. Thus, when yang is obstructed, it eclipses; when yin is stimulated, it surges. When yang and yin eclipse and surge, heaven and earth transform. The transformation of heaven and earth is called a great kalpa. When great kalpas intersect, heaven overturns and earth collapses, seas surge and rivers burst, people drown and mountains sink, gold and jade dissolve, the Six Directions merge into darkness, white corpses drift boundlessly, solitary spirits lament in the vast waves, the Great Crow sweeps filth from the sacred peaks, the Water Mother assumes office at the Nine Rivers, the Five Dragons exhale qi in the Northern Origin, the Heavenly Horses harness their reins to subdue demons, the Red Locks subdue spirits at the Gate of Chen, the Year Star extinguishes kings in the Golden Net, the sun and moon darken in the Three Eminences’ halls, the five qi halt their halos above the Nine Ridges, the Dragon King drums blossoms above the Eastern Well, the River Lord receives judgment beneath the Nine Seas, the Sage Lord manifests his chariot in the bright rosy clouds, and the Five Emperors examine the good and evil. At this time, the myriad evils are eradicated, ghosts and demons vanish without trace, and of the Eight Wastes and Four Extremities, not one in ten thousand remains. As for the convergence of heaven and earth, none but the Highest Three Heavens can avert it, and none without the Azure Registers and White Tallies can escape it.

It further states: The Celestial Pivot lies at the northwest corner of heaven, aligned with the Dipper. The Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper are the handle of the Celestial Pivot’s net, the canopy of the King of Dawn, the qi of the twelve celestial hours of the Nine Heavens’ Brahman conduct. When the Dipper’s net revolves, the Nine Heavens turn in unison. Heaven has four seasonal gates, and the Nine Heavens encompass thirty-six seasons. In one day and night, the Dipper’s net revolves through one seasonal gate. Over thirty-six days and nights, it traverses all thirty-six seasons. When the thirty-six seasons conclude, the Nine Heavens complete one wheel; three hundred sixty wheels make one cycle of the Nine Heavens. When the Nine Heavens complete one cycle, the qi of the Six Heavens all return to the Highest Three Heavens. Heaven alters its revolutions to hasten their degrees, and three thousand six hundred cycles constitute a minor kalpa. When minor kalpas intersect, the nine qi are rectified, the ten thousand emperors exchange thrones, people perish and ghosts vanish, the good and pure are governed, and the Six Directions are pacified and unified.

Nine thousand nine hundred cycles mark the end of a great kalpa. When a great kalpa ends, the numbers of the Nine Heavens are exhausted, and the revolutions of the Six Heavens are spent. When the Six Heavens’ revolutions are spent, qi is stimulated in the Three and Five, and malevolent spirits rampage, seizing the moment to act, spreading poison and annihilating people. All this arises from the exhaustion of revolutions and the extremity of numbers, riding the opportunity to stir, thus reaching this state.

The earth’s mechanism lies in the southeast quadrant, beneath the Nine Springs, where the mouths of the Nine Rivers inhale and exhale. The numinous mechanism connects upward to the celestial source’s molding flow, and laterally swallows the abyssal inlets of the Nine Caverns. The twelve terrestrial records push the waters of the Four Convergences; in one day and night, qi swells as they converge at the mechanism of the Nine Rivers. Over thirty-three days and nights, the mechanism turns northwest, unfolds northeast, and contracts southwest. When it unfolds, it overflows; when it contracts, it wanes, cycling through the Four Convergences. The celestial source’s downflow surges in waves—this is called one turn. Three hundred thirty turns make one degree. One degree compels the Water Mother to hasten her meeting with the Dragon King, and the River Lord to receive judgment from the Three Heavens. Three thousand three hundred degrees are called a yin obstruction. When yin is obstructed, it eclipses. When yin eclipses, waters surge, rivers burst, mountains sink, and earth vanishes. Nine thousand three hundred degrees mark the end of a great kalpa, the extremity of yin’s revolutions. At this time, the Nine Springs surge in vast waves, the Water Mother drums at Dragon Gate, mountains and seas merge into darkness, and the Six Directions lie flat. This is the triumph of yin’s revolutions, the stimulation of earth’s qi.

It further states: On the seventh day of the seventh month of the first year of the Red Essence Kaihuang era, at the bingwu hour of midday, [the Perfected One] ascended to the Moon’s Upper Palace in the Jasper Metropolis, received talismans from the Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning, opened the Golden Yang Jade Casket and the Dark Harmony Jade Maiden’s oral command, and issued the register of the August People. From the three luminaries’ radiance before the Kaihuang era to the Kaihuang era itself, countless kalpas have passed, and the successes and failures of heaven and earth cannot be recounted. The Nine Heavens Venerable, in the Kaihuang reckoning, calculated the celestial origins, examined and predicted the kalpas’ revolutions, recorded the names of those who attained the Dao in the Azure Registers and White Tallies, and inscribed the register of the August People. The numbers culminated in Tang Yao—this was a minor kalpa. At its intersection, gains and losses amounted to two hundred forty thousand people. Those destined to attain it, from the time after Tang onward, numbered forty-six. Between the dinghai year and the preceding and following years, in the jiashen year, the minor kalpa’s convergence occurs, and people’s names are determined.

At this juncture, the Yang’s ninefold calamities and the hundred-sixth cycle of qi converge, the two qi part and unite, and fortune and misfortune intersect—those who pass through shall be spared! Yet after the jiashen year and before the jiashen year, at the inception of the renchen year, nine cycles have revolved, and by the gengzi year, the omens of fortune and misfortune manifest, the Dao’s course becomes clear and bright. A crimson star shall appear in the east, a white comet shall trespass the moon’s gate, monstrous offspring shall emerge from the mouths of insects, and rebellious hordes shall fill the rivers of Yue with corpses. People shall devour their own kind, smoke shall vanish for ten thousand li, mighty ministers shall claim dominion, and feeble lords shall be shrouded in dust. Thereafter, the five numinous spirits shall blaze with auspicious signs, their virtue uniting with the root, and from the lineage of the Dragon Essence shall arise a sovereign who restores the clan. He shall pacify the four barbarians, and those who answer the celestial tally shall prosper.

In the era of the Dragon and Tiger, the three-sixth cycle shall summon forth; the people shall suffer no untimely deaths, and the throne shall know no peril. After Tang, the forty-sixth dinghai year marks the completion of three minor kalpas. Furthermore, from the fifty-fifth dinghai year to the renchen and guisi years, this is the great kalpa’s cycle. When the great kalpa’s cycle arrives, heaven and earth shall overturn, gold and jade shall dissolve, people shall sink into mountains and vanish, and the six directions shall merge into darkness. The revolution of heaven and earth’s destiny—how can one resist its course? Only those inscribed in the Azure Registers and White Tallies of the Three Lofty Heavens may spread their vast wings and soar, ascending the clouds with unblinking gaze!

This is the decree of the Jade Maiden of Mystic Harmony, the discourse of the Golden Yang and Jade Casket on the successes and failures of heaven and earth, the right and wrong of fortune and misfortune.

The *Scripture of Soaring through the Eight Luminaries* states: When the great kalpa’s cycle arrives, the three paths wax and wane, the two qi unite and part, and the ordering of things reaches its term. In the era following Tang, the Yang’s ninefold calamities shall dispel disasters and eliminate misfortune beforehand, vigorously seeking the perfected transcendents above.

The *Precepts of Lord Lao* states: Westward in the Flowing Sands lies the Boundless Land, where a colossal stone stands three hundred zhang high, its circumference spanning fifteen hundred li. To the north of this stone lies Mustard Seed City, its walls forty li square, with stone altars on all four sides, each twenty zhang high. Once a year, flying immortals place a single mustard seed within this city, and with a sweep of their robes, they brush the colossal stone until it wears away, indistinguishable from level ground. When Mustard Seed City is filled with mustard seeds, the cosmic cycle completes, and the world ascends one stage.

The *Essential Rites of the Numinous Treasure Retreats and Precepts* states: A stone like Mount Kun, with mustard seeds filling a forty-li expanse, and celestial beings in gauze robes—once every hundred years, they brush this stone until it is worn away, removing a single mustard seed. Such is the duration of a kalpa’s end; who among mortals could comprehend its vastness?

The *Scripture of the Numinous Treasure’s Natural Revolutions of Heaven and Earth* states: The Numinous Treasure’s natural revolutions encompass the great Yang’s nine and the great Bo’s six, as well as the minor Yang’s nine and the minor Bo’s six. Three thousand three hundred years constitute the minor Yang’s nine and minor Bo’s six, while nine thousand nine hundred years constitute the great Yang’s nine and great Bo’s six. The heaven’s tribulation is called the Yang’s nine, and the earth’s depletion is called the hundred-six. After the Jin clan’s era, in the jiashen year, the revolutions of heaven and earth’s fortune and misfortune shall conclude at the convergence of the Yang’s nine. At that time, the Dao and virtue shall become manifest, and malevolent forces shall run rampant. The sagely ruler shall assume his mandate in the renchen year. It further states that in the Water Dragon era, the immortal lord shall draw the bow and the eighteen sons shall emerge—this scripture contains ten clauses, which are not recorded here in full.

*Laozi as the Imperial Preceptor’s Rank*
*Scroll Eight of the* Tai Ping Section: *The Transmission of Laozi’s Scripture, Precepts, Rituals, and Essential Instructions* states: Laozi is the great sage who attained the Dao, the teacher of both the hidden and the manifest. When responding to conditions, he transforms and adapts to all directions; when his work is complete, he conceals himself and abides in constancy. Abiding without abiding, he is ever-present without absence; the absence within presence resides in the boundless; the boundless’ bound resides in the Supreme Mystery. The Supreme Mystery is the capital of the Supreme Ancestor’s ultimate dominion. Laozi dwells here, his transformations responding to the ten directions, unfolding the wonders of being and non-being, and endlessly engaging with all things—beyond description.

In recent times, he emerged into the world and was born at the beginning of the Zhou dynasty. Descending in humble guise, he was born among the common folk, demonstrating that even those of lowly birth may cultivate the Dao and attain it without hindrance. He traversed the six voids and taught across the three realms. The Dharma beyond the world and the Dharma within the world, the active and the quiescent—none did he fail to fully explore.

During the reign of King Wen of Zhou, he served as the Keeper of the Archives. Some say he lived in the world for over two hundred years, and in the forty-third year of King Ping’s reign, in the year *guichou* of the sexagenary cycle, on the twenty-eighth day of the twelfth month, he expounded the *Five Thousand Character Text* to the Pass Prefect Yin Xi.

The *Scripture on the Conversion of the Barbarians* states: After Fuxi, Laozi was born and became the teacher of emperors, styled Master of Profound Clarity, also called Master of the Fields and Wilds, and composed the *Scripture of Primordial Yang*. During the time of Shennong, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Great Accomplishment, also named Master Guo Cheng, and composed the *Scripture of the Primordial Essence of the Great One*. During the time of Zhu Rong, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Transmitted Foreknowledge, also named Master of Broad Longevity, and composed the *Scripture on Massage and the Circulation of Essence*. These three lineages cultivated together, each governing through non-action, and after eighteen thousand years, brought about Great Peace. The people were pure and simple, and no further governance was needed. Only the natural *qi* of non-being served as the law, without coercion or conquest. The *qi* of the Dao returned to them, and none failed to submit. These were the sovereigns of the Three August Ones.

During the time of the Yellow Emperor, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Broad Accomplishment, and composed the *Scripture of Dao Attainment*. During the time of Emperor Ku, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of the Green Chart, and composed the *Scripture of the Yellow Court of the Dao and Its Principles*. During the time of Emperor Yao, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Accomplished Service, and composed the *Scripture of Proper Affairs*. During the time of Emperor Shun, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master Yin Shou, and composed the *Scripture of the Dao and Its Virtue*. The Yellow Emperor was supremely sagely, enabling the imperial enterprise to be passed down in succession. Lifespans varied in length, corresponding to the Five Phases, alternating in mutual conquest and dominance, with the strong and weak oppressing one another. These were the Five Emperors.

During the time of the Xia kings, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master Li Zixu, and composed the *Scripture of Primordial Yang*, as well as the *Scripture of Virtue and Admonitions*. During the time of King Tang, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Bestowed Principles, and composed the *Scripture of the Origin of the Dao*. During the time of King Wen, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master of Harmonious Settlement, also called Master of Vermilion Essence, and also served as Keeper of the Archives. During the time of King Wu, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Master Guo Shu, also called Master of Continued Accomplishment, and served as the Archivist Beneath the Pillars. During the time of King You, he emerged as the emperor’s teacher, styled Heavenly Elder, also called Laozi, and served as the Archivist Beneath the Pillars. He composed the *Scripture of Longevity* and, together with Yin Xi, composed the *Five Thousand Character Text* in two scrolls. Later, he traveled with Yin Xi to the Western Regions and composed the *Scripture on the Buddha’s Conversion of the Barbarians* in six hundred forty thousand characters. After returning to China with the barbarian king, he composed the *Scripture of Great Peace*. In later ages, he will remain among humankind, desiring that the people of the world cultivate goodness and righteousness, revere and uphold virtuous transformation, assist the Dao and its laws, support the state and sustain destiny, labor for the welfare of the common people, and deliver them from calamitous years, enabling them to encounter the midst of the Great Clarity.

The above, like a cascading river, is now called the *Dao and Its Virtue*. The preface states: "Laozi served as the state teacher in every generation"—this is the meaning of that. Master Meng Zhizhou’s *Comprehensive Titles of the Laozi Scripture* says: "One thousand two hundred Laozi." This refers to those one thousand two hundred, as Laozi himself had other scriptures. It also states: "Later disciples achieved this, as with Boyang." Thus, it is known that the honorific title Boyang originated in the prosperous Zhou era. This title, whether hidden or manifest, is difficult to thoroughly investigate.

The *Jade Emperor’s Mysterious Record of the Seven Sages* states:
*"Subtly the divine artisan,
The numinous virtue, empty and rare.
Illuminating dragon patterns in the azure abyss,
Radiating cloudlike splendor in the nine heavens.
Washing his lofty form in orchid and jade,
Emitting golden essence from the jasper spring.
Arranging the seven records in the celestial register,
Clarifying the inscribed scriptures in hidden scrolls.
Encompassing the sunken and the bold,
Revolving the stagnant wheel.
Gathering the five symbols,
Assembling the perfected of the highest realm.
Truly the Highest’s descending transformation,
To spread teachings to all directions."*

The *Scripture of Great Peace* on Laozi’s conversion of the Western Barbarians states: Laozi traveled west for over eighty years, having been born between the Yin and Zhou dynasties.

Master Guigu’s *Inner Transmission of the Perfected Lord of the Unsurpassed, the Pass Prefect, and the Venerable Master of the Beginning of Literature* states: In the first year of the Zhou’s *Wuji* era, in the year *guichou* of the sexagenary cycle, on the twenty-fifth day of the twelfth month of winter, Laozi crossed the pass. The Pass Prefect Yin Xi instructed the gate officers: "If an old man arrives from the east, riding a blue ox and a simple plank cart, do not allow him to pass." Later, they indeed saw an old man fitting this description seeking to cross the pass. The gate officers refused, reporting Yin Xi’s words to him. The old man said: "My home is east of the pass, but my fields are west of it. I wish to go gather firewood—please allow me to cross." The gate officers again refused entry and reported to the Pass Prefect. The Prefect immediately went out to greet him and paid him the respects due a disciple. The old man initially declined and sought to depart, but the Pass Prefect earnestly faced north and served him. Laozi consented and stayed.

At that time, Laozi had a hired laborer named Xu Jia, who was paid one hundred coins per day. Laozi had previously made an agreement with him: "I will repay your wages in full, but I must first travel to the Western Sea, the Da Qin, and the Anxi kingdoms. Upon my return, I will repay you in gold, fully covering the amount owed." Xu Jia, seeing that Laozi was about to embark on a distant journey, doubted he would return and thus refused to wait for his wages. At that time, a beautiful woman, hearing that Xu Jia was owed a large sum, sweetly said to him: "Why not sue immediately to claim your wages? I will be your wife." Xu Jia, swayed by her words, filed a complaint with the Pass Prefect, suing Laozi for the money. The Pass Prefect presented Xu Jia’s complaint to Laozi. Laozi said: "My salary is meager, and I have no servants. I previously hired this man and told him that upon returning from the Western Sea, Da Qin, and Anxi kingdoms, I would repay him in gold, fully covering the amount owed. How have I broken our agreement to be sued?" Xu Jia had followed Laozi for over two hundred years and was owed seven million coins. Laozi said to Xu Jia: "I once told you that upon returning from the Western Sea, Da Qin, and Anxi kingdoms, I would repay you in gold. Why could you not endure the humiliation and now bring a lawsuit against me? You have followed me for over two hundred years, and your life should have ended long ago. It is only by virtue of my *Tai Xuan* talisman of longevity residing within you that you still live."

Upon finishing his words, Laozi saw the *Tai Xuan* talisman of longevity fly from Xu Jia’s mouth and return before him, its script fresh and luminous. Xu Jia had already crumbled into a pile of white bones. Xi, witnessing Xu Jia’s death for betraying his heart, then wished to see Laozi revive the dead. He said: "I shall repay this debt on his behalf. I have prepared the coins—may you pardon Xu Jia’s past transgressions and grant him new life." Laozi, moved by compassion, replied: "Very well! This was never my anger toward Xu Jia; he betrayed his original resolve, and the Dao departed of its own accord." Laozi then cast the talisman once more onto the withered bones, and Xu Jia revived as before. Xi explained the situation to him, and Xu Jia kowtowed in gratitude and repentance. Laozi instructed: "Return what you owe," and dismissed him.

Laozi descended to serve as the Zhou preceptor in the first year of *Shang Huang*, the *dingmao* year, on the twelfth day of the first month, the *bingshen* day. As the Zhou’s Way was nearing decline and the king neglected virtue, unable to govern the people through the Dao and virtue, this age of excess and chaos could not be restored. Thus, the Preceptor traveled in humble attire, intending to journey far away.
